Mîr Mamed entered, moved his bed close to the girl's bed and put the lamp in the middle of both beds and he too sat on his bed, he took out his tobacco pouch and filled his pipe and lit it, and took his puff and blew smoke over his head and the girl's head, and slowly took out the amber prayer beads and counts them bead by bead and plays with them, he is completely unaware of the wind of fate (unbothered) and does not look in the girl's direction and does not pay attention to her.

296. Keçik di dilê xwe de diqiçqiçe û ji çirê ditirse ku carek din deng jê derkeve û bipeyive.
296. The girl grinds in her heart and fears the lamp lest a sound comes out of it once again and it speaks.

297. Ziq li çirê dinêre.
297. She stares intently at the lamp.

298. Şev zîz bû, deng ji dunyayê bilîya, Mîr Mamed deng li çirê kir û got: "Çira min mûm û fenera min şev dirêj e, qîyamet dûr e, ji çîrokekê ji serpêhatîyekê ji min re bibêje".
298. The night became silent, sound vanished from the world, Mîr Mamed called to the lamp and said: "My lamp, my candle and my lantern, the night is long, the resurrection is far, tell me of a story, of an adventure".

299. Û dûman bi ser serê xwe û serê keçikê xist û guhdarî kir.
299. And he blew smoke over his head and the girl's head and listened.

300. Keçik cardî ma behitî, kela girî ket qirikê ji hêrs û qehra nema dizane wê çawa bike.
300. The girl again remained stunned, a fit of weeping caught in her throat out of anger and wrath, she no longer knows what she will do.

301. Şah Bilbil: Mîrê, min begê min agir bi serê min ketîye qiçeqiça ji nava min tê ma ez ê çi bibêjim, de xem nake guhê xwe bidin min û got:
301. Şah Bilbil: My mîr, my beg, fire has fallen on my head, the crackling sound comes from my inside, so what shall I tell, well no matter, give me your ear, and he said:

302. "Hebû tu nebû rehme li gora mirîyê min û we bû, dibêjin, sê rêwî bi hev re bûn, hevalên rê peyadar in û her yek turikê wî li milê wî ye, qûnaxek hilanîn yek danîn li wan bû şev û ji hal ketine.
302. "There was, there was not, mercy was upon my dead and yours, they say, three travelers were together, road companions on foot and each one's sack is on his shoulder, they passed a stage and set one down, night fell upon them and they fell out of condition.

303. Ketin çîyê li sitarkê digerin lê rûnên û razên xwe rehet bikin.
303. They entered the mountain, looking for a shelter to sit and sleep and rest themselves.

304. Pêrgî şikeftekê bûn derbas bûn hundirê wê qirşik û stûrik kom kirin û agir dadan, xwarina xwe xwarin, ava xwe vexwarin, tesele bûn, germ bûn, tamara xewê da ser çavên wan, rabû yekî got, şev reş e û çîya ye û teba hene çênabe em her sê bi hev re razên, yekî got: Ma çi bikin?
304. They came across a cave, entered inside it, gathered twigs and small branches and lit a fire, ate their food, drank their water, relaxed, got warm, the vein of sleep took over their eyes; one got up and said, the night is black and it is a mountain and there are wild beasts, it won't do for all three of us to sleep together; one said: So what should we do?

305. Got divê em bi dorê şîyarîya xwe bikin û bi dorê razên.
305. He said we must do our waking in turn and sleep in turn.

306. Rabûn pişka xwe avêtin bê kî pêşî nobetê û şîyarîyê bike û yê duduyan kî ye û yê dawî, her duyên dawî li ber êgir razan û ketin xewa şêrîn de.
306. They got up, cast their lots as to who will do the watch and waking first and who is the second and the last, the last two slept by the fire and fell into sweet sleep.

307. Yê şîyar xerat bû, rabû aletê xwe ji tûrikê xwe derxistin û qurmekî dara anî û sebira xwe pê anî birî û xeritand kir wek peykerê keçikê.
307. The awake one was a carpenter, he got up, took his tools out of his sack, brought a log of wood and amused himself with it, cut and turned it, making it like a girl's statue.

308. Noba wî xelas bû deng li yê duduyan kir û got, rabe şîyarîya te ye û ez ê razêm.
308. His watch finished, he called to the second one and said, get up, it is your waking and I will sleep.

309. Û di xew re çû.
309. And he went to sleep.

310. Evê din rabû agir dada, rûnişt, dît ku hevalê wî yê pêşî peykerê keçikê ji dar çêkirîye.
310. This other one got up, lit the fire, sat down, saw that his first friend had made a girl's statue from wood.

311. Ev jî terzî bû, rabû tûrikê xwe vala kir û ta û derzîya xwe bi dar ve kir û cawê xweşik dirût û li bejina keçikê kir, kire bûka bi xeml û xêz.
311. He was a tailor, he got up, emptied his sack and put his thread and needle to the wood and sewed beautiful cloth and put it on the girl's figure, making her a bride with ornaments and adornments.

312. Wî ji nobeta xwe qedand û sebra xwe bi dirûna xwe anî.
312. He too finished his watch and amused himself with his sewing.

313. Rabû deng li yê dawî yê razayî kir û got, rabe rabe bû dora te vêca ez ê razêm.
313. He got up, called to the last sleeping one and said, get up, get up, it is your turn, now I will sleep.

314. Xwe dirêj kir li ber rivîna êgir, çavên xwe girtin û raza.
314. He stretched himself out by the flame of the fire, closed his eyes and slept.

315. Yê sisêya rabû çû derket derve agirê xwe nû dada, şikeft rûhnî bû, çavên wî li wêneya keçikê ket, dilê wî
315. The third got up, went outside, lit his fire anew, the cave became bright, his eyes fell upon the girl's figure, his heart

316. lê xist û pê re firiya û xwe çeng kir peykerê keçikê dît ku dar e û xemilandî ye.
316. beat and flew with her, and he lunged at the girl's statue, seeing that it is wood and adorned.

317. Nas kir ku hevalê wî sebra xwe anîne û her yekî tiştek çêkiriye.
317. He realized that his friends had amused themselves and each had made something.

318. Ew jî dîndar bû, xwedî ol bû, rabû xwe pêk anî û destê xwe bi ber Xwedê vekir û berzûrî Xwedê bû û digot, ya Xwedakê şev û rojê tê min fedîkar neke li pêşîya her du hevalên min û tu rih û jiyanê bi vê keçikê ve bîne.
318. He was a religious man, an owner of faith, he got up, prepared himself, opened his hands toward God and supplicated to God and was saying, O God of night and day, You will not make me ashamed before my two friends, and You bring soul and life to this girl.

319. Çavê xwe girtîye û berzûrî Xwedê dibe heya berê sibê.
319. He has closed his eyes and supplicates to God until just before morning.

320. Xwedê ew fedîkar nekir û jiyan û rawan bera laşê darikî da û kir keçikek sipehî û nazdar.
320. God did not make him ashamed and poured life and soul into the wooden body, making her a beautiful and delicate girl.

321. Her du hevalên wî jî ji xwe rabûn û her yekî got, ev keçik ya min e û ji min re derdikeve.
321. His two friends also woke up and each one said, this girl is mine and she comes to me.

322. Yê xerat dibêje: Ku min peyker çênekiriba nedibû qîz, û keçik ji min re ye.
322. The carpenter says: If I had not made the statue she would not have become a girl, and the girl is for me.

323. Yê terzî dibêje: Ku min cil û xemla wê lê nekiriba nedibû qîz, û keçik ji min re ye.
323. The tailor says: If I had not put her clothes and adornment on her she would not have become a girl, and the girl is for me.

324. Yê oldar dibêje: Ku ne ji min ba û ez berzûrî Xwedê nebûma rih û rawan pê ve nedihat û Xwedê li halê min nerî û ez fedîkar nekirim bi we re, û keçik ji min re dikeve bi heqîya Xwedê".
324. The religious man says: If it were not for me and I had not supplicated to God, soul and spirit would not have come to her, and God looked upon my state and did not shame me with you, and the girl falls to me by God's right".

325. Şah Bilbil: Ey mîrê delal ma tu dibêjî ji kê re dikeve?
325. Şah Bilbil: O dear mîr, so who do you say she falls to?

326. Ê min ez dibêjim ji xerat re dikeve wî peyker çêkir.
326. As for me, I say she falls to the carpenter, he made the statue.

327. Mîr Mamed: Ê min ez dibêjim ji terzî re dikeve, çimkî wî bi cila xemiland.
327. Mîr Mamed: As for me, I say she falls to the tailor, because he adorned her with clothes.

328. Û her duyan ji qazî ve gengeşî kirin yek dibêje ya xerat e û yê din dibêje na na ji terzî re dikeve.
328. And the two of them argued like a judge, one says she is the carpenter's and the other says no, no, she falls to the tailor.

329. Bi vîi hawî ketin qirka hev de, keçik ji hêrs û qehra got: "Mala we bivirite!
329. In this manner they flew at each other's throats, the girl, out of anger and wrath, said: "May your house be destroyed!

330. Ne ji xerat re û ne ji terzî re dikeve, ji mêrikê oldar re dikeve li ser destê wî û duayên wî ji Xwedê re rih pê hat.
330. She falls neither to the carpenter nor to the tailor, she falls to the religious man; by his hand and his prayers to God, soul came to her.

331. Şah Bilbil: Madam wilo ye tu jî ji birakê min re dikeve û yê bin serê te ji min re dikeve.
331. Şah Bilbil: Since it is so, you too fall to my brother, and the one under your pillow falls to me.

332. Bi hustê mar girt û kuşt û ji nû ve şahî li dar xistin û govend gerandin û mehra bûk û zavayî birîn, sê roj û sê şevan li zirne û daholê xistin û dûre Mîr Mamed û jina xwe û birakê xwe Şah Bilbil berê xwe dan malê.
332. He grabbed the snake by the neck and killed it, and anew they held a celebration and danced the govend and bound the marriage of the bride and groom, for three days and three nights they played the zurna and drum, and then Mîr Mamed and his wife and his brother Şah Bilbil turned toward home.

333. ## Sînem û Mela Itman
333. ## Sînem and Mela Itman

334. Di dema piştî fermandarîya Selahedîn de û vegera wî li bajarê Şamê gelek nûner û cîgir li herêm, îmaret, bajar, Şaristan û li hemû keleh û asêgehan man.
334. In the time after Saladin's command and his return to the city of Damascus, many representatives and deputies remained in the regions, emirates, cities, provinces, and in all the castles and strongholds.

335. Piştî çûna Selahedîn ber dilovanîya Xwedê.
335. After Saladin's passing to God's mercy.

336. Her emîrek û her fermandarek ma mîrê bi destê xwe, piştî çûna Al-Melak Al-Salih ber dilovanîya Xwedê Dewleta Eyûbîyan ji hev ket û perçe perç bû û Memalîkan zora wan bir û bi dû de Holako hat û herêm û kela û dizeyên mayîn di destê Eyûbîyan de giş herifandin wek Meyafarqîn û mîrê wê yê bi nav û deng.
336. Every emir and every commander remained a mîr by his own hand; after Al-Malik Al-Salih's passing to God's mercy, the Ayyubid State fell apart and was fragmented to pieces, and the Mamluks overpowered them, and afterwards Hulagu came, and all the remaining regions and castles and fortresses in the hands of the Ayyubids were ruined, like Meyafarqîn and its famous and renowned mîr.

337. Yek ji begên dêya Mîr Mamed fermandarê Misrê bû.
337. One of Mîr Mamed's mother's begs was the commander of Egypt.

338. Bajarê Misrê bajarekî pir mezin û giran e.
338. The city of Egypt is a very large and heavy city.

339. Ava ye li ser sê sed û şêst mihlan û taxan e.
339. It is built over three hundred and sixty districts and neighborhoods.

340. Her mehelakê (tarakê) têde sih û sê minara ye.
340. In each neighborhood (quarter) there are thirty-three minarets.

341. Bajarê Misrê li ser ava mezin, çem û cobara ye. ye
341. The city of Egypt is on great water, rivers and streams.

342. Dibêjin di dema Mîr Mamed de miletê Misrê gelekî pêşketî bû bi bazirganî û çandinîyê, û dar û devîyên li dor rûbarê Nîlê çitar û mihela hebû, xerat, hesinkut, aş û qeraşa lê kar dikirin, û çi mizgefta hebû sofî û mela têde Quran dixwendin û feqe û suxte têde perwerde dikirin û ew fêrî ola misilmantîyê dikirin.
342. They say in the time of Mîr Mamed the nation of Egypt was very advanced in trade and agriculture, and the trees and bushes around the Nile river had camps and neighborhoods, carpenters, blacksmiths, millers and grinders worked there, and whatever mosque there was, sufis and melas read the Quran in it and students and disciples were educated in it and they taught them the religion of Islam.

343. Miletê Misrê bi kêf û şahî ye, çi kesê cot karîbe û çi kesê karmend be û çi kesê mela be û xwende û feqe û suxte be.
343. The nation of Egypt is with joy and celebration, whether one is a farmer and whether one is an official and whether one is a mela and student and pupil and disciple.

344. Dibêjin saleke xêr û bêr bû, miletê Misrê her yek bi karê xwe daketîye.
344. They say it was a year of goodness and blessing, the nation of Egypt each set to their own work.

345. Mela di mizgefta de bang kirin û gotin: "Bbûye dema kar û barê çûna Mala Xwedê, yê bixwaze û di dilê wî de ye çûna hecê bera karê xwe bike û navê xwe li cem başbazirganekî pêşkêşekê binivîse".
345. The melas in the mosques called out and said: "It has become the time for the chores of going to the House of God; whoever wants to and has going on the Hajj in his heart, let him make his preparations and write his name with a chief merchant for presentation".

346. Melakî qene bi hev re bimeşin û karibin xwe ji diz û çeta biparêzin.
346. A mela, so that they walk together and are able to protect themselves from thieves and bandits.

347. Mîr Mamed jî dixwest here Mala Xwedê, zarokên wî tune ne bûn û qêmîşî dotmama xwe (jina xwe) nedikir ku jinekê bîne ser.
347. Mîr Mamed too wanted to go to the House of God; he had no children and could not bear to bring a second wife over his cousin (his wife).

348. Rabû karên xwe kirin û şêwirmendên xwe civandin û kar û barê dewletê sipart wana û kar û îşê malê û miqatebûna jina wî sînem siparte oldarê mezin miftîyê dewletê Mela Itman û karê xwe kir bi başbazirganê Misrê re, ew û çend kesên hawîrdora wî.
348. He got up, made his preparations and gathered his advisors, and entrusted the affairs of the state to them, and entrusted the chores and business of the house and the taking care of his wife Sînem to the great religious man, the state mufti Mela Itman, and made his preparations with the chief merchant of Egypt, he and a few people of his entourage.

349. Bi rê de hecan peyadar bûn û bazirgan li hesp û devan siwar bûn.
349. On the road the pilgrims were on foot and the merchants were mounted on horses and camels.

350. Mîr Mamed qesr û qûnax bin destê Mela Itman kirin û berê xwe da oxirê û pişta xwe da felekê roj bi roj, qûnax bi qûnax dimeşin û datînin mehek dido qedyan û nêzîkayî li Hicazê kirin.
350. Mîr Mamed placed the palace and estate under the hand of Mela Itman and turned toward his journey and turned his back to fate; day by day, stage by stage they march and set down; a month or two finished and they drew near to the Hejaz.

351. Em ê dev ji Mîr Mamed û hecacyan berdin û em ê vegerin Misrê û herin cem Mela Itman û li kar û finasê wî guhdar bikin.
351. We will leave Mîr Mamed and the pilgrims and we will return to Egypt and go to Mela Itman and listen to his deeds and schemes.

352. Mela Itman kesekî çavlider bû, tolaz û bêewle bû, bêwijdan û zikreş bû.
352. Mela Itman was a covetous person, he was a scoundrel and untrustworthy, he was without conscience and malicious.

353. Piştî ku mîr pişta xwe dayê û çû bi oxira Xwedê de, Mela Itman ket gumanan de û karê bêbextî û finasê nebaş li dora kuşka Sînemê digerand, jê pirs dikir, dixwest pê re bipeyive carekê duduyan Sînemê nas kir ku nêta mela xirabe û dilê wî nepaqij e û çavên wî çavên tolaza ne.
353. After the mîr turned his back to him and went on God's journey, Mela Itman fell into suspicions and circled the business of treachery and bad schemes around Sînem's palace, asking for her, wanting to speak with her; once, twice Sînem realized that the mela's intention is bad and his heart is impure and his eyes are the eyes of a rogue.

354. Sînem hêdî hêdî xwe vegirt, xwe jê parast û nema hişt mela nêzîkî wê û kuşka wê bibe.
354. Sînem slowly withdrew herself, protected herself from him and no longer let the mela come close to her and her palace.

355. Mela kir û nekir tu çiq di Sînem nekir, rabû dest bi tep û rîpa kir û fen û fût gerandin.
355. The mela tried and tried but made no dent in Sînem, he got up and started with tricks and traps and set up schemes and plots.

356. De li vir, de li wir pîrek cadû kar
356. Here, there, a sorceress old woman

357. dît, mela ew girt û anî hicra xwe û pere û zêr danê û jê xwest alîkarîyê pê re bike û Sînem têxe davikê de bi çi hawî be û soz jê re da bi zêra.
357. he found, the mela took her and brought her to his chamber and gave her money and gold and asked her to help him and put Sînem in a trap in whatever way possible, and gave her a promise with gold.

358. Pîra pîra cadûvan bêbext û bê wijdan cilê kevnik û peritî li xwe kirin û ji nîvê şevê pê ve çû ber derîyê Mala Sînemê û li wir palda.
358. The old woman, the sorceress old woman, treacherous and without conscience, put on old and tattered clothes and from midnight on went to the door of Sînem's house and lay down there.

359. Carîya Sînemê derket çû û hat wê rojê pê de pîrê ji wir neçû.
359. Sînem's maid came out, went and came, from that day on the old woman did not leave from there.

360. Carîyê hat ji xatûna xwe re got: Pîrek ji doh de li devê derî ye û dixwaze te bibîne, carek dido sisê Sînem dilê wê bi pîrê şewitî û derket devê derî bi pîrê re peyivî û jê re got: “Ha çi bela te ye pîrê, tu li çi digerî, tu çi dixwazî, ka bêje pîrê?".
360. The maid came and said to her lady: An old woman has been at the doorway since yesterday and wants to see you; once, twice, three times Sînem's heart burned for the old woman and she came out to the doorway, spoke with the old woman and said to her: "Ha, what is your trouble, old woman, what are you looking for, what do you want, come speak, old woman?".

361. Kelogirî bû û got: "Ez gorî xatûna xwe bim, ez pîreke bêkes im, ez ji kerwanê hecacîyam mame û ez tu kesî nas nakim li vî bajarî.
361. She started crying and said: "May I be a sacrifice for my lady, I am a lonely old woman, I was left behind from the pilgrims' caravan and I do not know anyone in this city.

362. Hema ji bo Xwedê ez ê li devê derîyê te bim bi dergevanî û qerwaşî hema rojê parîk nan bide min heya hevalên min vegerin ji hecê wê kerwanê wan di vir re bê, ez ê jî bi wan re vegerim welatê xwe cih û warê xwe.
362. Just for God's sake I will stay at your doorway as a doorkeeper and servant, just give me a piece of bread a day until my friends return from the Hajj, their caravan will come through here, and I too will return with them to my country, my place and land.

363. Dilê Sînem pê şewitî û got: "De xem nake pîrê hema li vê kuxika dergevanîyê razê".
363. Sînem's heart burned for her and she said: "Well no matter, old woman, just sleep in this doorkeeper's hut".

364. Rok dido derbas bûn pîrê xwe nêzîkî Sînemê kir û got: "Ez gorî te me hema destûra min bide ez ê bêm hewşê ez ji derve ditirsim bi şev kûçik û teba di vir re diçin û tên”.
364. A day or two passed, the old woman approached Sînem and said: "I am your sacrifice, just give me permission, I will come to the courtyard, I am afraid of outside, at night dogs and wild beasts come and go through here".

365. Sînem: De xem nake pîrê were hewşê.
365. Sînem: Well no matter, old woman, come to the courtyard.

366. Her sibe pîrê radibe xwe girê dide, daw û delingê xwe hildide û wê hewşê gişî avreşandî dike û dimalîne û paqij dike û her û her xwe nêzîkî Sînemê dike.
366. Every morning the old woman gets up, ties herself, pulls up her skirt and trouser legs and sprinkles water over all that courtyard and sweeps and cleans it, and ever and always brings herself closer to Sînem.

367. Heya Sînemê ew derbasî hundirê kuşka xwe kir, û pîrê wek çipçipkê her sibe radibû mal û xanî û ode giş rêş dikirin û hewş avreşandî dikir û taştêya Sînemê çêdikir û datanî ber, û cil û berg û firax dişûştin heya Sînem lê ewle bû û hişt li cem xwe weke carîyekê.
367. Until Sînem let her inside her palace, and the old woman like a sparrow would get up every morning and sweep all the house and building and rooms and sprinkle water on the courtyard and make Sînem's breakfast and put it before her, and wash the clothes and garments and dishes until Sînem trusted her and kept her beside herself like a maid.

368. Pîrê bi dora Sînemê ket, "xatûna min tu jina Mîrê Misrê ye gereke her în tu herî avgerm û serşokê û hindik maye ku mîr bê bi xêr û xweşîyê û Xwedê bêje erê wê bedena te şîn bike kurekî qenc bide te û warê mîr şîn bibe bi destûra Xwedê".
368. The old woman fussed around Sînem, "my lady, you are the wife of the Mîr of Egypt, every Friday you must go to the hot baths and wash, and little time remains for the mîr to come in goodness and health; and if God says yes, He will make your body green (fertile) and give you a good son, and the mîr's estate will flourish with God's permission".

369. Sînem jineke afret e, dilê wê tenik bû û got: Belkî Xwedê xêra me qebûl bike û bedena min şîn bike û dilê mîr rehet bike.
369. Sînem is a pure woman, her heart was tender and she said: Maybe God will accept our good deed and make my body green and rest the mîr's heart.

370. Bi ya pîrê kir ku here avgermê serokê û got: Divê kes bi min nizanibe ha pîrê, mîr ne li mal e û ez bê destûra wî ji mal derdikevim û ev tişt ne durist e jî, lê xem nake belkî Xwedê li halê min û mîr bipirse û bi xêr û xweşî vegere malê.
370. She acted on the old woman's word to go to the main hot baths and said: No one must know of me, old woman, the mîr is not at home and I am leaving the house without his permission, and this thing is not right either, but no matter, maybe God will ask after my condition and the mîr's, and he will return home in goodness and health.

371. de xem nake pîrê.
371. well, no matter, old woman.

372. Pîrê bi mihna kirîna şeh û sabûnê got: Ez ê herim bazarê pêdivîyê te çi hebin ez ê bikirim qene roja înê em herin avgermîyê.
372. The old woman, on the pretext of buying combs and soap, said: I will go to the market, whatever needs you have I will buy them, so that on Friday we may go to the hot baths.

373. Pîrê bi lez û bez derket û berê xwe da mizgefta Mela Itman û bi dizî jê re got roja înê em ê herin avgerma serşoka mezin, serşoka qîz û jinê mîra, paşa, axa, başbazirganîya mezina.
373. The old woman went out quickly and running, and turned to Mela Itman's mosque and secretly said to him, on Friday we will go to the big hot baths, the baths of the girls and wives of the mîrs, pashas, aghas, and great chief merchants.

374. Mela Itman rabû ferman da roja înê tu kes neçe avgerma mala mîran, wê jina mîr û carîya xwe bi tenê herin xwe lê bişon û veşon, û fermanî dergevanê serokê jî kir ku kes derbas nebe ne mêr û ne jin.
374. Mela Itman got up and gave the order that on Friday no one should go to the hot baths of the mîrs' households; the mîr's wife and her maid will go alone to wash and bathe there, and he also ordered the head doorkeeper that no one should enter, neither man nor woman.

375. Roja înê Sînema pepûk hayê wê ji tiştekî tune ye da dû pîra cadûkar û çû kete avgerma serşokê, çawa Sînem kete di odeya avgermê de û cilê xwe ji xwe kirin pîrê bi dizî derket û derî li Sînemê girt û ji derve de kilît kir û çû kilît da destê Mela Itman û zêrê xwe stendin û çû ji bajêr derket bi lez û bez revîya.
375. On Friday, poor Sînem, unaware of anything, followed the sorceress old woman and went and entered the hot baths; as soon as Sînem entered the hot bath room and took off her clothes, the old woman secretly went out, closed the door on Sînem and locked it from the outside, and went and gave the key into Mela Itman's hand, took her gold, and left the city, running away with speed.

376. Mela Itman çi kir bêbexto?
376. What did Mela Itman do, the treacherous one?

377. Hêdî hat derî vekir û kete odeya serşoka Sînemê de, cibe û şaşik danîn û kiras bi ser xwe de anî, rahişt lûfik û sabûnê û pişta Sînem firikand.
377. He came slowly, opened the door and entered Sînem's bath room, put down his cloak and turban and brought a shirt over himself, grabbed the loofah and soap and scrubbed Sînem's back.

378. Ji pepûka Sînem werê ku pîrê ye ew jî cilê xwe dike û pişta wê difirikîne heya hêdî hêdî mela destê xwe dirêjî pêsîr û memikan kir.
378. Poor Sînem assumes that it is the old woman and she is doing her clothes and scrubbing her back, until slowly the mela stretched his hand to her bosom and breasts.

379. Sînem: Ev çi ye pîrê tu çime destê xwe dirêjî pêşberê min dike.
379. Sînem: What is this old woman, why are you stretching your hand to my front.

380. Axîn û himîn ji mela hat û ew kişand bi ser xwe de û got: Xatûna min ez im ez, delal û nazika min ma ev çi roj e dergehê bihuştê hemû vekirî ne, nazik û perîkevokê, xebxeb şîn difirin û datînin îro ez ê bihuşta xweş bi çavê serê xwe bibînim, xanima min kevok û dîlbera min.
380. Sighing and groaning came from the mela, and he pulled her over himself and said: My lady, it is me, it is me, my dear and my delicate one, what a day this is, the gates of paradise are all open, delicate and fairy dove, the blue small birds fly and settle; today I will see sweet paradise with the eyes of my head, my madam, my dove and my beloved.

381. Û cardî ew bi ser xwe de kişand bi hêrs û xiste hembêza xwe de.
381. And again he pulled her over himself with force and put her in his embrace.

382. Sînem av bi ser xwe da kir û xwe ji kef û sabûnê xelas kir û kir û nekir xwe ji destê mela xelas nekir.
382. Sînem poured water over herself and freed herself from the foam and soap, but try as she might, she did not free herself from the mela's hand.

383. Nas kir ku ketîye dafikê de û tu çare jê re tune ye û bi dest lepkê nikare bi mela.
383. She realized that she had fallen into a trap and there is no solution for her and with bare hands she cannot overcome the mela.

384. Rabû dev ji zor û circirê berda û dest bi xap û fena kir.
384. She got up, gave up on force and struggling, and started with deceit and tricks.

385. Sînem: Ez gorî te me seyda, min digot qey tu henekê xwe bi min dikî û tu ji min hez nakî ez çemedî serê te bim sedê wek mîr dikim çemeda serê te, de ka min berde ez xwe ji vê sabûn û kefê xelas bikim ma her ez ji te re me, ma ez ê bi ku derê de herim.
385. Sînem: I am your sacrifice, master, I thought perhaps you were joking with me and you do not love me; let me be a sacrifice for your head, I make a hundred like the mîr a sacrifice for your head, come on, let me go so I can free myself from this soap and foam, after all I am yours anyway, where will I go.

386. Mela rabû bi kêf û şahî û ramîsanek bi zorê jê stand û got: "Ox ev çi bihuşt e, ev çi gul û çîçek û beybûn e îşev wê çîya li çîya binerin, gur û şêr wê li serê çîya bizûrin, çivîk û tilûr wê bifirin pelwaz bidin û bikin çîveçîv, û fîxan û şalûr û bilbil wê mûzîka evînîyê ji min û Sînema min re bibêjin.
386. The mela got up with joy and celebration and forcefully took a kiss from her and said: "Oh, what paradise this is, what rose and blossom and daisy this is; tonight mountain will look upon mountain, wolves and lions will roar on the mountaintop, sparrows and birds will fly, taking wing and chirping, and the wailing ones and the bee-eater and the nightingale will sing the music of love for me and my Sînem.

387. De rabe xezala min de rabe, zerîyê û nazikê, şox û şengê de rabe".
387. Come on, get up, my gazelle, come on, get up, blonde and delicate one, vivacious and joyful one, come on, get up".

388. Sînem rabû û got: Seyda de ka cilê xwe deyne ez ê serê te û laşê te bi sabûna şînokê qenc bişom û dûre em ê kêf û henekê xwe bi dilê xwe û bi bêhna fireh bikin, ma çi li dû me heye.
388. Sînem got up and said: Master, come put your clothes down, I will wash your head and your body thoroughly with the blue soap, and then we will have our fun and joking to our heart's content and with wide breath (at our leisure), what is chasing us anyway.

389. Mela di nav lepê Sînemê de sist bû.
389. The mela loosened up in Sînem's hands.

390. Sînem rû û serê wî kef kir û ji nişkê ve rahişt tasa hindo û li nîvê serê wî xist.
390. Sînem lathered his face and head and suddenly snatched up the copper bowl and struck the middle of his head.

391. Tas (zerik) di nîvê serî de çû xwarê û xwîn bi ser mela de herikî û mela ji hiş ket.
391. The bowl (brass) sank down into the middle of his head, and blood flowed over the mela, and the mela fell unconscious.

392. Sînem rabû cilê xwe li xwe kirin û eba şaqoye û serçavika xwe bi ser xwe de kir, kilît ji bêrîka mela derxist, derî vekir nerî ku êvar e şev ketîye erdê, berwar û berwar meşîya heya giha malê kete hundir û derî li xwe girtin û kelagirî ew hilanî bû îskeîska wê û bi ser hal û hetîketîya xwe de ponijî, nema dizane wê çi bike.
392. Sînem got up, put her clothes on, and put her black cloak and head-cover over herself, took the key out of the mela's pocket, opened the door, saw that it is evening and night has fallen on the earth, walked up the slope and up the slope until she reached home, went inside and closed the doors on herself, and a fit of weeping seized her, sobbing, she pondered over her condition and scandal, no longer knowing what she will do.

393. Dibêjin, "tas hat û çingirî yek bê derewe wê deh bêjin rast e.
393. They say, "the bowl came and clinked (rumor spread), if one says it is a lie, ten will say it is true.

394. Ya Rebî ya Xwedê yo ev çi bela bû hate serê min", û digirî.
394. O Lord, O God, what a trouble this was that came upon my head", and she wept.

395. 1. Tasa hindo ji sifir e.
395. 1. The Indian bowl is of copper.

396. Çar tas elbek in, her tasek çar lîtir av dikevinê.
396. Four bowls are one measure, four liters of water go into each bowl.

397. Piştî çend demjimêran mela bi ser hişê xwe ve hat, şev lê bûye nîvê şevê agir û pîto ji serê wî tê ji êşa.
397. After several hours the mela regained his senses, night had become midnight for him, fire and flames come from his head from the pain.

398. Hema rabû şaşika xwe bi serê xwe şidand û xwe ji xwînê paqij kir, cilên xwe li xwe kirin û derket ji hundirê avgerma serşokê pîsapîs dimeşe.
398. He immediately got up, tightened his turban around his head and cleaned himself of the blood, put his clothes on and went out of the inside of the hot baths, limping.

399. Çû kuşka xwe û şand pey hekîm û bijîjkan qene serê wî derman bikin.
399. He went to his palace and sent for doctors and physicians so they could treat his head.

400. Bi şeb û kuzûrîyê û ji wan re digot: "Ez ji ser pêlpêloka minara mizgeftê de ketim, min dikir ku ez herim banga serê sibê bêjim ji bo nimêjê û hema min dît ji nijkê ve ez şemitîm wek deh zilam min bidehfînin û ji jor ve ez hatim xwarê, hestîkî min sax nema ye tu dibêje qey ez di cûnî (cirn) de te ez kutame û ez nizanim bê serê min li çi ketîye, li qorzîya kevirê pêlpêlokê ketîye qet ez nizanim, ez ji ser hişê xwe çûm û min tiştek nedît hema ez şîyar bûm û min çavên xwe vekirin ku ez di nav xwînê de vegevizîme û agir û pêtî bi serê min ketîye, bi zor û heft bela min xwe gihand kuşkê, De Xwedê û Pêxember ji we razî bin û rehma Xwedê li dê û bavê we be hûn ê xweşik derman bikin û baş girê bidin”.
400. With groaning and moaning he was saying to them: "I fell from the stairs of the mosque's minaret, I was trying to go and say the morning call to prayer, and I just saw that suddenly I slipped as if ten men were pushing me, and from above I came down; not a bone of mine remains whole, you would say as if I were pounded in a mortar, and I don't know what my head hit, whether it hit the corner of the stair stone I don't know at all, I lost my senses and I saw nothing, I just woke up and opened my eyes to find I am wallowing in blood and fire and flame have fallen on my head, with difficulty and seven troubles I reached the palace. Come, may God and the Prophet be pleased with you and God's mercy be upon your parents, you will treat it nicely and bandage it well".

401. Piştî mela bi ser hişê xwe ve hat û birîna wî hêdî hêdî hat hev û şewta dijwar şikest û piçekî kêm bû mela rabû dest bi nameyan kir û şand ji mîr re.
401. After the mela regained his senses and his wound slowly came together, and the severe burning broke and decreased a little, the mela got up, started on letters, and sent them to the mîr.

402. "Mîrê min!
402. "My mîr!

403. Ez bi gorî serê te bim ez, ezbenî ez, vê nameyê ji te re dinivîsim lê divê tu li min negirî bê ez ê çi bibêjim û çi nebêjim.
403. May I be a sacrifice for your head, I, my sir, I am writing this letter to you, but you must not hold it against me what I will say and what I will not say.

404. Mîrê min!
404. My mîr!

405. Piştî ku tu bi oxira xwe de çûyî û dinya xêz vêz bû çend roj û heftî qedîyan û hûn bi dûr ketin, ez neçar im ku ez bibêjim ji ber ku te ez kirime îşgerê xwe li ser mal û kulfetê te û ez Miftîyê Misrê me ne durist e ku çi çêbibe û ez ji te re nebêjim ez pê gunehkar dibim.
405. After you went on your journey and the world turned topsy-turvy, a few days and weeks finished and you fell far away, I am forced to speak because you made me your manager over your house and household, and I am the Mufti of Egypt; it is not right that whatever happens I do not tell you, I become a sinner by it.

406. Mîrê min!
406. My mîr!

407. Nizanim çilo dest pê bikim divê tu li min negirî û tilîyê min pênûsê nagirin ku ez binivîsim ev tiştê ne kesî dîtî û negotî û belkî tu bibêje çima heya niha te nedigot tu nuh dibêje.
407. I do not know how to start, you must not hold it against me and my fingers do not grip the pen for me to write this thing that no one has seen or spoken of, and maybe you will say why were you not speaking until now, you are speaking newly.

408. Berê te li çûnê bû û berê te li mala Xwedê bû bi kêf û şahî bû yî, ma çidibû ku ez kêfa te li te bişikînim û min digot belkî
408. Your direction was toward going, and your direction was toward the House of God; you were with joy and celebration, how could it be that I break your joy, and I was saying maybe

409. Xwedê wê vegerîne ji xeta xwar û dev ji finasê xwe berde, lê ez çi bikim ezbenî pîsîtîyê zora başîtîyê bir, bê şerm û bê fedî sînem Xatun şevbihêrka digerîne bi xort û serseryan re heya serê sibehê di nav kesê wilo de bû.
409. God will turn her back from the crooked line and she will give up her schemes, but what can I do, sir, wickedness overpowered goodness; without shame and without embarrassment Lady Sînem holds night parties with youths and vagabonds, until morning she was among such people.

410. ez nema zanim çi bibêjim û çi nebêjim.
410. I no longer know what to say and what not to say.

411. Ezxulam û aniha berê te li malê ye ez ji te re eşkere dikim finasê Sînemê qene tu çareyekê jê re bibînî û berî tu bê û tu bihetikî li nav miletê Misrê û bê ka tu çi ji min re dibêjî ji bo ku ez bikim".
411. May I be a servant, and now that your direction is homeward, I reveal Sînem's schemes to you so that you may find a solution for it and before you come and you are disgraced among the nation of Egypt, and tell me what you say for me to do".

412. Name gihast dest Mîr Mamed, xwend û xwend, carekê diduya û sisêyan.
412. The letter reached Mîr Mamed's hand, he read it and read it, once, twice, and three times.

413. Bawer nekir ku Sînem vî tiştî bike û ji xwe re got: "Û çilo miftîyê welêt û cîgirê bawerîyê Mela Itman vî tiştî dibêje û ji min re dişîne ku ne rast ba mela nedigot û nedişand û Sînem dotmama min e û hezkirina min e û evqas sal me bi hev re derbas kirinemin tiştek jê nebihîst û min tiştek li dorê nedît û qeysî serê derzîyê ez pê guman neketime lê ez çi bikim tas hat û çingirî çi rast, çi derew be em hetikîn”.
413. He did not believe that Sînem would do this thing, and said to himself: "And how does the mufti of the country and the deputy of faith Mela Itman say this thing and send it to me? If it were not true the mela would not say it and would not send it; and Sînem is my cousin and my love, and all these years we have spent together I heard nothing from her and I saw nothing around her, and not even the size of a needle's head have I fallen into suspicion of her, but what can I do, the bowl came and clinked, whether it be true, whether it be a lie, we are disgraced".

414. Û mîr maye di kul û xema de bi xwe re dipeyive wek dîna lê hatîye nema bawer dike bê wê kengî bigihêje malê.
414. And the mîr remains in pain and sorrow, talking to himself, he has become like a madman, no longer believing when he will reach home.

415. Mela Itman name li ser nameyê dişîne qene mîr bersivekê jê re bişîne bi kuştina Sînemê ji bo kar û finasê xwe veşêre û careke din nivîsand û got:
415. Mela Itman sends letter upon letter so that the mîr will send him an answer for the killing of Sînem, to hide his deeds and schemes, and once again he wrote and said:

416. "Ey mîrê min ka ez çi bikim ji vê hetîketîyê, bajarê Misrê bajarekî mezin û giran e dost û yarê Sînem hemî xort û gedan e.
416. "O my mîr, what am I to do about this scandal, the city of Egypt is a large and heavy city, Sînem's lovers and paramours are all youths and boys.

417. Ey mîrê min bajarê Misrê li ser sê sed û şêst mihelan e.
417. O my mîr, the city of Egypt is built upon three hundred and sixty neighborhoods.

418. Dost û yarê Sînemê hemî meyvexurê çarçîya ne".
418. Sînem's lovers and paramours are all fruit-eaters of the markets".

419. Pepûkê Mîr Mamed serê xwe li bin guhê tehta dixe nema dizane wê çi bibêje û çi bi yarê bide û derdê wî ye zû bigihêje malê.
419. Poor Mîr Mamed hits his head against the side of rocks, he no longer knows what to say and what to decide, and his concern is to quickly reach home.

420. Mela jî nameyê li ser nameyê dişîne û gunehê Sînemê giran dike, û pepûka Sînemê hayê wê ji kar û finasê mela tune ye ku nameyan ji mîr re dişîne û wêna dihetikîne û bi dost û yar dike.
420. The mela too sends letter upon letter and makes Sînem's sin heavier, and poor Sînem has no awareness of the mela's deeds and schemes, that he is sending letters to the mîr and disgracing her and making her out to have lovers and paramours.

421. Wê derî li xwe kilît kirîye û nema dihêle çûk bi çûkanîya xwe derbas bibe kuşka wê, nema li tu kesî ewle dibe û bi şev û bi roj digirî û dibêje, "weyla li min bextreşê, weyla li min rûreşê, ez ê çi bersiva xwe li ber mîr bidim, weyla li min jarê, li min qijokê, weyla li min kurekemê, vî kûçikî vî telaqreş î çi anî serê min ya Rebî ya Xwedêyo ji te ve beyan e xuya ye û tu zanî ez bêrî me ji van tiştan û vî bêbextî bêwijdan î bextê min bi reş kir ka ez ê çi bikim, çi bibêjim ez jin im, pîrek im kes ji min bawer nake û xelkê ji rêya wî ya spî û bi du bihusta dirêj bawer wê bikin û ew miftîyê ola misilmana ye û melê mîr e, ma ez pepûka Xwedê çime û li ber çime û çi hêjame kevnek jin im”.
421. She has locked her doors upon herself and no longer lets even a bird with its bird-ness pass into her palace, she no longer trusts anyone and cries by night and by day and says, "woe is me, black-fortuned, woe is me, black-faced, what answer will I give before the mîr; woe is me, miserable one, woe is me, wailing one, woe is me, short-sighted one; what has this dog, this black-divorced one brought upon my head; O Lord, O God, from You it is evident and visible, and You know I am innocent of these things and this treacherous, conscienceless one has blackened my fortune; what shall I do, what shall I say, I am a woman, a female, no one will believe me, and the people will believe his white beard, two spans long, and he is the mufti of the Muslim religion and the mîr's mela; so what am I, God's poor one, and what do I stand for, and what am I worth, I am an old woman".

422. Şev çûn û roj hatin kerwanê mîr û hecacîyan nêzîkayî li bajêr kir.
422. Nights went and days came, the caravan of the mîr and the pilgrims drew near to the city.

423. Mela rabû pêşwazîyeke mezin li dar xist û hemû mela û feqê mizgeftan û suxtê xwendevan li xwendina Quranê dicivin û banga li mêjê û Alah û Akber û feqa û suxta beylûta li dar dixin û govendê digerînin.
423. The mela got up, organized a great reception, and all the melas and students of the mosques and reading pupils gather for reading the Quran, and the call to prayer and Allahu Akbar, and the students and pupils arrange festivities and dance the govend.

424. Û miletê Misrê bi dû wan de ne her malek hatine pêşîya hecacê xwe û hayê pepûka Sînemê ji vî tiştî tune ye û pê nehisîyaye ku hecacî hatine.
424. And the nation of Egypt is behind them, every household has come before their pilgrim, and poor Sînem has no awareness of this thing and has not sensed that the pilgrims have come.

425. Heya ketin nav bajêr ji nû ve Sînem rabû xwe girê da û bang li çend carîyan kir û kete hafa xwe de û hat pêşwazîya mîr.
425. When they entered the city, anew Sînem got up, girded herself, called a few maids, composed herself, and came to welcome the mîr.

426. Ew nizane bê mela çi kirîye û çi bêbextî ji mîr re gotîye.
426. She does not know what the mela has done and what treachery he has told the mîr.

427. Mîrê reben ser di ber de, çavpêl, rûçiktehl, mêş ji rûyê wî bikeve wê bibe pazde perçe.
427. The wretched mîr, head bowed, eyes swollen, face bitter, if a fly fell from his face it would shatter into fifteen pieces (he is furious).

428. Demjimêr hêdî hêdî derbas bûn mêvan û pêşwazîyên mîr rabûn çûn malên xwe.
428. The hours slowly passed, the mîr's guests and welcomers got up and went to their homes.

429. Şev ket erdê mîr ma rûniştî ne deng û ne pêjin.
429. Night fell on the earth, the mîr remained sitting, no sound and no noise.

430. Sînem hat xêrhatin tê da û silav lê kir û rûnişt.
430. Sînem came, welcomed him, greeted him, and sat.

431. Demek derbas bû deng ji her duyan nehat ne mîr deng kir û ne Sînem.
431. A time passed, no sound came from either, neither the mîr made a sound nor Sînem.

432. Sînem: Lo lo kur mamo lo lo pismamo şev li min û te hatî nîvê şevê lo lo kuramo lolo pismamo ma tu nabijî tu çawa yî lê lê dotmamê vê şevê.
432. Sînem: Oh oh cousin, oh oh cousin, the night upon me and you has become midnight, oh oh cousin, oh oh cousin, won't you say how are you, oh oh cousin, this night.

433. Mîr: Lê lê Sînemê, ne li ser bextê min be li ser bextê Mela Itman be dibêje dost û yarê Sînemê hemî çet e û keleş in.
433. Mîr: Oh oh Sînem, may it not be upon my fortune, may it be upon Mela Itman's fortune, he says Sînem's lovers and paramours are all bandits and rogues.

434. Lê lê dotmamê lê lê bextreşê ne li ser bextê min be li ser bextê Mela Itman be dibêje dostê Sînemê pêxwas û serxweş in.
434. Oh oh cousin, oh oh black-fortuned, may it not be upon my fortune, may it be upon Mela Itman's fortune, he says Sînem's lovers are barefoot and drunkards.

435. Sînem: Lo lo kurmamo lo lo pismamo derfetê bide min lo lo kurmamo ez bersiva xwe bidim û bibêlînim.
435. Sînem: Oh oh cousin, oh oh cousin, give me the opportunity, oh oh cousin, so I can give my answer and explain.

436. Mîr: Lê lê Sînemê lê lê dotmamê ma tu çi bibêjî çi bibêlînî ku tas û çingirî wê sed bê rast e heya yek bêje bêbextî ne.
436. Mîr: Oh oh Sînem, oh oh cousin, what will you say, what will you explain, since the bowl came and clinked, a hundred will say it is true, while only one says it is treachery.

437. Sînem: Wey li min rûreşê bêxwedîyê ev çi bêbextî ne, wey li min pepûkê ma ez rebena Xwedê ka ez çi bikim wey li min porkurê li min qijokê.
437. Sînem: Woe is me, black-faced, ownerless one, what treachery this is, woe is me, poor one, what am I, God's wretched one, to do, woe is me, hair-shorn one, woe is me, wailing one.

438. Mîr: Lê lê Sînemê lê lê dotmamê bajarê Misrê bi darê bî ye, lê lê Sînemê, lê lê dotmamê ji bajarê Misrê derkeve bê fedî ye.
438. Mîr: Oh oh Sînem, oh oh cousin, the city of Egypt is with willow trees, oh oh Sînem, oh oh cousin, leave the city of Egypt, shameless one.

439. Lê lê dotmamê çevên min bar nabe ez te bikujim bi min zor û zehmetî ye.
439. Oh oh cousin, my eyes cannot bear it, to kill you is hard and difficult for me.

440. De rabe rabe berî banga serê sibê li me dere.
440. Come on, get up, get up, before the morning call comes upon us.

441. Sînem bêçar e bû hema rabû û ji dîwana mîr derket wek dîna û berzûrî Xwedê bû û got: "Ya rebî ya xwedêyo ji te ve xuya ye bêbextî li min bûye ez pepûka Xwedê ez ê çi bikim kes ji min bawer nake.
441. Sînem was desperate, she simply got up and went out of the mîr's room like a madwoman, and supplicated to God and said: "O Lord, O God, it is visible from You that treachery has happened to me, what am I, God's poor one, to do, no one believes me.

442. Ya xwedêyo tu heft sala xela û cela (zuhayê) li Misrê rake tu bedena jinê wan şîn neke tu şîrê dewar û pezê wan bi xwîn û elemke û tu Mîr Mamed bi nexweşîkê bixe û heft kulav di bin de birizin li ser piştê be û rihet nebe heya neyêm ser û serpêhatîya xwe jê re bi ta û derzîyê vekim ku nas bike ez bêrî me û Mela Itman bêbext e".
442. O God, raise seven years of famine and drought in Egypt, do not make the bodies of their women green (fertile), make the milk of their cattle and sheep into blood and pus, and strike Mîr Mamed with a sickness, and let seven felt mats rot beneath him, let him be on his back and not rest until I come over him and unfold my adventure to him with thread and needle, so that he knows I am innocent and Mela Itman is treacherous".

443. Di derî re derket berê xwe da çolê derveyî bajêr û tim û tim ber bi bakur ve çû.
443. She went out through the door, turned to the wilderness outside the city and went ever and always toward the north.

444. Ro lê derket hat taştîya xwe bixwe, li xwe nerî û li cilê xwe nerî û got: "Ez bi vî rengî û bi va cila ji destê pêxwas û keleş û rêwîya xelas nabim".
444. The sun rose on her, she came to eat her breakfast, looked at herself and looked at her clothes and said: "Like this and with these clothes, I will not be saved from the hands of the barefoot, the rogues, and the travelers".

445. Meşîya meşîya li kerîk pez rast hat berê xwe da şivên û çû cem û jê re got: "Kuro şivano ji te zêrek û ev cilê li min, tê berxekî, kavirekê ser jê bikî û bigurênî em ê goştê wê bixwin û tê îyarê wê bide min".
445. She walked and walked, came across a flock of sheep, turned to the shepherd and went to him and said to him: "Boy, shepherd, here is a gold coin for you and these clothes on me, you will cut the head of a lamb, a yearling, and skin it, we will eat its meat and you will give me its hide".

446. Kêfa şivan hat zû kavirek avêt erdê û ser jê kir û gurand, goşt biraştin, xwarin û Sînem rahişt îyar û bi axê zuha kir û çû bi rê de li xwe kir bo kes wê nas neke ku jin e.
446. The shepherd was glad, quickly threw a yearling to the ground and cut its head and skinned it; they roasted the meat, ate, and Sînem took the hide and dried it with dirt and went on the road, putting it on so no one would recognize her as a woman.

447. Bi lez û bez ji erda Misrê derket û dimeşe û dilezîne qûnax bi qûnax û gund bi gund heya gihaşt bajarekî mezin bi çem û cobar, bi dar û devî, bi dewar û pez û tilûr.
447. With speed and running she left the land of Egypt and marches and hurries, stage by stage and village by village, until she reached a large city with rivers and streams, with trees and bushes, with cattle and sheep and birds.

448. Sînem navê xwe xist Gurî û berê xwe da mala paşê ku gepek nên bixwe li wê hewşê.
448. Sînem put her name as Gurî (the Mangy One) and turned to the pasha's house to eat a piece of bread in that courtyard.

449. Piştî taîtîya paşê ji malê derket berê xwe da dîwan û odeyê, Sînem (Gurî) çû pêşîyê û got: "Ezxulam, ez bêkes im, bêxwedî me, ez gurî me dixwazim gepek (parîk) nanê xwe bi qerwaşî bixwim".
449. After the pasha's breakfast, he came out of the house and turned to the court and room, Sînem (Gurî) went before him and said: "May I be a servant, I am lonely, I am ownerless, I am mangy, I want to eat my piece of bread through servitude".

450. Paşe: Ma ka law ez ê çi karî ji te re bibînim li gorî te û taqeta te?
450. Pasha: Well, boy, what work shall I find for you according to you and your strength?

451. Û Gurî xwe kelegirî dike di bin îyarê kavirê de, Xwedê wilo kir kucarîya di wê navê re refê qazan ji hewşê derxistin û ajotin derve û hin cêrî di ber xwe de dibêjin, "nebixêr ev qaz li me bûne bela kes tune ye wan bibe çolê biçêrîne..."
451. And Gurî holds back her tears under the yearling's hide; God so willed it that the maids in that moment brought a flock of geese out of the courtyard and drove them outside, and some maids were saying to themselves, "woe, these geese have become a trouble to us, there is no one to take them to the wilderness to graze..."

452. Deng çû Gurî.
452. The sound reached Gurî.

453. Gurî: Ezbenî, ah va qazê te bê şivan in.
453. Gurî: My sir, ah, look your geese are without a shepherd.

454. De hema destûrê bide min ez ê herim ber wan şivanê qaza bi qerwaşî.
454. Come just give me permission, I will go before them as a goose shepherd in servitude.

455. Paşe: Baş e wele, de here law wan dûr bibe di nav daristanê re bibe ser çem, wê li wir ji xwe re biçêrin û êvarî wan werîne lûs.
455. Pasha: Fine by God, come on go, boy, take them far through the forest, take them to the river, they will graze there for themselves and in the evening bring them to the pen.

456. Kuro kuro Kurtêlxuro de here here bide pêşîya qaza û Gurî bibe ser çêm, û rêya çûn û hatinê şanî Gurî bike û vegere.
456. Boy, boy, Scavenger boy, come on go, go lead the geese and take Gurî to the river, and show Gurî the way going and coming, and return.

457. Kurtêlxuro da pêşîya qazan û Gurî, rahişt şivekê û da dû qazan û ajotin birin ser çêm, û xulam vegerîya.
457. The Scavenger led the geese and Gurî, grabbed a stick and went after the geese, drove them and took them to the river, and the servant returned.

458. Gurî li dora xwe nerî hawîrdor ne kes û ne kûs, nîvro ye germ bûye dinya.
458. Gurî looked around herself, all around there is no one and nobody, it is noon, the world has grown hot.

459. Hema Sînem çermê xwe ji xwe kir û kete ava çêm bi lez û bez xwe şûşt û derket careke din çermê xwe li xwe kir bîna wê derket, xwe li ber qaza dirêj kir û di dilê xwe de got: "Xêr e Xwedayo ez dûrî xelkê me û hayê kesî ji min tune ye û ez ê Şivantîya xwe bikim li ber van qazan û vî çemî nanê xwe bi
459. Then Sînem took off her hide and entered the river's water, washed herself quickly and came out, once again she put on her hide, she caught her breath, stretched herself out before the geese and said in her heart: "It is good, O God, I am far from the people and no one is aware of me, and I will do my shepherding before these geese and this river, and eat my bread

460. hesanî bixwim, xwe carê bi dizî bişom ka bê Xwedê çi li pêşîya min nivîsandîye", û xilmaşî xewê bû.
460. easily, occasionally washing myself secretly to see what God has written before me", and she dozed off to sleep.

461. Karê Gurî ma ev roj bi roj, meh bi meh û giha salan bi vî halî.
461. Gurî's work remained this, day by day, month by month, and it reached years in this state.

462. Em ê dev ji Sînem (Gurî) berdin di wî karî û wî halî de û em ê vegerin bajarê Misrê dîwana Mîr Mamed û Mela Itman.
462. We will leave Sînem (Gurî) in that work and that state, and we will return to the city of Egypt, to the court of Mîr Mamed and Mela Itman.

463. Xwedê daxwaza Sînem bi cih anî û mîr nexweş ket li ser piştê, ne hekîm û ne bijîşk û ne tu kes ji nexweşîya wî fêm dike û derman lê nayên.
463. God fulfilled Sînem's request and the mîr fell sick on his back, neither doctor nor physician nor anyone understands his sickness and medicines do not work on him.

464. Salê kulavek di bin de dirize û miletê Misrê ketine halekî pîs de, ne xwarin, ne zad û ne nan xelk çûne helaketê.
464. Each year a felt mat rots beneath him, and the nation of Egypt fell into a terrible state, no food, no grain, and no bread, the people went into ruin.

465. Jinên wan nema têr dibin, zarokan naynin, pez û dewarê wan bê gon û zayîn mane û Mela Itman maye mîrê bi destê xwe ve, ne kes li pêş û ne li paş çi bêje ew e û çi fermanê derxe bi navê mîr e kes nikare li ber rabe.
465. Their women are no longer satisfied, they do not bring children, their sheep and cattle have remained without mating and birthing, and Mela Itman has remained a mîr by his own hand, there is no one before him and no one behind him, whatever he says goes, and whatever order he issues is in the mîr's name, no one can stand against him.

466. Bixwe, birjîne, biavêje, xelkê bigire, berde, bikuje, wan têxe zindanê de, kes li hemberî wî tune ye wek berazê yekane ye kes newêre jê re bibêje sîya te xwar e.
466. Let him eat, let him spill, let him throw, let him arrest people, release them, kill them, put them in prison, there is no one against him; he is like a lone boar, no one dares say to him your shadow is crooked.

467. Sal bi dû salê de derbas bûn miletê Misrê û ajalê xwe nêvî mirin ji birçîna, ji tîna, ji feqîrtî û belengazîyê û qirêjê.
467. Year after year passed, half the nation of Egypt and their animals died from hunger, from thirst, from poverty and destitution and filth.

468. Sal li hev vegerîyan kete sala heftan de.
468. Years turned upon each other, it entered the seventh year.

469. Çire tu nabêjî kurê paşê derketîye nêçîrê û hatîye nav daristanê dexla malbatê.
469. What do you know, the pasha's son went out hunting and came into the forest of the family's estate.

470. hilkişîya ser dareke fêkî û hêdî hêdî ji xwe re jê dike û dixwe û hayê Sînemê jê nîne.
470. He climbed up a fruit tree and slowly plucks and eats for himself, and Sînem is completely unaware of him.

471. Wê jî pepûkê wek her car çermê xwe bi ser xwe de anî û kete avê, qîjîn bi qaza ket kurê paşê serê xwe rakir û li hêla qazan nerî bê çibû çima qaza kir qajeqaj.
471. She too, poor thing, as always pulled her hide over herself and entered the water, a squawking caught the geese, the pasha's son raised his head and looked toward the geese to see what happened, why the geese were cackling.

472. Dema serê xwe rakir û nerî bê çi horîya bihuştê di nav avê de ye, çi qozaxa jina ye.
472. When he raised his head and looked, what a houri of paradise is in the water, what a blossom of a woman.

473. Devê wî ma ji hev û gosretmayî ma wek termekî li ser darê.
473. His mouth fell open and he remained astounded, like a corpse on the tree.

474. Pepûka Sînem çermê xwe li xwe kir wek her car û êvarî berê xwe da malê cê lûsê qazan.
474. Poor Sînem put on her hide as always, and in the evening turned toward home, the place of the goose pen.

475. Kurê paşê şîyar bû ji wê gosretê û ji xwe re dibêje, "gelo ev xewn bû ev rastî bû çawa ev heft salê vê jinkê li ber qazê
475. The pasha's son awoke from that astonishment and says to himself, "I wonder, was this a dream, was this reality, how is it that for these seven years this woman is before the geese

476. me qedîyane û kesek pê guman neketîye ev çi jine çi bela wê ye çi gosret û bela hatine serê wê heya xwe xistîye vî halî", û kurê paşê pîsapîs dimeşe û berê xwe daye malê bawer nake ku Gurî bigire û saxtî bike û nas bike.
476. have passed for us and no one has fallen into suspicion of her, what woman is this, what is her trouble, what astonishment and trouble have come upon her head until she put herself in this state", and the pasha's son walks limping and has turned his direction home, not believing (trusting himself) to catch Gurî and examine and recognize her.

477. Roj çû ava, qaz çûn lûsê xwe, Gurî jî li devê derîyê wan rûniştîye, kurê paşê giha malê ji dêya xwe re got îşev bera Guri şîva min ji min re bîne odeya min.
477. The sun went down, the geese went to their pen, Gurî too is sitting at the doorway of their door; the pasha's son reached home and said to his mother, tonight let Gurî bring my dinner to me in my room.

478. Xatûn (dêya wî): Wa weylê pepû tu çi dibêjî kuro gurî ye qedê serê bi kinik, bêvil bi lîçik, çilo wê xwarina te ji te re bîne?
478. Xatûn (his mother): Oh woe, poor thing, what are you saying boy, she is mangy, short-statured, nose with snot, how will she bring your food to you?

479. Ma xulam tune ne tu dîn bûye çi bi te hatîye.
479. Are there no servants, have you gone mad, what has happened to you?

480. Kurê paşê: Ez ne dîn im ne serxweş im bera Gurî şîva min bîne û hew.
480. The pasha's son: I am not mad, I am not drunk, let Gurî bring my dinner and that is all.

481. Û meşîya bi lez ket hundirê odeya xwe de û derî li xwe asê kir, girt.
481. And he walked with speed, entered inside his room and secured the door on himself, closed it.

482. Şev ket erdê bû wextê şîva xatûnê.
482. Night fell on the earth, it became the time for the xatûn's dinner.

483. Şîva kurê xwe dagirt û danî ser tevekê û bang li Gurî kir: "Gurî Gurî! Hela tu were vir".
483. She filled her son's dinner and put it on a tray and called to Gurî: "Gurî, Gurî! Come here for a moment".

484. Gurî rabû bi tirs û hêrs, "çi ye xatûna min, tu çi ji min dixwazî? Ezxulam ez giş qilêr im genî me".
484. Gurî got up with fear and anger, "what is it my lady, what do you want from me? May I be a servant, I am all filth, I am foul-smelling".

485. Xatûn: Xem nake ji te re ev teveka xwarin li ser û bibe ji kurê min re li odeya xwe ye.
485. Xatûn: No matter to you, this tray with food on it, and take it to my son, he is in his room.

486. Guri (kelogirî bû): Ez genî me, ez bi qilêr im, çilo ez ê rajim xwarina mîrê xwe? ez nikarim.
486. Gurî (started crying): I am foul-smelling, I am with filth, how will I pick up my mîr's food? I cannot.

487. Xatûn: De rahijîyê gurîyê pîs yê çepel ev fermana kurê min e.
487. Xatûn: Come pick it up, filthy mangy one, dirty one, this is my son's order.

488. Gurî ji neçarî hêdî rahişt tevekê û berê xwe da odeya kurê paşê.
488. Gurî out of necessity slowly grabbed the tray and turned to the room of the pasha's son.

489. Sînem nas kir ku tiştek heye û kurik ew nas kirîye hema tevek danî ser devê derî, û di reşê de got: "Nigo bi qurbano", bi lez û bazdan ji bajêr derket û tim û tim berjêr bû.
489. Sînem realized that there is something and the boy has recognized her, she just put the tray down at the doorway, and in the dark said: "May the feet be a sacrifice", with speed and running she left the city and went ever and always downward.

490. Demek qedîya şîva kurê paşê nehat qîr kir li xulama kurtêluura: "Ka Gurî, li ku ma?"
490. A time passed, the pasha's son's dinner did not come, he yelled at the scavenger servant: "Where is Gurî, where did she remain?"

491. Hatin kom bûn li devê derî dîtin ku şîva wî li ser tevekê ye û pisîk û kitik ketine ser dixwin.
491. They came and gathered at the doorway, they saw that his dinner is on the tray and cats and kittens have fallen upon it eating.

492. Ka Gurî ka Gurî dunya şevreş e kes kesî nabîne tu tilîyan di çavên yekî de bike te nabîne.
492. Where is Gurî, where is Gurî, the world is pitch black, no one sees anyone, if you put fingers in someone's eyes they do not see you.

493. Bi vir de Gurî bi wir de Gurî Xwedê bide Gurî, wenda bû tu dibê qey erd veqelişî û Gurî têde wenda bû.
493. Gurî here, Gurî there, may God give Gurî, she disappeared, you would say as if the earth split open and Gurî disappeared into it.

494. Xulam, kurtêlxur, şivan, gavan, gundî giş ker û gêj bûn Gurî nedîtin.
494. Servants, scavengers, shepherds, cowherds, villagers all became deaf and dizzy, they did not find Gurî.

495. Wê şevê pê de Gurî nesekinî û nehedinî û xwe ji sînorê wî bajarî dûr xist, bi şev dimeşe û bi roj xwe vedişêre ji tirsa pêxwasan, çetan, dizan, rêwî û rêbiran.
495. From that night on Gurî did not stop and did not rest and distanced herself from the border of that city, walking by night and hiding herself by day from fear of the barefoot, bandits, thieves, travelers and highwaymen.

496. Şevek dido, heftîk dido kete meha mehek dido qedyan Sînem nêzîkayî li welatê Misrê kir, hêdî hêdî bîna xelkê derket, dar û devî û şinkayî şîn û kesk bûn, ava çemê mezin zelal bû, xelkê têr av vexwarin, mî û berx li hev banîyan, bû horhora çêleka, û borebora canga, barebara pez û likelika bizina.
496. A night or two, a week or two, it entered months, a month or two finished, Sînem drew near to the country of Egypt, slowly the breath of the people came out, trees and bushes and greenery became blue and green, the water of the great river became clear, the people drank full water, ewes and lambs called to each other, it became the lowing of the cows, and the bellowing of the bulls, the bleating of the sheep and the bleating of the goats.

497. Jîyan kete welêt, laşê Mîr Mamed nerm bû, rihayî kete canê wî, vêca dikare xwe bilebitîne, kêfa wî hat canê wî sivik dibe.
497. Life entered the country, Mîr Mamed's body softened, relief entered his soul, now he can move himself, his joy came, his soul becomes light.

498. Milet kete kêf û şahîyê.
498. The nation entered joy and celebration.

499. Cotkarî çûn cotê xwe, bexçeçî çûn nav bexçeyan û şînkayî çandin, xwedîyê peza mih û berxê xwe derxistin çolê çêrê, gavan û serwana dewarê xwe û devê xwe derxistin nav dexil û daristanan, xelk bi kêf dibin û her yekî berê xwe da karê xwe.
499. Farmers went to their plowing, gardeners went into the gardens and planted greenery, the owners of sheep took their ewes and lambs out to the wilderness for grazing, cowherds and cameleers took their cattle and camels out into the fields and forests, the people become joyful and each one turned to their own work.

500. Sînem kete rexê bajarê Misrê li kêleka bajêr derbas bû maleke belengaz dît ku mêrik û jina xwe û du zarok in bê şîv û bê xwarin.
500. Sînem entered the side of the city of Egypt, passed by the side of the city, saw a destitute household that is a man and his wife and two children without dinner and without food.

501. Rabû zêrek ji paşla xwe derxist û da dest xwedîyên malê, û jê re got: "Pismam ez rêwî me ne ji vî welatî me ez kesî nas nakim û nizanim herim bazarê, de şite ev zêr ji min re cilên zilama bikire, û bi perê mayî ji xwe û jina xwe û zarokên xwe re jî cila bikire û xwarinê ji me re werîne".
501. She got up, took a gold coin from her bosom and gave it to the hand of the owners of the house, and said to him: "Cousin, I am a traveler, I am not from this country, I do not know anyone and do not know how to go to the market, come take this gold coin, buy men's clothes for me, and with the remaining money buy clothes for yourself and your wife and your children, and bring food for us".

502. Mêrik bi kêf û lez û bez berê xwe da çarçîyê û tiştê xwe giş kirîn û bi lez hat malê cilên xwe li xwe kirin, şîva xwe danîn û xwarin, zarokan kêf kir, dilîzin û henekan dikin, cejna wa ye.
502. The man with joy and speed and running turned to the market and bought all his things and quickly came home, they put on their clothes, put down their dinner and ate, the children rejoiced, they play and make jokes, it is their feast.

503. Malxweyê malê ji mêvanê xwe re got: "Ezbenî mîrê me nexweş e ev heft salê wî li ser derzika piştê ye ferman daye mala gişa ku mêvanê kê bên divê hûn bînin odeya mîr pirsa ji wan dike çîrok û stran û serpêhatîya ji wan dixwaze qene
503. The master of the house said to his guest: "My sir, our mîr is sick, for these seven years he is on the needle of his back (flat on his back), he has given an order to all the houses that whoever's guests come you must bring them to the mîr's room, he asks them questions, wants stories and songs and adventures from them so that

504. sebra wî bînin û piçkî êşa xwe ji bîr bike, û qedexe ye ku em nerin ez ê gunehkar bibim".
504. they may bring him patience (amuse him) and he may forget his pain a little, and it is forbidden that we do not go, I will become a sinner".

505. Sînem: Na na pismam çima tê sûclî bibe ez jî dixwazim herim civata mîrê we û ez wî bibînim bê ka çi bûyer û gosret hatine, serpêhatîyek xweş û durist li cem min heye ez ê jê re bibêjim de rabe em herin dîwana mîr.
505. Sînem: No, no, cousin, why should you be guilty, I too want to go to the assembly of your mîr and see him, to see what events and astonishments have come, I have a sweet and true adventure with me, I will tell it to him, come get up, let us go to the mîr's court.

506. Rabûn û her duyan dan tenista hev û çûn civata mîr, çawa ketin odeyê de laşê mîr sivik bû û li qûn rûnişt û got: "Hatina we xêr e û nigê we li min hat, kuro tu kî ye û mêvanê te çi kes e û ji ku ye?
506. They got up and the two of them walked side by side and went to the mîr's assembly, as soon as they entered the room the mîr's body became light and he sat on his bottom and said: "Your coming is goodness and your feet have come upon me (brought me luck), boy, who are you and what person is your guest and from where?

507. Tu di bê qey ez ê li ser destê wî sax bibim û rihet bibim".
507. You would say as if I will heal and rest by his hand".

508. Her du li nav şekala rûniştin ode tije ye, humîn û gumîn ji civatê tê.
508. The two of them sat among the shoes, the room is full, murmuring and muttering comes from the assembly.

509. Mela Itman û çend melayên din û feqê wan li hawîrdora mîr rûniştine û jê re sersaxîyê dixwazin.
509. Mela Itman and a few other melas and their students have sat around the mîr and wish him health.

510. Mîr: Mêvanê delal tu ji ku derê yî, ji kîjan welatî yî, te çi dîtîye, çi bihîstîye? ka were nêzîk rûne û ji min re bêje qene em şevbihêrka xwe derbas bikin.
510. Mîr: Dear guest, where are you from, from which country are you, what have you seen, what have you heard? Come sit near and speak to me so that we may pass our evening gathering.

511. Mêvan: Mîrê min, paşayê min, ez ê serpêhatîyeke rast û durist ji te re bêjim lê kes ji civatê ranabe, û tê derî kilît bike û kilîtê têke bin çoga xwe de û dûre ez ê çîrokê ji te re ta bi derzîyê ve bikim.
511. Guest: My mîr, my pasha, I will tell you a true and correct adventure but no one from the assembly shall rise, and you will lock the door and put the key under your knee and then I will unfold the story to you with thread and needle (in detail).

512. Mîr: Wele mêvano dengê te bi min xweş tê, ka were were hemberî min rûne, kuro dergevano derî bigire û asê û kilît bike û ka kilîtê werîne.
512. Mîr: By God, guest, your voice sounds sweet to me, come, come sit opposite me, boy, doorkeeper, close the door and secure and lock it, and come bring the key.

513. Dergevan rabû derî girt û kilît anî da dest mîr û mîr xist bin çoga xwe de û deng li mêvan kir, "vêca ka serpêhatîya xwe bibêje".
513. The doorkeeper got up, closed the door and brought the key, gave it to the mîr's hand and the mîr put it under his knee and called to the guest, "now come tell your adventure".

514. Sînem: Ezxulam, ev çîrok min ji devê kesê nas û xwedî wijdan bihîstîye.
514. Sînem: May I be a servant, I have heard this story from the mouth of a known and conscientious person.

515. "Dibêjin li welatekî ji welatê misilmana mîrê wan bi kêf û Şahî bû û miletê wî bi xêr û xweşî bû.
515. "They say in a country of the countries of the Muslims their mîr was with joy and celebration and his nation was in goodness and health.

516. Mîr ji dotmama xwe dikir û dil ketin hev û bi rastîya gotinê, Pêxemberê Xwedê şû kirin û daweta xwe hefteyekê li dar xistin û govend û dîlan bi kêf û
516. The mîr was in love with his cousin and they fell in love with each other and by the truth of the word, they married according to God's Prophet and held their wedding for a week and danced the govend and the dance with joy and

517. Şahî gerandin.
517. celebration.

518. Salek dido qedîyan tu zarok ji wan re çênebûn, rabû mîr berê xwe da mala Xwedê ji xwe re ji Xwedê bixwaze warê wî şîn bike li darê dinê.
518. A year or two finished, no children were born to them, the mîr got up and turned his direction to the House of God to ask for himself from God to make his estate green (flourish) in the world.

519. Mîr: Wele ev gotin û peyvên te bi min xweş tên, bêje bêje.
519. Mîr: By God these words and speeches of yours sound sweet to me, speak, speak.

520. Mela Itman: Ev çi çîrok e, ev çi vir e, ka derî veke ez herim malê.
520. Mela Itman: What story is this, what lie is this, come open the door, let me go home.

521. Mêvan: Na çênabe kes derkeve ji odeyê me bazara xwe bi mîr re kirîye.
521. Guest: No, it cannot be, no one leaves the room, we have made our bargain with the mîr.

522. Mîr: Na na guh nedîyê derî venabe û tu kes dernakeve, bêje bêje.
522. Mîr: No, no, pay no attention to him, the door does not open and no one goes out, speak, speak.

523. Mêvan: Rabû mîr karê xwe kir bi kerwanê hecacîya re û berî ku bi rê bikeve, civata şêwirdara li dar xist û îş û imûrê dewletê dan dest wan û îş û imûrê malbatê û kuşka jinê emanetî miftî û melê xwe yê ku lê bi ewle bû kir û jê re got: "Mela çavê te li malê be, li kulfet be ji te pê ve ez kesî ewlekar nabînim" û mîr berê xwe da oxirê û pişta xwe da felekê bi dilekî rihet û tesel.
523. Guest: The mîr got up, made his preparations with the pilgrims' caravan and before he set out on the road, he organized the council of advisors and gave the affairs and business of the state into their hands and entrusted the affairs and business of the family and the wife's palace to his mufti and mela whom he trusted, and said to him: "Mela, keep your eye on the house, on the household, apart from you I see no one trustworthy", and the mîr turned his direction to the journey and turned his back to fate with a rested and serene heart.

524. Erê mîrê min melê bêbext û telaqreş cadû û pîrê sêrbend bera mala jina mîr dan, rokê hefteyekê pîra sêrbend û cadûkar gelek zêr û pere ji mela xwaribû û sibê û êvarî dikire niqeniq li ser serê xatûna pepûk û dilê wê bi pîrê şewitî û ew xiste nav malê bi qerwaşî.
524. Yes my mîr, the treacherous and black-divorced mela released a sorceress and magic-working old woman onto the house of the mîr's wife; for a day, for a week the magic-working and sorceress old woman had eaten much gold and money from the mela and morning and evening she whined and nagged over the head of the poor xatûn, and her heart burned for the old woman and she put her inside the house in servitude.

525. Pîra bêbext jinik ji rê bir, û ew kişand avgermê serşoka pîrek û jina qene rojek înê xwe bişon û veşon.
525. The treacherous old woman led the woman astray, and drew her to the hot baths, the baths of females and women so that on a Friday they might wash and bathe themselves.

526. Mela Itman: Ev çi ye, ev çi çîrok e, ev çi vir in, ev çi derew in!
526. Mela Itman: What is this, what story is this, what lies are these, what falsehoods are these!

527. Mîr: Kuro tu dibêje qey ez rihet bûm law nema derek ji laşê min têşe, bêje mêvano bêje mirovo, çiqas gotinên te xweş in li canê min tên.
527. Mîr: Boy, you would say as if I have rested, boy, no place of my body hurts anymore, speak guest, speak man, how sweet your words are, they suit my soul.

528. Bû firtefirta qûna mela û nema erd digire û hema dibêje derî vekin bavo ez fetisîm bîna min çikîya, ez mirim ji bo Xwedê derî vekin ez bîna xwe derxim.
528. Fidgeting and squirming took hold of the mela's bottom and it no longer holds the ground and he just says open the door father, I am suffocating, my breath has dried up, I have died, for God's sake open the door so I can let my breath out.

529. Mêvan: Firtefirtê neke, derî ji kesî re venabe mercê min bi mîr re ye.
529. Guest: Do not fidget, the door does not open for anyone, my condition is with the mîr.

530. Mîr: Guh mede mela, ez derî venakim kuro te ez rihet kirim xwedêhişto tu yî hekîm û bijîjkê min Xwedê tu ji min re şandî.
530. Mîr: Pay no attention to the mela, I am not opening the door, boy, you have rested me, God-kept one, you are my doctor and physician, God sent you to me.

531. Û humîn û gumîn bi civatê ket her yek ji xwe re tiştekî dibêje, ev çi bûyer e, ev çi gosret e, ev çi kesanedîtî ye.
531. And murmuring and muttering fell upon the assembly, each says something to himself, what event is this, what astonishment is this, what unseen thing is this.

532. Mîr: De bêje mêvanê delal Xwedê alîkarê te be.
532. Mîr: Come speak, dear guest, may God be your helper.

533. Mêvan (Sînem): Erê mîrê min erê paşayê min de were li vê gosretê binere, li vê kesnedîyê, vê bêbextîyê.
533. Guest (Sînem): Yes my mîr, yes my pasha, come look at this astonishment, at this unseen thing, this treachery.

534. Piştî jinik (xatûn) kete avgerma serşokê bêbava pîra cadûkar ew tazî kir û serê wê kef kir, bi dizî derket û kilît da dest melê bêîman û bêwijdan.
534. After the woman (xatûn) entered the hot baths, the fatherless sorceress old woman undressed her and lathered her head, secretly went out and gave the key to the hand of the faithless and conscienceless mela.

535. Mela bi dizî kete serşokê û derî kilît kir û asê kir û cilê xwe ji xwe danîn û dest avête jinkê.
535. The mela secretly entered the bath and locked and secured the door and took off his clothes and laid his hand upon the woman.

536. Civat: Batil batil pek li vê kesnedîyê li vê bênamûsîyê.
536. Assembly: Void, void (false, false), alas at this unseen thing, at this dishonor.

537. Û humîn û gumîn careke din kete civatê de, hemû mane devjihev ji vê bûyer, gosret û bênamûsîyê.
537. And murmuring and muttering once again entered the assembly, they all remained open-mouthed from this event, astonishment, and dishonor.

538. Mela Itman: Ev çi bêbextî ye, ev çi rûreşî ye, ev çi derew in, ev çi çîrok e ku bextê mela û feqa reş dike?
538. Mela Itman: What treachery is this, what black-facedness is this, what lies are these, what story is this that blackens the fortune of melas and students?

539. ev bêbextî ne weleh ev giş derew û vir in.
539. this is treachery, by God this is all lies and falsehoods.

540. Kuro dergevan law derî veke ez fetisîm, ez mirim bîna min çikîya ye, dilê min lê dixe ji bo Xwedê derî vekin.
540. Boy, doorkeeper, boy, open the door, I am suffocating, I have died, my breath has dried up, my heart is pounding, for God's sake open the door.

541. Şêxo serê xwe bi ser hevalê xwe de xwar kir: Kuro Ûso ev bûyer wek bûyera mîrê me ye law.
541. Şêxo bowed his head over his friend: Boy, Ûso, this event is like our mîr's event, boy.

542. Ûso: Ha ha bira bê tu wilo nabêje û deng here mîr law ma Mela Itman wilo bêbext û telaqreş e, na na ne wilo ye.
542. Ûso: Ha ha, brother, you do not say so lest the sound go to the mîr, boy, is Mela Itman so treacherous and black-divorced, no, no, it is not like that.

543. Simo (devê xwe xist bin guhê Hiso de): Bi Xwedê ev serpêhatîya mîrê me û Mela Itman e ma tu li mela nanêre kuro bê çi firtefirt lê ketîye û qûna wî erd nagire hema dibêje derî vekin dixwaze bireve ma kes wek wî bê wijdan hene.
543. Simo (put his mouth under Hiso's ear): By God this is the adventure of our mîr and Mela Itman, do you not look at the mela, boy, see what fidgeting has fallen upon him and his bottom does not hold the ground, he just says open the door, he wants to run away, is there anyone without conscience like him.

544. lawo Hiso ji cergê go mîr nexweş ketîye û fermanî ketîye destê mela ma tu li halê me û belengazîya me nanere, kes nema dikare parî k
544. boy, Hiso, from the liver (from the core), since the mîr fell sick and the command fell into the mela's hand, do you not look at our state and our destitution, no one can anymore eat a piece

545. nên bixwe lawo em nema diwêrin gilî û gazinan ji hev re bikin.
545. of bread, boy, we no longer dare to make complaints and grievances to each other.

546. Hiso: Hema bi Xwedê rast e, ev bûyera mîrê me ye kuro ma tu nabêje ka xatûna me Sînem mane ji wê çaxê de wenda ye.
546. Hiso: Just by God it is true, this is our mîr's event, boy, why do you not say where is our xatûn Sînem, after all she has been missing since that time.

547. Bekiro: Wey pek û hezar carî pek ev çi çîrok e lawo kesî tiştê wilo nedîtine û yê min bi xwe min nebihîstîye jî ev pîsîtî û bênamûsî ji van mela tê, bi Xwedê dilê min lê xera dibû ku ev mela tolaz e.
547. Bekiro: Woe, alas, and a thousand times alas, what story is this, boy, no one has seen such a thing and as for me myself, I have not even heard of it, this filth and dishonor coming from these melas, by God my heart was spoiled for him (I suspected him), that this mela is a scoundrel.

548. Birahîm: Lawo kuro de xwe ragirin bê ka dawî çi çêdibe ev çîrok ne bela sebeb e û ev mêvan ne hindik e, û dengê wî zirav e tu dibêjî qey jineke, pîrekeke lawo.
548. Birahîm: Boy, boy, come hold yourselves to see what happens at the end, this story is not without reason and this guest is not little (insignificant), and his voice is thin, you would say as if he is a woman, a female, boy.

549. Mela Silêman: De na lo ez vî tiştî tu car bawer nakim çawa mela û Quranxwendî û oldar û xêr û guneha zane wê rabe ew bi xwe vê bênamûsîyê bike!
549. Mela Silêman: Come no, man, I never believe this thing, how could a mela and Quran-reader and religious man who knows good deeds and sins get up and do this dishonor himself!

550. mane agirê dojehê heye.
550. after all there is the fire of hell.

551. Mela Hesen: Wele heger ev rast be heqê wî melayî xazoq e.
551. Mela Hesen: By God, if this is true, that mela's right (due) is the impaling stake.

552. Mela Itman: Lawo ji bo Xwedê derî vekin ez peqîm, ez mirim bîna min teng e kuro çawa li vî mêvanî guhdar dikin mirtib e, qereçî ye kes nizane bezê bin guhê bavê wî ji ku ye.
552. Mela Itman: Boy, for God's sake open the door, I have burst, I have died, my breath is tight, boy, how are you listening to this guest, he is a gypsy, he is a vagabond, no one knows where the fat under his father's ear is from (where he comes from).

553. Bê çi zane derew, vir û bêbextîyan li hev bîne û bike çîrok, de sîlekê li bin guhê wî xin berdinê ji civatê, ma qeşmerê wilo yê ku mero lê guhdarî bike.
553. See how he knows to bring lies, falsehoods, and treachery together and make a story; come, strike a slap under his ear and release him from the assembly, is such a clown one that a man should listen to?

554. ev çi qeşmer e ku li ser mela û olan bêbextî û derwan dike, ma mela û feqa û zilamê oldar yên devê te ne kurooooo?!
554. what clown is this who makes treachery and lies about melas and religions, are melas and students and religious men for your mouth, booooy?!

555. Bi navê Xwedê yê şêrîn ku mîr ne rûniştî ba û ne civata wî ba niha min yê sîlak di çapa devê te de lê xistaya û dest û nigê te girê daba û biavêta binê zindanê.
555. By the sweet name of God, if the mîr were not seated and it were not his assembly, right now I would have struck a slap across the measure of your mouth and tied your hands and feet and thrown you to the bottom of the prison.

556. Tu li devê wî binêre kuro bê çi zane derew û bêbextîyan li hev siwar bike.
556. You look at his mouth, boy, see how he knows to mount lies and treachery upon each other.

557. Mîr: Bîna xwe fireh bike seyda tu çima wilo xwe diqeherîne mêrik çîrokekê ji me re dibêje û ne ji welatê me ye, bi Xwedê ez bi gotinên wî rehet dibim.
557. Mîr: Widen your breath (be patient) master, why are you angering yourself so, the man is telling us a story and he is not from our country, by God I rest with his words.

558. Mela Itman: Mîrê min ev mêvan zimandirêj e û xwedênenas e, çawa dev diavêje kesê dîndar û ewlîyayên Xwedê ev mêvanekî milhide, gawir e, kuştina wî helal e gelek nigê xwe
558. Mela Itman: My mîr, this guest is long-tongued and ignorant of God, how he throws his mouth at (insults) religious people and God's saints, this guest is an apostate, he is an infidel, his killing is lawful, he extends his foot greatly

559. radide û destê xwe dirêj dike ji sînorê edebê derbas bûye, çênabe em lê guhdarî biki,n em ê pê re gunehkar bibin, mîrê min heya rûnîştina pê re nedurist e.
559. and stretches his hand out (oversteps bounds), he has passed the border of decency, it cannot be that we listen to him, we will become sinners with him, my mîr, even sitting with him is not right.
