560. Mîr: Xem nake seyda bîna xwe fireh bike mêvanê me ye û divê em miqatebûnê bidênê, bila çi kes be li ser çi dînî be şeveke û wê Xwedê derbas bike.
560. Mîr: No matter, master, widen your breath, he is our guest and we must give him care, whoever he may be, whatever religion he is on, it is one night and God will pass it.

561. Civat qerebalix e.
561. The assembly is crowded (noisy).

562. Her yek ji xwe re tiştekî dibêje.
562. Each says something to himself.

563. Civat gêjo mêjo bûye hin dibêjin qey bira ev mela wilo bêwijdan in û hin dibêjin na lo çima çawa bû wê çilo mela vî gunehê mezin bike, û hin dibêjin min digot wele çima mela wilo rêya xwe şayîk dikin û cibê xwe witî dikin û şaşka xwe spî û mezin dikin.
563. The assembly has become dizzy and confused, some say perhaps, brother, these melas are so conscienceless, and some say no man, why, how could it be, how would a mela commit this great sin, and some say I was saying, by God, why do melas smooth their path like that and iron their cloaks and make their turbans white and large.

564. Di wê navê re mîr destê xwe hilda, civat ker bû deng û pêjin ji civatê bilîya, her yek di cihê xwe de ma rûniştî bêdeng, çawa ziq li mîr dinerin.
564. In the meantime the mîr raised his hand, the assembly became deaf (silent), sound and noise disappeared from the assembly, each remained sitting silently in his place, staring fixedly at the mîr.

565. Mêvan di ber xwe de bi dizî dikene û li mela dinere û ew jî maye li hêvîya mîr e ku destûrê bidê û çîroka xwe bi dawî bike.
565. The guest laughs secretly to himself and looks at the mela, and he too has remained waiting for the mîr to give him permission to finish his story.

566. Qederekî civat ma mest û bêdeng tu dibê qey kes li dîwanê tune ye û her yek şaş û gêj maye ji xwe re diponijin bê ka wê dawî çilo be.
566. For a time the assembly remained stunned and silent, you would say as if no one is in the court, and each remained astonished and dizzy, pondering to themselves how the end will be.

567. Mîr (berê xwe da mêvanê xwe): Fermo mêvanê delal serpêhatîya xwe bibêje hêdî hêdî û bi bînfirehî çiqas bi min xweş tê.
567. Mîr (turned his direction to his guest): If you please, dear guest, tell your adventure slowly and with wide breath (calmly), how sweet it sounds to me.

568. Mêvan (Sînem): Belê mîrê min ma ez ê çi bibêjim û çi nebêjim pepûka jinkê di teştê de rûniştî bû, serî, rû û çav bi kefa sabûnê bû ji wê werê ku pîra wê ye dest avêt lûfik û pişta jinkê firkand û hino hino dest dirêjî bedenê wê kir.
568. Guest (Sînem): Yes my mîr, what shall I say and what shall I not say, the poor woman was sitting in the basin, her head, face and eyes were with the foam of soap, from her assumption that it is her old woman, he grabbed the loofah and scrubbed the woman's back and little by little stretched his hand to her body.

569. Jinik veciniqî û av bi ser serê xwe û rûyê xwe de kir dît ku çi zebenî li hember e.
569. The woman jolted and poured water over her head and her face, she saw what a demon is opposite her.

570. Civat careke din humîn û gumîn pê ket ji gosretî, bêşermdarî û bênamûsîyê, û her yek di ber xwe de dibêje, 2pek pek ev tişt jî li dinyayê heye rûyê yekî dikeve binê nigê wî ji şerm û fedîya".
570. The assembly once again fell into murmuring and muttering from the astonishment, shamelessness and dishonor, and each says to himself, "alas, alas, this thing too exists in the world, one's face falls under his foot from shame and embarrassment".

571. Mîr careke din destê xwe hilda civat sekinî berê xwe da mêvan û got: "Bibêje bibêje bê ka li dawî çi heye".
571. The mîr once again raised his hand, the assembly stopped, he turned his direction to the guest and said: "Speak, speak, to see what is at the end".

572. Mêvan: Ma ez ê çi bibêjim mîrê min devê min nagere vê bênamûsîyê bînim ser zimanê xwe lê ez ê bibêjim qene tu nas bike bê çiqas bêbextî û telaqreşî li vê dinyayê hene û qîzê bava bextreş dibin bi bêbav û bêbexta re.
572. Guest: What shall I say, my mîr, my mouth does not move to bring this dishonor onto my tongue, but I will speak so that you may know how much treachery and black-divorce there are in this world, and daughters of fathers (noble girls) become black-fortuned with the fatherless and the treacherous.

573. Û pepûkê jina çi bibêjin kes ji wan bawer nake darê şikestî ne û tas hat û çinginî wê deh bêjin rast e heya yek bêje derew e.
573. And the poor women, whatever they say no one believes them, they are broken sticks; and the bowl came and clinked, ten will say it is true while one says it is a lie.

574. Mîrê min pepûka jinkê ma behetî û di cih de hişk bû ji fedîya nema zane wê çawa xwe binixumîne hema pepûkê ji neçarî porê xwe bi ser laşê xwe de berda.
574. My mîr, the poor woman remained astounded and froze in place from embarrassment, she no longer knows how she will cover herself, the poor thing out of necessity just let her hair down over her body.

575. Civat: Batil batil ev çi bênamûsî ye kes li jina xwe wilo nake ev çi zebenî ye bavo ma kesê wilo li dinyê hene kafir jî wilo nakin.
575. Assembly: Void, void, what dishonor is this, no one does this to his wife, what demon is this, father, are there such people in the world, even infidels do not do so.

576. Mela cardî qûna xwe li erdê xist û di ber xwe de digit, "ev çi çîrok e, ev çi gotin in", û diricifî ji hêrs û tirsa û kef bi deva ket, bi ser riha wek melkesekê de dipijiqî û mela nema zanîbû.
576. The mela again hit his bottom on the ground and was saying to himself, "what story is this, what words are these", and he trembled from anger and fear and foam fell to his mouth, splattering over his beard like a broom, and the mela no longer knew (what to do).

577. Bi desta riha xwe rast dikir.
577. With his hands he straightened his beard.

578. Simo: Kuro ji yê tenista xwe re, tu dibê qey li qûna mela rast e ma tu lê nanere?
578. Simo: Boy, to the one beside him, you would say as if it is true upon the mela's bottom (he is guilty), do you not look at him?

579. Silo: Na na xuya ye lê rast e mêrik ne qûnşil ba wilo nedikir.
579. Silo: No, no, it is visible it is true upon him, if the man were not wet-bottomed (guilty) he would not act so.

580. Sîmo: erê birak ava hêdî mi hecêb (gosret) jê dît, wek marê bin kayê ye tiştê me nebihîstibû jî me bihîst û dît.
580. Simo: Yes brother, wow now I have seen astonishment from him, he is like a snake under the straw, what we had not even heard we have heard and seen.

581. talîya dinyayê ye law çawa miftîyê dewletê melê dozdehilm û bawermendê mîr rabe vî tiştî bike, çilo li xwe datîne ku dakeve vê rezaletê, qey ev dîn bûbû law?
581. It is the end of the world, boy, how could the state mufti, the mela of twelve sciences and the mîr's trusted one, get up and do this thing, how does he put it upon himself to descend to this disgrace, had he gone mad, boy?

582. Dînê biçolaketî wilo nakin.
582. The madmen fallen to the wilderness do not do so.

583. Hovo: Hûûû... ev bele ye bele ye, mela ye bi şaşik û tirme ye, melakî bêewle ye.
583. Hovo: Hooo... this is a trouble, it is a trouble, he is a mela with a turban and shroud (cloak), he is an untrustworthy mela.

584. Mîr careke din destê xwe hilda, civat rawetîya, deng ji odeyê bilîya.
584. The mîr once again raised his hand, the assembly stopped, sound disappeared from the room.

585. Mîr li xwe dinere laşê wî bê çi sivik bûye dikare rabe ser xwe û bimeşe di dilê xwe de got: "Xwedê îşev ev mêvan û
585. The mîr looks at himself, see how light his body has become, he can stand up and walk; in his heart he said: "Tonight God has sent this guest and

586. Hekîmê Luqman ji min re şandîye", li civatê nerî bê civat ketîye çi hêlekanê her yek bi xwe re dipeyive, li Mela Itman nerî kesmê wî, lebta wî, çavên wî zerdoq mane û diçirisîn, riha wî ketîye devê wî gêjo mêjo bûye, dilê mîr lê xera bû ku melê wî qûnşil e û belak wî heye.
586. Luqman the Physician to me", he looked at the assembly, see what rocking the assembly has fallen into, each talks to himself, he looked at Mela Itman, his figure, his movement, his eyes have remained yellowish and were glittering, his beard has fallen into his mouth, he has become dizzy and confused, the mîr's heart spoiled for him (he suspected him) that his mela is wet-bottomed (guilty) and has a trouble (is hiding something).

587. Berê xwe da mêvan, nerî mêvan dibin simbêlan re dikene û rûgeş e.
587. He turned his direction to the guest, saw the guest laughs from under his mustaches and is bright-faced.

588. Mîr: Bêje mêvanê delal bêje bê ka talî çi heye, û çilo çêbû?
588. Mîr: Speak, dear guest, speak to see what is at the end, and how did it happen?

589. Mêvan (Sînem): Erê mîrê min ma piştî vê bûyerê, vê qebhetê ez ê çi bibêjim.
589. Guest (Sînem): Yes my mîr, after this event, this fault, what shall I say.

590. pepûka jinkê ma gosretmayî, şaş ma û devê wê ji tirsa ji şerm û fedîya şikest.
590. the poor woman remained astounded, she remained astonished and her mouth broke (she was speechless) from fear, from shame and embarrassment.

591. Û bi zorê devê wê gerîya û got: "Mela ez di bextê te û Xwedê de tê min nehetikîne derkeve derve.
591. And with difficulty her mouth moved and she said: "Mela, I am in your fortune and God's (I implore you), you will not disgrace me, go outside.

592. Xwedê di orta min û te de be ez li te mikur nayêm heya mirinê ne min tu dît û ne te ez dîtim vegere û derkeve hê tiştek çênebûye û kesî em nedîtine ji Xwedê pê ve".
592. May God be between me and you, I will not confess against you until death, neither I saw you nor you saw me, turn back and go out while nothing has yet happened and no one has seen us except for God".

593. Melê bêbext lê vegerand û got: "Ev wiqas sal û meh çavên min li dû te bû ku derfetek ji min re were û ez te bigirim û zeft bikim ma Xwedê bi xwe te ji destê min xelas nake", û jinik bi hêrs û himet kişand ber sînga xwe.
593. The treacherous mela returned to her and said: "For these many years and months my eyes have been after you for an opportunity to come to me and for me to catch and seize you, even God Himself does not save you from my hand", and with anger and force he pulled the woman to his chest.

594. Civat: Hooo... Ya Rebî star ev gosret û bêşermî û bênamûsî ye, batil batil li vê bênamûsîyê, li vê gosreta kesnedî, hewar e ji bo Xwedê ev jî heye?
594. Assembly: Hooo... O Lord protect, this is astonishment and shamelessness and dishonor, void, void at this dishonor, at this unseen astonishment, it is a cry for help for God's sake, does this too exist?

595. Û careke din bû vinevina civatê devjihevî mane, nema zanin wê çi bibêjin ji fedîya û tirsa ji Xwedê şaş û gêj mane.
595. And once again it became the buzzing of the assembly, they have remained open-mouthed, they no longer know what they will say from embarrassment and fear of God, they have remained astonished and dizzy.

596. Û her mela kef bi ser dev û rîyê ketî ye û xwe li erdê dixîne, û dibêje, "bo Xwedê derî vekin ez fetisîm min derxînin derve, ay ez mirim, ay ez mirim".
596. And the mela, foam has fallen over his mouth and face and he hits himself on the ground, and says, "for God's sake open the door, I am suffocating, take me outside, oh I am dead, oh I am dead".

597. Şemsedîn: Yabo bi Xwedê qûna mela şil e, ma hûn lê nanerin bê çi kêferatê dike ku ne zinêkar ba, ev helebel nedikir, wê ew jî wek va melê din û kesê civatê wê guhdar ba bêdeng û rûniştîba bê lebt û leq.
597. Şemsedîn: Father, by God the mela's bottom is wet (he is guilty), do you not look at him to see what struggling he makes, if he were not an adulterer, he would not make this uproar, he too would have been like these other melas and people of the assembly, he would have been listening silently and sitting without movement and stirring.

598. Xuya ye ev tep û rîp giş yê wî ne qey bala we ne lê ye?
598. It is visible these tricks and traps are all his, is your attention not on him?

599. Şerfedîn: Xwedê kesî şaş neke, ya Rebî tu me bistirîne, ev mirov hay jê nîne.
599. Şerfedîn: May God not mislead anyone, O Lord, shelter us, this man has no awareness of it (is oblivious to consequence).

600. Hovo: Xwe bistirînin yabo ma xwe ne kesî bi destê we girtîye û zor li we kirîye, tu xwe biparêze wê Xwedê te bistirîne, tu xwe neparêze ji xwe tê bihetike, berê hatîye gotin.
600. Hovo: Shelter yourselves, father, after all no one has taken you by your hand and forced you, you protect yourself, God will shelter you; you do not protect yourself, you will disgrace yourself anyway, it was said before.

601. Ya Rebî tu me şaş neke, ku em şaş bûn tu me berokaş neke.
601. O Lord do not mislead us, if we were misled, do not let us roll down the slope.

602. Feqe Hesen: Ev e heyran ev e wilo ye, golaka dikeve kêr lê pir dibin.
602. Feqe Hesen: This is it, beloved, this is how it is, when the calf falls, the knives upon it become many.

603. Mîr dest hilda, civat sekinî, deng qut bû her yek di cihê xwe de bêpêjin bû û got: "De bibêje mêvanê delal, bi Xwedê çîroka te bi serê xwe ye ku ne rast ba laşê min hewqas sivik nedibû û êş û nexweşî hêdî hêdî ji canê min dernediket, de bibêje".
603. The mîr raised a hand, the assembly stopped, sound was cut, each became noiseless in his place and he said: "Come speak, dear guest, by God your story is unique; if it were not true my body would not have become so light and pain and sickness would not slowly leave my soul, come speak".

604. Mêvan: Erê mîrê min Xwedê nehêle ji gelac, cadûkar û bêbextan re, ma pepûka jinkê wê çi bike, pîreke bêhimet e û ketîye nav lepê yekî wek qantirekî çavsor û têrceh, hema bi jinkê ve radipelike.
604. Guest: Yes my mîr, may God not leave it to the gossips, sorcerers, and treacherous ones; what will the poor woman do, she is a powerless female and she has fallen into the hands of one like a red-eyed and barley-fed mule, he just clings to the woman.

605. Jinkê nas kir ku filitandina wê tune ye, û ne bi fen û hîla be xelas nabe, rabû jinkê dev ji zor û destlepkê berda, û bi fen û xapan kir û got: "Seyda ez gorî, ev tu ji dil û can evîndarê min î, ez ê sedê weke min kevnejinê dikim bi gorî şindolê serê te, min digot qey tu henekan dikî, de ka hilî min berde ez xwe ji vê kef û sabûnê bişom û serê te û laşê te bi destê xwe bifirkînim û dûre em ê kêfa xwe bikin.
605. The woman realized that she has no escape, and if not by trickery and guile she will not be saved; the woman got up, gave up on force and bare hands, and started with tricks and deceits and said: "Master, I am your sacrifice, since you are my lover from heart and soul, I make a hundred old women like me a sacrifice for your head (for you), I thought perhaps you were joking; come on, get up, let me go so I can wash myself of this foam and soap, and I will scrub your head and your body with my own hand, and then we will have our fun.

606. Ma çi li dû me heye?"
606. After all, what is chasing us?"

607. Piştî van gotina, melê min û te zewrê wî sist bûn û xwe bi destê jinkê ve berda.
607. After these words, the mela of mine and yours, his grip loosened and he surrendered himself to the woman's hand.

608. Jinkê jî nemerdî nekir, zû zû ew xiste serşokê û serê wî û riha wî qenc kef kir û rahişte tasa hindo û heya Xwedê huner dayê û ji kel tas hilda û go req li nîvê serê mele da.
608. The woman too was not ungenerous (did not hesitate), quickly quickly she put him in the bath and lathered his head and his beard thoroughly, and grabbed the Indian bowl and with whatever skill God gave her she raised the bowl from the boil (with full force) and hit it crack in the middle of the mela's head.

609. Civat humîn û gumîn pê ket, û qêrîn û barîn bi hinekan ket ji lerza.
609. The assembly fell into murmuring and muttering, and shouting and crying fell upon some from trembling.

610. Silo: Wey tu dêya min be lê, ma ka jinê wek te?
610. Silo: Woe, may you be my mother, well, where are women like you?

611. Simo: Jin jî hene û jinkok jî hene.
611. Simo: There are women and there are mere females.

612. Şemo: Şêr şêr e çi jine çi mêr e.
612. Şemo: A lion is a lion, whether it is a woman or a man.

613. Seyfedino: Wele qenc kir, ma jinê xelkê ji te re berdayî ne kuro?
613. Seyfedino: By God she did well, are the people's women let loose for you, boy?

614. Hovo: Ma ka jinê wilo li ku hene?
614. Hovo: Well, where are such women?

615. Şerfedîn: Qîzê bava pir in, qîzê camêra ji dunya yê naqelin, jineke binamus hêjaye sed mêrê bênamûs.
615. Şerfedîn: The daughters of fathers are many, the daughters of brave men do not end from the world, a woman with honor is worth a hundred men without honor.

616. Sino: Namûsa xelkê buha ye ne ji her kesî re berdayî ye.
616. Sino: The honor of the people is expensive, it is not let loose for everyone.

617. Mela Itman: Law ji bo Xwedê ez mirim kuro, hûn giş li va derewa guhdar dikin û ji vî sewterî bawer dikin!
617. Mela Itman: Boy, for God's sake I have died, boy, you all listen to these lies and believe this fool!

618. Feqe Hesen: Wey li vê gosretê li vê hetîketîyê, li vê bûyera kesnedî ye.
618. Feqe Hesen: Woe at this astonishment, at this disgrace, at this unseen event.

619. Silêmano: Law de hêdî, de ka rawestin bê dûre çi çêbû mela mir, ma?
619. Silêmano: Boy, come slowly, come wait to see what happened afterwards, did the mela die?

620. Sofi Elî: Wey îşele bimire û ranebe, ma teresê wilo ji çire ne?
620. Sofi Elî: Woe, God willing he dies and does not rise, what are such scoundrels for anyway?

621. Mehmûdo: Xwedê zane bê ew zarokên ji te bikevin bê wê çi şêr bin (jina hêja).
621. Mehmûdo: God knows the children that fall from you, what lions they will be (worthy woman).

622. Mîr carek din destê xwe hilda, civat sekinî, deng ji wan bilîya, berê xwe da mêvanê xwe û got: “Ka bibêje mêvanê delal, te îşev dîwan hejand û civat şaş û gêj kir, ev çi serpêhatî ye?
622. The mîr once again raised his hand, the assembly stopped, sound disappeared from them, he turned his direction to his guest and said: "Come speak, dear guest, tonight you shook the court and made the assembly astonished and dizzy, what adventure is this?

623. Tiştê wilo jî li dunyayê hene û em pê nizanin de ka bibêje ka bibêje".
623. Such things too exist in the world and we do not know of them, come speak, come speak".

624. Mêvan (Sînem): Erê mîrê min û ji wilo xerabtir jî heye.
624. Guest (Sînem): Yes my mîr, and there is even worse than that.

625. Mîr: De ka dawîyê ji me re bibêje, bê mela mir, ma? çi pê hat?
625. Mîr: Come tell us the end, did the mela die? what happened to him?

626. Mêvan: Na na nemir ma kengî ê wilo dimirin wek pisîka bi heft rihan e.
626. Guest: No, no, he did not die, when do such ones die, he is like a cat with seven lives.

627. Mîrê min piştî mela ket û di nav xûnê de vegevizî, jinka reben rabû kilît ji bêrîka wî derxist, derî vekir û bi lez û bazdan revîya çû malê û derî giş li xwe girtin nehişt kes bi ser bikeve ne ji navmalîya, ne ji cêrîyan, û ma bi şev û roj digirî li ser bextê xwe yê reş.
627. My mîr, after the mela fell and wallowed in blood, the wretched woman got up, took the key out of his pocket, opened the door and with speed and running fled, went home and closed all the doors on herself, did not let anyone discover her, neither from the household nor from the maids, and remained crying by night and day over her black fortune.

628. Mîr: Ê û ka vî bêbavê mela çi kir piştî rabû, û bi ku de çû?
628. Mîr: And so what did this fatherless mela do after he got up, and where did he go?

629. Mêvan: Bêbexto dest bi bêbextî û derew û viran kir û name li ser namê ji mêrê wê re dişand û digot: "Jina te bûye qehp, yarikê wê bi şev û bi roj li civata wê ne, pêxwas in.
629. Guest: The treacherous one started with treachery and lies and falsehoods and sent letter upon letter to her husband and was saying: "Your wife has become a whore, her paramours are in her assembly by night and by day, they are barefoot.

630. Çete û keleşên Misrê her şev mêvanê wê ne heya mêrê jinkê hat mela serê wî tije kir, û bêyî ku bersiva jina xwe bide berdayê ji şar û bajarê Misrê, û ev heft salê min, pepûkê min qijokê li çol û pola zikekî têr û diwazdê birçî, bi hêsêrî, bi qerwaşî, bi jar û belengazî îyarê berxa li xwe kiribû ji bo kes wê nas neke ku jin e, û niha va ez li civata we rûniştî me û heger hûn bawer nakin rabin şaşika Mela Itman ji ser serê wî hilînin hûn ê şûna tasa hindo di serê wî de bibînin, û bi çavên serê xwe bibînin û nas bikin bê Mela Itman çi bêbextî û çi telaqreşî anîn serê min.
630. The bandits and rogues of Egypt are her guests every night, until the woman's husband came, the mela filled his head, and without giving his wife an answer, he dismissed her from the province and city of Egypt, and for these seven years of mine, poor me, wailing me in the wilderness and deserts, one belly full and twelve hungry, with captivity, with servitude, with misery and destitution, I had put the hide of lambs on myself so that no one would recognize her (me) as a woman, and now here I am sitting in your assembly, and if you do not believe, get up, lift Mela Itman's turban from his head, you will see the mark of the Indian bowl in his head, and see with the eyes of your head and recognize what treachery and what black-divorce Mela Itman brought upon my head.

631. Civat: Hela hela, hewar hewar, pek li vê ecêbê li vê gosretê çi melakî bênamûs, kuro rabin wî girê din, wî bikujin, wî daşilqandî bikin wî li xazoqê bixînin.
631. Assembly: Oh oh, help help, alas at this wonder, at this astonishment, what a dishonorable mela; boy, get up, tie him up, kill him, mangle him, put him on the impaling stake.

632. wey li vê gosret û kesnedî yê!
632. woe at this astonishment and unseen thing!

633. Hema çend xort rabûn mela girtin û şaşik ji serî hilanîn, dîtin bê heydê çi newal û birîn di serê wî de ye, mela avêtin nav niga û bi kulm pehîna pê ketin, û kula wî di dilê gelekan de bû û gelek jê didexisîn û diqeherîn û kêfa gelekan li hat û dikenîyan û digotin, "bera wilo li vî teresî bê milet xistibû helakê".
633. Immediately a few youths got up, grabbed the mela and lifted the turban from his head, they saw, wow, what a valley and wound is in his head; they threw the mela among the feet and fell upon him with fists and kicks, and the pain of him was in the hearts of many and many were jealous of him and angry with him, and the joy of many came and they were laughing and saying, "let it be so for this scoundrel, he had put the nation into ruin".

634. Mîr careke din destê xwe hilda, û civat rawestîya, mîr rabû li ser doşeka xwe rûnişt û ferman da, "Mela Itman bi werîsa girê din û bi zincîra qeyd û bend û kilît bikin û bavêjin binê zindanê, heya sibê bê civat û şêwirdar çi dibêjin.
634. The mîr once again raised his hand, and the assembly stopped; the mîr got up, sat on his mattress and gave the order, "Tie Mela Itman with ropes and fetter and bind and lock him with chains and throw him to the bottom of the prison, until tomorrow to see what the assembly and advisors say.

635. Sê çar xorta mela girê dan bi zincîra û avêtin binê zindanê.
635. Three or four youths tied the mela with chains and threw him to the bottom of the prison.

636. Mîr deng li civatê kir û got: "Gelî dost û heval û gundî û şêrîyara!
636. The mîr called to the assembly and said: "O friends and companions and villagers and nobles!

637. Şev li me bû nîvê şevê hindik maye ro hilê, me gişa nas kir serpêhatîya Sînem û melê bêbext.
637. Night upon us has become midnight, little remains for the sun to rise, we all recognized the adventure of Sînem and the treacherous mela.

638. Ev heft salê min li erdê nexweşê li ser derzîya piştê û dotmama min ji neçarî û ji tirsa bêbextîyê bi çol û pola ketîye, bi qerwaşî, bi erzanî, bi
638. These seven years of mine on the ground, a sick man on the needle of the back (flat on my back), and my cousin out of necessity and from fear of treachery has fallen to the wilderness and deserts, with servitude, with cheapness, with

639. dînîtî çerm û îyarê pez li xwe kirîye qene kes pê guman nekeve û bêolên weke mela pir in li darê dinê.
639. madness she had put the skin and hide of sheep on herself so that no one falls into suspicion of her, and those without religion like the mela are many in the world.

640. De rabin gelî mirovan herin malê xwe û vê bûyerê bînin ber çavên xwe, û pepûka Sînem ev heft salê wê qedyane têr nebûye ji xewa şêrîn timî bi tirs û dil bi kul û xemgînî xilmaş dibû.
640. Come get up, O people, go to your homes and bring this event before your eyes, and poor Sînem, these seven years of hers have finished, she has not been satisfied with sweet sleep, always with fear and a heart with pain and sorrow she would doze off.

641. Civat bela bû her yek çûn mala xwe û Sînem û Mîr Mamed mane şîyar heya sibê gilî û gazinên xwe ji hev re dikirin.
641. The assembly dispersed, each went to their home and Sînem and Mîr Mamed remained awake until morning, making their complaints and grievances to each other.

642. ## Gotinên Li Malan
642. ## Words At The Homes

643. Zeyneb: Tu heya niha li ku bû Simo, ma tu natirse ji diza, ji çeta ku têkevin mala me?
643. Zeyneb: Where were you until now, Simo, do you not fear thieves, bandits that they might enter our house?

644. Simo: Hûû... Zeynebê, tiştê îşev me dîtin tu kesî hê nedîye û nebihistîye.
644. Simo: Hooo... Zeyneb, the things we saw tonight no one has yet seen or heard.

645. Zeyneb: Pepû Simo çi bû, çi çêbû?
645. Zeyneb: Poor Simo, what was it, what happened?

646. Simo jêr bûyer bi ta û derzîyê vekir.
646. Simo unfolded the event to her with thread and needle.

647. Zeyneb: Pepû pepû talîya dinyê ye, kuro ev tişt û Mela Itman.
647. Zeyneb: Alas, alas, it is the end of the world, boy, this thing and Mela Itman.

648. É û ka mîr çikir ji mela, ew kuşt, ew hişt, çi kir jê?
648. And so what did the mîr do to the mela, did he kill him, did he leave him, what did he do to him?

649. Simo: Hîn tu li ku ye keçê sibê wê dadgehê li dar xin û bê ka wê çi bikin jê.
649. Simo: Where are you still (you have seen nothing yet), girl, tomorrow they will hold court and see what they will do to him.

650. Li maleke din.
650. At another house.

651. Silo hêdî derî vekir û kete hundir li reşê.
651. Silo slowly opened the door and entered inside in the dark.

652. Fatê (jina wî): Pepû ev kî ye, kuro tu diz î, tu kî yî?
652. Fatê (his wife): Poor me, who is this, boy, are you a thief, who are you?

653. Silo: Keçê ez im, ez netirs, ez Silo me.
653. Silo: Girl, it is me, do not fear, I am Silo.

654. Fatê: Pepû Silo, heya niha tu li ku bûyî, çima tu wilo dimîne derengî şevê û tu min jina ciwan bi tenê dihêle, ma tu nizanî sîpe û tolaz li çarçîya digerin?
654. Fatê: Poor Silo, where were you until now, why do you remain so late in the night and leave me, a young woman, alone, do you not know rascals and scoundrels roam the markets?

655. Silo: Ha hew fatê, tu nizanî bê îşev çi çêbû li odeya mîr.
655. Silo: Just stop Fatê, you do not know what happened tonight in the mîr's room.

656. Fatê: Pepú Silo, çi çêbû hinka hev kuştin, hinka hev revandin, çi bû?
656. Fatê: Poor Silo, what happened, did some kill each other, did some kidnap each other, what was it?

657. Silo: Na na ne kuştin û ne revandin.
657. Silo: No, no, neither killing nor kidnapping.

658. û jê re bûyer bi ta û derzîyê vekir.
658. and he unfolded the event to her with thread and needle.

659. Fatê: Ê pepûko Silo, û Sînem Xatûn vegerîya malê?
659. Fatê: Ah, poor Silo, and did Sînem Xatûn return home?

660. weyla tu dê û xweha min be, ê û çi kirin ji wî teresê mela, ne kuştin?
660. woe, may you be my mother and sister, and so what did they do to that scoundrel mela, did they not kill him?

661. Silo: Na na sibehê wê wî li dadegehê gunehkar bikin û li qazoxê bixînin.
661. Silo: No, no, tomorrow they will find him guilty in court and put him on the impaling stake.

662. Li maleke din.
662. At another house.

663. Feqe Hesen derî vekir û kete hundir û hema dibê ya star, ya star li vê ecêbê.
663. Feqe Hesen opened the door and entered inside and just says O Protector, O Protector at this wonder.

664. Eyşê (jina wî): Pepû Feqe Hesen, çi bi te hatîye, qey tu dîn bûye kuro, star stara te ye?
664. Eyşê (his wife): Poor Feqe Hesen, what has happened to you, have you gone mad boy, is this 'protector, protector' yours?

665. Feqe Hesen: Rebenê Eyşê tu rabe rab, tu biner li vê bênamûsîyê, em oldar û dîndar nema karin serê xwe hildin li nav xelkê, çavên me nema bar dibe.
665. Feqe Hesen: Wretched Eyşê, you get up, get up, you look at this dishonor, we religious and faithful men can no longer raise our heads among the people, our eyes can no longer bear it.

666. Û bûyer jê re dûr û dirêj kir ji pêşî heya dawî, û hema Eyşê di be re dibêje, "pepû pepû, li min rebenê, li min kezîkurê, ev tişt jî li dinyayê hene!"
666. And he made the event far and long (told it in detail) for her from beginning to end, and Eyşê just says to herself, "alas, alas, woe to wretched me, woe to short-braided me, these things too exist in the world!"

667. Li maleke din
667. At another house

668. Seyfedîn kete hundir û rahişt misînê destnimêjê ku destmêj bigire.
668. Seyfedîn entered inside and grabbed the ablution pitcher to perform ablution.

669. Jinik pê şîyar bû.
669. The woman woke up from him.

670. Perîşanê: Pepû kuro tu kî yî?
670. Perîşanê: Poor me, boy, who are you?

671. Seyfedîn ev tu ye?
671. Seyfedîn, is this you?

672. piştî çavên xwe vekir,
672. after she opened her eyes,

673. Ev heya niha tu li kû bû kuro, qey tu fedî nakî ji bavê xwe heya nîvê şevê li tolazîya digere?
673. Where were you until now, boy, are you not embarrassed before your father roaming in vagabondage until midnight?

674. Seyfedîn: Keçê perîşanê, ez li odeya mîr bûm, û ev çi lewlewa te ye?
674. Seyfedîn: Girl Perîşanê, I was in the mîr's room, and what is this blabbering of yours?

675. Ma ez ê vî tiştî me?
675. Am I one for this thing?

676. Qey tu fedî nake tu wilo dibêje?
676. Are you not embarrassed you speak so?

677. Ma tu çi li dora min dîtîye?
677. What have you seen around me?

678. Perîşanê: Erê erê, ka bêj bê çima hûn wilo man dereng?
678. Perîşanê: Yes, yes, come speak, see why you remained so late?

679. Seyfedîn: Hal û serpêhatîya Sînem û Mela Itman ev bû û dest pê kir.
679. Seyfedîn: The state and adventure of Sînem and Mela Itman was this, and he started.

680. Wê şevê pê de xew neketiye çavên xelkê Misrê de, giş şîyar bûn li ser dengê zilamê ji civatê vegerîyane malê, ê ku ew û jina xwe rabûne hev û heya çîrok jê re gotîye, û xortê ku dêya wî yan bavê wî pê de dixeyide û dibêje, "kurê min şev ne xalîye ne durist e gelekî li civata bimîne, şev e diz hene law derbekê li we xin, kî zane bê kî ye, hûnê ji kîsî xwe herin, law ne baş e bimînî derngê şevê..."
680. From that night on sleep did not enter the eyes of the people of Egypt, all were awake upon the sound of the men returning home from the assembly, he who he and his wife woke each other and he told her the story, and the youth at whom his mother or his father is angry and says, "my son, the night is not empty (safe), it is not right to remain much in assemblies, it is night, there are thieves, boy, they might strike a blow on you, who knows who it is, you will go from your own pocket (die for nothing), boy, it is not good to remain late in the night..."

681. Û wê şevê pê de xelkê bajêr, jin û mêr bi bûyera Sînem û mela dipeyivîn.
681. And from that night on the people of the city, women and men, were speaking of the event of Sînem and the mela.

682. Li maleke din
682. At another house

683. Nûrê: Pepû Sîno, kuro heta niha tu li ku derê bû yî?
683. Nûrê: Poor Sîno, boy, where were you until now?

684. Tu li şevbihêrka kê bû?
684. At whose night gathering were you?

685. Ez zanim tu rast nameşe, mîza te ne zelal e, ka bibêje bê tu li ku derê bû, û we çi dikir?
685. I know you do not walk straight, your urine is not clear, come speak to see where you were, and what were you doing?

686. mîr. Sîno: Hûû... Xwedê ji te jî razî be, tiştê şevê dî çêbû li odeya
686. mîr. Sîno: Hooo... may God be pleased with you too, the things that happened last night in the room of the

687. Nûrê: Bêje bêje kuro, çi bû?
687. Nûrê: Speak, speak, boy, what was it?

688. Çi çêbû?
688. What happened?

689. Sîno: Keçê mane şevê din Sînem Xatûn bi cilê zilama hat civata mîr û serpêhatîya xwe û Mela Itman ta bi derzî yê vekir.
689. Sîno: Girl, after all last night Sînem Xatûn came to the mîr's assembly in men's clothes and unfolded her and Mela Itman's adventure with thread and needle.

690. Nûrê: Pepû pepû, te got çi?
690. Nûrê: Alas, alas, what did you say?

691. Sînem Xatun qey sax e?
691. Sînem Xatûn is alive?

692. Ev heft sal qedyan ne bêhn û ne berat e, li ku derê bû, û çilo hat, û çi got?
692. These seven years finished, there was neither breath nor trace, where was she, and how did she come, and what did she say?

693. Sîno: Hahew Nûrê, tiştê digot porê yekî spî dibû ji ecêb û gosret û bêbextîya.
693. Sîno: Just stop Nûrê, the things she was saying, one's hair would become white from the wonder and astonishment and treachery.

694. Û jê re çîrok dûr û dirêj kir.
694. And he made the story far and long for her.

695. Li maleke din
695. At another house

696. Şiveqê lê xist, lê nexist Mela Silêman kete hundir û rahişte misîn û derket derve, jinik pê hisîya çavên xwe vekirin û li qûn rûnişt.
696. The dawn struck, or it did not strike, Mela Silêman entered inside and grabbed the pitcher and went outside, the woman sensed him, opened her eyes and sat on her bottom.

697. Mela xwe pêk anî û vegerîya ser cilkê rûnişt ku rabe li mêjke.
697. The mela prepared himself and returned, sat on the rug to rise and pray.

698. Gulê (jina Mela Silêman): Pepû Silêmano, heya vê sibê tu li ku derê bû yî kuro?
698. Gulê (Mela Silêman's wife): Poor Silêman, where were you until this morning, boy?

699. qey hina hevûdu kuştibûn? Yan hina
699. had some killed each other? Or had some

700. hevûdu revandibûn?
700. had they kidnapped each other?

701. Jixwe ev karê we melaya ye, hûn xelkê li hev bînin û şîvê xweş bixwin û hin xelata jî bigirin ji bûk û zavayên ku hûn mehra wa dibirin.
701. After all this is the work of you melas, you bring people together and eat a nice dinner and take some gifts as well from the brides and grooms whose dowry (marriage contract) you cut.

702. Mela: Pepûkê xwelîserê çavên te li xelata ye, li hibrî û gora ye, mane îşev ne ev tişt giş bûn, ne kuştin, ne revandin, ne mehirbirîn bû.
702. Mela: Poor ash-headed one, your eyes are on gifts, on ink and socks, after all tonight none of all these things were, it was not killing, not kidnapping, not cutting marriages.

703. Gulê: Pepû mela, naxwe tu li ku derê bû yî, û te çi dikir?
703. Gulê: Poor mela, then where were you, and what were you doing?

704. Şeva reş û tarî tu li çi yê xwe digerîyayî?
704. In the black and dark night what of yours were you searching for?

705. Tu jî weke hineka li tolazîya bûye, tu wilo rîka xwe şayik dikî û cibê xwe utî dike.
705. Have you too like some been in vagabondage, you smooth your beard so and iron your cloak.

706. Xuya ye tu çavlider î.
706. It is visible you are eye-outside (looking around/wandering).

707. Mela: De biner ha, bê çi dibêje, tu çi bêaqil e.
707. Mela: Come look here, see what she says, how mindless you are.

708. Keçê ma ez ê van tişta me?!
708. Girl, am I one for these things?!

709. Gulê: Nexwe tu li ku derê bûyî heya niha, va sibe ye rohilat e?
709. Gulê: Then where were you until now, look it is morning, it is sunrise?

710. Mela: Erê erê keçê tiştê şevê dî çêbû kesî nedîtîye û nebihîstîye.
710. Mela: Yes, yes, girl, the thing that happened last night no one has seen and has not heard.

711. Gulê: Pepû pepû silêmano, qey çi çêbûbû?
711. Gulê: Alas, alas, Silêman, what had happened then?

712. Mela Silêman: keçê wek her şev em li dîwana mîr rûniştîbûn, şêxekê şivan mêvanek bi xwe re anî odeyê bê Rebî û ya star.
712. Mela Silêman: girl, as every night we were sitting in the mîr's court, a shepherd şêx brought a guest with himself to the room, see O Lord and O Protector (how amazing it was).

713. Gulê: Çima qey çilo bû?
713. Gulê: Why, how was it?

714. Çi digot, û çi dikir?
714. What was he saying, and what was he doing?

715. Mela: Na keçê na tu nabê ne zilam bû, pîrek bû û cilê zilama li xwe kirbûn.
715. Mela: No, girl, no, you do not say he was not a man, it was a female and she had put men's clothes on herself.

716. Gulê: Pepû pepû li min qijokê, li min kezîkurê, çilo pîrek cilê zilama li xwe dike û tê odeya mîr nav zilama, ma ji wê jinê ecêbtir heye?!
716. Gulê: Alas, alas to wailing me, to short-braided me, how does a female put men's clothes on herself and come to the mîr's room among the men, is there anything more wondrous than that woman?!

717. Mela: Na keçê na ew Sînam Xatûn bû, ji qazî ve wilo kiribû.
717. Mela: No, girl, no, she was Sînem Xatûn, out of necessity (from fate) she had acted so.

718. Gulê: Pepû Silêman, qey Sînem Xatûn sax e?
718. Gulê: Poor Silêman, is Sînem Xatûn then alive?

719. Û ev heft salê wê li ku derê bû?
719. And for these seven years of hers where was she?

720. Li kijan welatî bû, û çi dikir, û çilo vegerîya malê?
720. In which country was she, and what was she doing, and how did she return home?

721. Mela: Hew hew ev serpêhatîyeke dûr û dirêj e, û dest pê kir.
721. Mela: Just stop, just stop, this is a far and long adventure, and he started.

722. ## Li maleke din
722. ## At another house

723. Sofi Ehmed ket hundir û hema dibêje, "ya Rebî stara te, ya Rebî tu me ji qeda û bela bistirîne, law hema rabin û rûnin û bibêjin ya star".
723. Sofi Ehmed entered inside and just says, "O Lord your protection, O Lord you shelter us from calamity and trouble, boy, just get up and sit down and say O Protector".

724. Helîmê: Çi ye Sofi Ehmed?
724. Helîmê: What is it Sofi Ehmed?

725. Çi bela te ye?
725. What is your trouble?

726. Careke din çi çêbûye?
726. What has happened once again?

727. Cardî şer çêbûye xelkê li talanê hev xistine?
727. Has war happened again, have the people struck at each other's plunder?

728. Sofi Ehmed: Na keçê na xwezî wilo ba û ne ev bêbextî û bênamûsî ba.
728. Sofi Ehmed: No, girl, no, if only it were so and it were not this treachery and dishonor.

729. Helîmê: Pepû sofî çi çêbûye?
729. Helîmê: Poor sofî, what has happened?

730. Çi qewimî ye?
730. What has occurred?

731. Sofi: ha hew Helîmê, mane şevê dî Sînem Xatun hat û kete odeya mîr bi cilê zilama û kesî ew nas nekir û serpêhatîya xwe û Mela Itman got û dûr û dirêj kir li odeyê, di wê civatê de.
731. Sofi: just stop Helîmê, after all last night Sînem Xatûn came and entered the mîr's room in men's clothes and no one recognized her and she told her and Mela Itman's adventure and made it far and long (detailed) in the room, in that assembly.

732. Helîmê: Pepû pepû li min rebenê, li min kezîkurê.
732. Helîmê: Alas, alas to wretched me, to short-braided me.

733. Sînem Xatûn li ku derê bû?
733. Where was Sînem Xatûn?

734. Ev heft sal qedyane, hê Sînem sax e?
734. These seven years have finished, is Sînem still alive?

735. Sofî: Erê jinik erê hîn sax e û pepûkê ji bêbextîya Mela Itman bi çol û pola ketibû, birçî, tazî, pêxwas.
735. Sofî: Yes, woman, yes, she is still alive, and the poor thing from Mela Itman's treachery had fallen to the wilderness and deserts, hungry, naked, barefoot.

736. Û çîrok got.
736. And he told the story.

737. ## Li maleke din
737. ## At another house

738. Feqe Elî kete devê derî ku rahêje misîn û here destmêj bigire, dengê banga melê serê sibê hat û got "Elah û Ekber".
738. Feqe Elî entered the mouth of the door to grab the pitcher and go to take ablution, the sound of the mela's morning call to prayer came and said "God is Great".

739. Feqe Elî: Elah û Ekber, Elah û Ekber.
739. Feqe Elî: God is Great, God is Great.

740. Ya Rebî tu li min negire vî bêbavê Mela Itman nimêj û misilmantî li ber çavên me reş kirîye.
740. O Lord do not hold it against me, this fatherless Mela Itman has blackened prayer and Islam before our eyes.

741. Pepûko bi dilekî ji destî deng li feqa kir û got: "Rabin rabin ma hûn dengê mela nakin, bi şev pê de hûn razayî ne, qey hûn têr xew nabin?"
741. The poor one with a heart out of hand (distressed) called to the students and said: "Get up, get up, do you not hear the sound of the mela, from the night onwards you are asleep, are you not satisfied with sleep?"

742. Feqe jî weke her roj rabûn ji xew û berê xwe dan cih şûştin û veşûştinê di mizgeftê de û dest bi timaz û heneka kirin.
742. The students too as every day got up from sleep and turned their direction to the place of washing and bathing in the mosque and started with jesting and joking.

743. Xortên xwîngerm in hayê wan ji bayê felekê tune ye, hîn tiştek nebihîstine.
743. They are warm-blooded (young) youths, they have no awareness of the wind of fate, they have not yet heard anything.

744. Feqe Elî dengê xwe hilda û got: Kuro gelî feqa rûnên bi aqil bin law bi Xwedê kes nema parîk nan dide me, bisekinin
744. Feqe Elî raised his voice and said: Boy, O students sit down, be with mind (be wise), boy, by God no one anymore gives us a piece of bread, stop

745. xwedênehiştno, tiştê hatîye serê me tiştekî kesnedî ye li darê dunyayê.
745. O God-forsaken ones, the thing that has come upon our head is an unseen thing in the world.

746. Feqa bi hesret û gosretmayî pirsîn, çima Feqe Elî?
746. The students with longing and astonishment asked, why Feqe Elî?

747. Çi çêbûye, dunya zîvirîye?
747. What has happened, has the world turned?

748. Quliptîye?
748. Has it flipped?

749. Xelkê, dijmina li talanê me xistîye?
749. Have the people, the enemies, struck at our plunder?

750. Feqe Elî: Xwezî wilo ba, û ne ev ecêba ha ba.
750. Feqe Elî: If only it were so, and it were not this wonder.

751. Feqa gişa bi hev re: Pek û sed carî pek, ev çi ecê b
751. All the students together: Alas and a hundred times alas, what wonder

752. e?!
752. is this?!

753. Feqa Elî: De meşin hicra xwe, dûra ez ê ji we re bêjim.
753. Feqe Elî: Come walk to your room, afterwards I will tell you.

754. Feqa hemîyan bi lez û bez, zû zû xwe pêk aînin û destnimêj girtin û bi sivikayî berê xwe dan hucrê û rawistîyan li hêvîya Feqe Elî ku derbas bibe û serpêhatîya Sînem Xatûn û Mela Itman ji wan re bibêje.
754. All the students with speed and running, quickly quickly prepared themselves and took ablution and lightly turned their direction to the room and waited for Feqe Elî to pass and tell them the adventure of Sînem Xatûn and Mela Itman.

755. Ew jî li wê navê rûnişt û dest bi çîrokê kir.
755. He too in that meantime sat and started the story.

756. Feqe Silo: Wey Xwedê mala te xira kiro Mela Itman, ma ev jî ji te?
756. Feqe Silo: Woe, may God ruin your house Mela Itman, is this too from you?

757. Feqe Hiso: De Xwedê mala wî li mîratê bigerîne, û êş û bela di laşê wî xîne.
757. Feqe Hiso: Come may God turn his house into a ruin, and put pain and trouble in his body.

758. Feqe Şerîf: De na lo ez bawer nakim, yekî wek Mela Itman vî tiştî bike.
758. Feqe Şerîf: Come no man, I do not believe it, that someone like Mela Itman would do this thing.

759. Feqe Hemîd: Na na tu bawer nake, ne wa mêrik ji te re bi cih û cîwar dike.
759. Feqe Hemîd: No, no, you do not believe it, see the man is establishing it (making it clear) for you with place and settlement.

760. Feqe Selîm: De yabo, ka em ê çilo bikin?
760. Feqe Selîm: Come father, well, how will we do?

761. çawa bikin ji vi bêbextî?
761. what should we do about this treachery?

762. Feqe Mihemed: Em ê çilo bikin?
762. Feqe Mihemed: How will we do?

763. ma ya me çi ye û çi şuxlê me jê heye?
763. after all what is ours (what business is it of ours) and what work of ours is there with him?

764. wî ev tiştê ha yê bênamûsî kirine, ma ya me çi ye?
764. he has done these things of dishonor, after all what is ours?

765. Û bi vî rengî feqe hemî ketine qirka hev de û her yek ji xwe re tiştekî dibêje bi qîr qîr, hin bi xeber û sixêf û gotinê çors, û hin dibêjin ka bê sibê wê çi bê serê me feqa û oldara û ditirsin ku Mîr Mamed vê xezebê û zor û zehmetîyê di serê me re derxe, û feqe û mela û dîndar û oldar li ber çavên wî reş bibin.
765. And in this way the students all fell into each other's throats and each says something to himself with shouting, some with insults and curses and coarse words, and some say let us see what will come upon the head of us students and religious men tomorrow, and they fear that Mîr Mamed will take this anger and force and difficulty out over our head, and students and melas and pious and religious men will become black before his eyes.

766. Û hin dibêjin na lo mîrê me zilamekî dilovan e, û ji Xwedê ditirse tu carî tiştê dervî rê nekirine û nake jî, ez bawer nakim.
766. And some say no man, our mîr is a merciful man, and he fears God, he has never done things outside the path and does not do them either, I do not believe it.

767. Feqe Mihyedîn: Yabo bi Xwedê mêrik çi bike ji serê me heqê wî heye law, erê em dîndar in û em hedîs û Quranê dixwînin lê em pêş pê nakin, û çi finasê pîs û genî hene ji mela û feqa dertê lawo.
767. Feqe Mihyedîn: Father, by God whatever the man does to our head he has the right, boy, yes we are religious and we read hadith and the Quran but we do not advance by it, and whatever dirty and rotten trickery there is comes out from melas and students, boy.

768. Feqe Şemsedîn: Kuro law mêrik heft sala nexweş û li ser piştê ma, û jina wî weke kehreke xezala bi çol û pola ket li şar û bajarê xerîb û nenas; bi parsê, bi kar û qerwaşîyê zikekî têr û dehê birçî û ev jina ciwan û nazik û nazdar têkeve vî halî bi potikê peritî, bi çerm û îyarê kehir û berxa, ji bo xwe biparêze ji tolaz û çavlidera, ji çeta û rêbira.
768. Feqe Şemsedîn: Boy, man, the man remained sick and on his back for seven years, and his wife like a gazelle fawn fell to the wilderness and deserts in a strange and unknown province and city; with begging, with work and servitude one belly full and ten hungry, and this young and delicate and coquettish woman falling into this state with tattered rags, with the skin and hide of fawns and lambs, in order to protect herself from vagabonds and wanderers, from bandits and highway robbers.

769. Hîn çavê we lê ye mîr li me bê rehm û dilovanîyê.
769. Is your eye still on this (do you still expect) that the mîr will come with mercy and compassion to us.

770. Hema bi Xwedê kî ji dêla wî ve be wê fermana serê misilmana, oldara, dîndara rake û devê mizgefta bigire û riha van sofî û mela û feqan bi gwîzanê ko û zingargirtî kur bike.
770. Just by God whoever is in his place will lift the command (order the execution) of the head of Muslims, religious men, pious men, and close the mouth of mosques and shave the beard of these sofîs and melas and students with a blunt and rusted razor.

771. law ma ne heqê wî ye?
771. boy, after all is it not his right?

772. Feqe Birahîm: Na na gelî hevala û feqa, yekî pîsîtî û xerabî kirîye, ma ya me çi ye?
772. Feqe Birahîm: No, no, O friends and students, one has committed filth and badness, after all what is ours (what business is it of ours)?

773. Feqe Simo: Ha hew mane golikek navê garanekê xera dike.
773. Feqe Simo: Just stop, after all one calf ruins the name of a herd.

774. Feqe Birahîm: Na na wilo nebêjin mîrê me zilamekî zane ye û dilovan e, û xwedênas e û kesî bi gunehê kesî naşewitîne, mî bi nigê xwe û bizin bi nigê xwe ye, kes nakeve tirba kesî de.
774. Feqe Birahîm: No, no, do not say so, our mîr is a wise and merciful man, and he is God-knowing and he does not burn anyone with the sin of anyone (punish the innocent), a sheep is by its own foot and a goat is by its own foot (everyone is responsible for their own actions), no one falls into the tomb of anyone else.

775. Zaro (feqe) di vê dan û standin û gengeşê de ne, dengê bangê banggêrê hat û dibêje hê ji hev re bêjin dengê min bera bê we.
775. The children (students) are in this exchange and discussion, the sound of the caller's (crier's) call came and says keep saying to each other, let my voice come to you.

776. "Îro nîvro wê Mela Itman li dadgehê bi bersivbidin.
776. "Today at noon they will make Mela Itman give answers in court.

777. Bi rûniştina Mîr Mamed û koma şêwirdar û dadwera, û guneh û finasê wî bînin ziman û eşkere pirsa jê bikin û ew bersiva xwe bide".
777. With the sitting of Mîr Mamed and the group of advisors and judges, and they will bring his sin and trickery to the tongue and openly ask him the question, and he is to give his answer".

778. Xelkê Misrê giş ketine hev, leq in nahedinin wek keleka ser avê ne.
778. The people of Egypt have all fallen into each other, they are shaking, they do not calm down, they are like a raft on the water.

779. Biçûk û mezin, jin û mêr, kal û pîr, hemû bi vê bûyerê dipeyivin.
779. Small and great, women and men, old men and old women, all are speaking of this event.

780. ## Li Ser Tenû ra
780. ## On The Ovens

781. Pîrek li ser tenûra digihêjin hev û ji hev re çîrok û bûyera dibêjin.
781. Females reach each other on the ovens and tell the story and events to each other.

782. bûn.
782. were.

783. Hêzin: Îro hemû gotin û peyv li ser bûyera Sînem û mela
783. Hêzin: Today all sayings and words are about the event of Sînem and the mela.

784. Elîfê: Welê Xecê te bihîst, çîroka şevê dî?
784. Elîfê: Is that so Xecê, did you hear the story of last night?

785. Xecê: Çîroka çi welê Elîfê, qey çi çêbûbû?
785. Xecê: The story of what, is that so Elîfê, what had happened then?

786. Elîfê: Mane şevê dî Sînem Xatun hatibû odeya Mîr Mamed bi cilê zilama û serpêhatîya xwe û mela got û wê jî dûr û dirêj kir.
786. Elîfê: After all last night Sînem Xatûn had come to Mîr Mamed's room in men's clothes and told her and the mela's adventure and made it far and long.

787. Emşo: Pepûkê Sekîna, te bihîst bê çi çêbû şevê dî?
787. Emşo: Poor Sekîne, did you hear what happened last night?

788. Sekîne: Erê welê, ma tu nanere li vê gosret û kesnedîyê?
788. Sekîne: Yes, is that so, do you not look at this astonishment and unseen thing?

789. Ev tişt jî li dunyayê hene, min digot qey mela guneha nakin.
789. These things too exist in the world, I thought perhaps melas do not commit sins.

790. Emşê: Ma çawa guneha nakin?!
790. Emşê: How do they not commit sins?!

791. Jixwe gunehê mezin şêx û mela dikin?
791. After all do the great sins not get committed by şêxes and melas?

792. Fato: Pepûkê Zeynebê, ma tu nabêjî bê çilo fen li vê pepûka Sînem Xatun kirin û xistin germava şûştinê de?
792. Fato: Poor Zeyneb, why do you not say how they tricked this poor Sînem Xatûn and put her in the hot bath for washing?

793. Çilo li wan ewle bû?
793. How was she secure (trusting) of them?

794. Zeynebê: Keçê ma hema wilo da dû wan û çû.
794. Zeynebê: Girl, after all she just followed them and went.

795. Na na ew bêbava pîra cadû fen lê kir û carî û navmalîya wê bû, bi tena xwe çûn.
795. No, no, that fatherless old witch tricked her and she was her maid and household servant, they went alone.

796. Lê wê bêbavê derî lê girt û kilît da melê bênamûs ku xwe li wan dera veşartibû, pîrê kilît da dest û perê xwe standin û revîya çû, û mela hat ket hundirê serokê de.
796. But that fatherless one closed the door on her and gave the key to the dishonorable mela who had hidden himself around those places, the old woman put the key in his hand and took her money and fled and went, and the mela came and entered inside the bath.

797. Ma çi hayê Sînemê jê hebû?
797. After all what awareness did Sînem have of it?

798. Fato: Pepû pepû, wey li min rebenê!
798. Fato: Alas, alas, woe to wretched me!

799. Pepûkê di vê mero li kesî ewle nebe.
799. Poor one, in this a man should not trust anyone.

800. Ferîda: Pepûkê porkurê Fethîya!
800. Ferîda: Poor short-haired Fethîya!

801. Te bihîst bê şevê dî çi çêbûbû?
801. Did you hear what had happened last night?

802. Fethîya: Erê welê min bihîst, mêrê min şevê dî li odeyê bû û hat ji min re got.
802. Fethîya: Yes, is that so, I heard, my husband was in the room last night and came and told me.

803. Ferida: Te dî welê, bê çi tiştê ecêbî ji van xwedîyê riha tên?!
803. Ferida: Did you see, is that so, what wondrous things come from these owners of beards?!

804. Fethiya: De wa wê heqê wî bidinê, ka bê wî bi çi rengî bikujin.
804. Fethiya: Come, now they will give him his right (due), let us see in what manner they will kill him.

805. Wê rojê tu bi ku de here, li zikaka, li çarçîya, li kargeha, li nav bexçeyan heya bi şivanê li çola, ev çîrok li dar e, her kes pê diştaxile û ji hev re dibêjin, "kuro bi Xwedê talîya dinyayê ye, çawa zilamekî wek Mela Itman dozdehilmî, hafizê hedîs û Quranê wê bi vî finasê pîs rabe?"
805. That day wherever you go, in the alleyways, in the markets, in the workshops, among the gardens even up to the shepherds in the wilderness, this story is ongoing, everyone talks about it and says to each other, "boy, by God it is the end of the world, how could a man like Mela Itman of twelve sciences, memorizer of hadith and the Quran get up with this dirty trickery?"

806. ## Li Dadgehê
806. ## In The Court

807. Dadmend, şêwirdar, qazî, miftî (cîgirê Mela Itman), Şêx û meşayixê bi nav û deng, axa û begên bajêr, başbazirganê li Misrê giş rûniştin li ser kursîya, bêdeng.
807. Judges, advisors, Islamic judges, muftis (Mela Itman's deputy), Şêxes and renowned elders, agha and begs of the city, chief merchants in Egypt all sat on the chairs, silently.

808. Dadgerê mezin û her du dadwerên li tenista rast û çepê Mela Itman anîn xistin rekela gunehkaran de piştî dest û lingên wî vekirin.
808. The grand judge and both judges on the right and left side had Mela Itman brought and put into the enclosure of the guilty ones after unbinding his hands and legs.

809. Dadger: Ha mela tu gunehkar î, ka tu çi dibêjî?
809. Judge: Ah mela, you are guilty, well what do you say?

810. Mela: Ma ez ê çi bibêjim, piştî vê hetîketîyê (Bi zorê deng jî hat fêm kirin.)
810. Mela: What shall I say, after this disgrace (His voice was understood with difficulty.)

811. Dadger: Bêje bêje, heger tiştek li cem te hebe ji rastîyê bêje, belkî tu gunehê xwe sivik bike.
811. Judge: Speak, speak, if there is anything with you from the truth speak, perhaps you might lighten your sin.

812. Mela çavên wî dikutkutîn, lêvên wî dilerizîn, zimanê wî girêdayî, rîka wî dikebitî, dikir nedikir deng jê dernediket û di ber xwe de digot: "Xwezî ez miribama û ev tişt nehatiba serê min", û çavên xwe girtin.
812. The mela, his eyes were fluttering, his lips were trembling, his tongue tied, his beard dropping, whatever he did no sound came out of him and he was saying to himself: "If only I had died and this thing had not come upon my head", and he closed his eyes.

813. Berdevk: Ma wê çi bibêje, gunehkar e gunehkar e, bersiv jê re nîne.
813. Spokesman: After all what will he say, he is guilty he is guilty, there is no answer for him.

814. Dadger: Ji mafê wî ye ku bersiva xwe bide.
814. Judge: It is from his right that he gives his answer.

815. Kirin, nekirin deng nema ji mela hat û bi hêdî dibêje, "ez mirî me ez mirî me".
815. They did, they did not (whatever they tried), no sound came from the mela anymore and he slowly says, "I am dead, I am dead".

816. Dadger û dadmendên li dorê li hev şêwirîn, ka em çi bikin ji mela?
816. The judge and the judges around consulted with each other, what shall we do to the mela?

817. - Heqê wî mere wî herî bike û li sûk û çarçîyan bigerîne.
817. - His right is that a man (we) cover him in mud and walk him through the markets and bazaars.

818. - Na wele heqê wî mere alîyekî wî kur bike û alîyekî bihêle û li hewşê wî girê bidin û kî di ber wî re here tif bike wî.
818. - No, by God, his right is that a man shaves one side of him and leaves one side and they tie him in the courtyard and whoever goes past him spits on him.

819. Kuro ya baş ew e hûn wî li xazoqê xînin, lagasînê.
819. Boy, the good thing is you put him on the impaling stake, in the public square.

820. - Hûûû.. wilo ne tiştek e.
820. - Hooo.. that is nothing.

821. Heqê wî tazî bikin û bêrîkan di laşê wî de bikin û rîka wî tako tako rakin û diranên wî yeko yeko bi kelbetanan rakin.
821. His right is they strip him naked and cut pockets in his body and pluck his beard strand by strand and pull his teeth one by one with pliers.

822. - Ev çi ye law... Gereke hûn wî daşilqandî bikin serjêr daleqînin heya bimire.
822. - What is this, boy... It is necessary you mangle him and hang him upside down until he dies.

823. - Na na wilo hindik e.
823. - No, no, that is too little.

824. Gereke hûn wî girê bidin di orta du kuçikên har û birçî de.
824. It is necessary you tie him in the middle of two rabid and hungry dogs.

825. Dadger: Rabin her yek herin karê xwe em ê careke din bi hevûdu bişêwirin.
825. Judge: Get up, each go to your work, we will once again consult with each other.

826. Careke din milet û xelkê bajêr ketin hêlekan û gengeşeyê de bê ka wê çi bikin ji serê melayî, û her yek ji xwe re tiştekî dibêje ji vê çîrokê pê ve tune ye, bûye benîşt û ketîye devê xelkê de.
826. Once again the nation and the people of the city fell into rocking and discussion as to what they will do to the mela's head, and each says something to himself, there is nothing other than this story, it has become chewing gum and fallen into the mouths of the people.

827. Bi vî halî du roj qedîyan.
827. In this state two days finished.

828. Roja sisêya dengê banggêra di minara de li hemî tar û zikaka bela bû.
828. On the third day the sound of the criers in the minarets spread in all the neighborhoods and alleyways.

829. "Hêêê.. nîvro li gasînê li orta bajêr wê gunehê Mela Itman lê bibirin".
829. "Heee.. at noon in the square in the middle of the city they will cut (decide) Mela Itman's sin upon him".

830. Xelkê gişa dev ji kar û îşê xwe berdan û hatin li dora gasîna bajêr rawistîyan heya mela werînin.
830. All the people gave up their work and labor and came and stood around the city square until they brought the mela.

831. xelk hatin zilam bi rêz û xelek li dora gasînê, û jin û pîrek derketin jora xanîya û temaşe dikin.
831. the people came, men in rows and rings around the square, and women and females went up on top of the houses and watch.

832. Berî nimêja nîvro dadger û şêwirdar û qazî û miftî û gergerê bajêr jî civîyan.
832. Before the noon prayer the judge and advisors and Islamic judges and muftis and managers of the city also gathered.

833. Çend xorta du qantir anîn vajî hev sekinandin û her nigekî mela bi noqa yekê ve girê dan.
833. A few youths brought two mules and stopped them opposite each other and tied each leg of the mela to the halter of one.

834. Ev qantir ev sê roja êm nedane yekê, birçî ye û av nedane ya din, tî ye, û satila avê li pêşîya ya tî danîn bi dûrbûna gavekê, û tûrê ceh li pêşîya ya birçî danîn bi dûrbûna gavekê û serê her du qantira bi hev re berdan, her duyan bi hêrs xwe kişandin ser êm û avê û mela di orta wan de hat çirandin di nêvî re.
834. These mules, for these three days they did not give feed to one, it is hungry, and did not give water to the other, it is thirsty, and they placed the bucket of water in front of the thirsty one at a distance of a step, and they placed the sack of barley in front of the hungry one at a distance of a step and released the heads of both mules together, both of them with anger pulled themselves towards the feed and water and the mela in the middle of them was torn in half.

835. Bû Elah Elaha xelkê, bû lîrelîra jinaû pîreka.
835. It became the 'God, God' of the people, it became the trilling of women and females.

836. Hin dibêjin di heqê wî de bû, hin dibêjin de bixwe tu elimîye li dora jinê xelkê bigere, û hin dibêjin ohyan a me li te hat te wiqas zor û zehmetî li xelkê dikir, û hin dibêjin Xwedê nehêle sala sed û yekê be wê eşkere bûbe.
836. Some say it was in his right (he deserved it), some say well yourself you are accustomed to wandering around the people's women, and some say yes ours came upon you, you were doing so much force and difficulty to the people, and some say God does not let it be a hundred and one years, it will be revealed.

837. Piştre xelk bela wela bûn, termê mela birin veşartin li deverekê binax kirin.
837. Afterwards the people scattered, they took the mela's corpse and buried it in a place underground.

838. Ji nû ve kêf û şahî li dar xistin daweta mîr û Sînem nû kirin hefteyekê dahol û zirnê betal nekir, û qîz û xortê welêt diketin dîlanê û govend digerandin, û miletê Misrê ketin şahî û xêra Xwedê de.
838. Anew they established joy and celebration, they renewed the wedding of the mîr and Sînem, for a week the drum and zurna did not cease, and the girls and youths of the country fell into the dance and led the govend (circle dance), and the nation of Egypt fell into the joy and blessing of God.

839. Jiyan ji nû ve vebû ji jina, ji ajala, ji teyr û tilûra, ji gul û gîya û çîçeka.
839. Life opened anew for women, for animals, for birds and fowls, for roses and grass and flowers.

840. Qîz û xorta bi dildarî hevûdu xwestin û şo kirin û govend û dîlan li hemû deverê bajar û gundan çêdibûn.
840. Girls and youths with love asked for each other and rejoiced and govend and dances were happening in all areas of the city and villages.

841. Piştî heft salên zor, zehmetî û qiriktahlîyê, rojek nû li welêt hilat bi kêf û şahî û xêr û xweşî û ji nû ve Mîr Mamed û Sînem Xatûn dest bi jiyaneke nû kirin bi şahî û dildarî, û Xwedê bedena Sînem şîn kir û warê mîr nû kir.
841. After seven years of force, difficulty and bitterness, a new sun rose in the country with joy and celebration and goodness and pleasantness and anew Mîr Mamed and Sînem Xatûn started a new life with celebration and love, and God made Sînem's body green (healed her) and renewed the mîr's domain.

842. Xwedê kurekî sipehî û xweşik da wan.
842. God gave them a handsome and beautiful boy.

843. ## Sîyamendê Silîva Xwedîyê Tîr û Kevanê Ekfîyê Zîvî
843. ## Sîyamend of Silîva Owner of the Arrow and Bow of Silver Ekfî

844. ## Erdnîgarîya Silîvayê (Silva, Farqîn)
844. ## The Geography of Silîva (Silva, Farqîn)

845. Şarê Silîvanîyê dikeve bakur û rojhilatî Amedê de bi nêzîka 170 km.
845. The city of Silîvanî falls in the north and east of Amed by about 170 km.

846. Derebegîyeke mezin e, topraxa wê nêzîkî 1400 km, û erdeke bilind e di ser derya re bi qasî 2760m bilind e, hawîrdor xerbe û qelaç û çîya ne, dikeve orta her du çemên mezin de, Dicle û Ferat.
846. It is a great principality, its land is near 1400 km, and it is a high land above the sea, high by about 2760m, the surroundings are ruins and peaks and mountains, it falls in the middle of both great rivers, the Tigris and the Euphrates.

847. Çîyayê wê bi baran û berf û kanî ne, hemî dar û devî ne.
847. Its mountains are with rain and snow and springs, they are all trees and bushes.

848. Bajarekî kevnare ye ji berî zayînê ve, gelek cara selacîqê roma dagir kirine û gelek caran firsê ecem dagir kirine û bi dehê caran miletê wê hatîye talankirin ji her du dijminan ve.
848. It is an ancient city from before the birth (BC), many times the Seljuks of Rome have occupied it and many times the Persians of Ajam have occupied it and tens of times its nation has been plundered by both enemies.

849. welatekî xweş e bi xêr û xêrat e bi çandinî ye ji genim û ceh, û nîsk, û noka, û ji hemî dar û devîya û rez û werza, ji hemî cûrayên fêkî û mêwê tirî, û li dorê çem û cobar diherikin ji ava baranê, ji berfê û ji kanîyê ji çîyê dertên.
849. it is a pleasant country with goodness and charity, it is with agriculture from wheat and barley, and lentils, and chickpeas, and from all trees and bushes and vineyards and fields, from all kinds of fruit and grape vines, and around it rivers and streams flow from rainwater, from snow and from the springs that come out of the mountain.

850. Şîn dibin li dorê mêrg û delav, gul û gîya û çîmen û nefel.
850. Meadows and pools, roses and grass and lawns and clover grow green around it.

851. Xwedî dikin naxirê dewar û çêleka û kerîyê mî û bizina.
851. They raise herds of cattle and cows and flocks of sheep and goats.

852. Miletekî karker û karmend e û bi her tiştê xwe ve têr û dewletî ye.
852. It is a worker and official (hardworking) nation and with everything of theirs they are satisfied and wealthy.

853. ji ber wilo tim cavên derve lê digerîyan û diz û çeta û talançî û pêxwasa her sal êrîş dikirin ser bajêr û gundewarên wê.
853. because of that outside eyes always searched upon it, and thieves and bandits and plunderers and vagabonds every year attacked the city and its countryside.

854. Miletê wê hawîrdora bajêr sûrek mezin û bilind lê kir ji bo karibe dijmina vegerîne, û heya niha hîn perçenine ji kelehê û ji sûrê û ji pira kevnare "Pira Malbadî" mane.
854. Its nation built a great and high wall around the city in order to be able to turn back the enemies, and until now there still remain pieces of the castle and of the wall and of the ancient bridge "Pira Malbadî".

855. Şarê Farqînê di vi halî de jiyana xwe derbas dikir, geh bi xweşî û geh bi şer û pevçûn û vegerandina talana, heya misilmantî hat û welatê kurdistanê û hemî rojhilata navîn dagir kirin bi şûr û mertala, bi zor û talana, û ola misilmanîyê belav kirin.
855. The city of Farqîn was passing its life in this state, sometimes with pleasantness and sometimes with war and conflict and returning the plunder, until Islam came and occupied the country of Kurdistan and all the Middle East with sword and shield, with force and plunder, and they spread the religion of Islam.

856. Bi xweşî bû bû, bi xweşî nebû bi zorê, ji ber ku miletê kurd ji berê de xwedênas bû û xwedî ol bû.
856. If it was by pleasantness it was, if it was not by pleasantness it was by force, because the Kurdish nation from before was God-knowing and owned a religion.

857. Ango berî misilmana û ola ereban bi hezarê salan kurd di dîrokê de xwedênas in, ezî ne, êzidî (xwedayî) û zerdeştî ne bi Xwedakê şev û rojê "Ahoramezda" bawer in û xwe ji "Ehrîman"ê bi tirs diparastin.
857. That is to say, thousands of years before Muslims and the religion of the Arabs, Kurds in history are God-knowing, they are Ezî, Ezidî (godly) and Zoroastrian, they believe in one God of night and day "Ahura Mazda" and protect themselves with fear from "Ahriman".

858. Lê dema ola Pêxember Mûsa, cihûtî derket gelek ji kurdan bûn cihû û çûn ser ola Mûsa, Silêman û Dawud.
858. But when the religion of Prophet Moses, Judaism, came out, many of the Kurds became Jews and went upon the religion of Moses, Solomon and David.

859. Lê dema ku ola xirîstîyanî hat û Pêxember Îsa xuya bû û derket holê gelek ji kurdan careke din bûn xirîstîyan û ketin ola Pêxember Îsa de.
859. But when the Christian religion came and Prophet Jesus appeared and came out to the middle (emerged), many of the Kurds once again became Christians and fell into the religion of Prophet Jesus.

860. Jixwe piştî ku ola ereba, "misilmanî" derket, û Pêxember Mihemed Quran belav kir, ereba welatê xelkê bi zorê vekirin û talan kirin, yê bi xweşî bû misilman xwe û zarokên xwe fik kirin ji cizî û kuştinê, û yê bi xweşî nebû misilman cizî jê standin, yan dikuştin û bi zorê zarokên wan û jinên wan tanîn dikirin misilman û qîzê wan dikirin carî û sebî û li xwe helal dikirin, û gelek ji eşîrên kurdan revîyan ji ber misilmana, ew dikuştin û talan dikirin.
860. After all, after the religion of the Arabs, "Islam", came out, and Prophet Muhammad spread the Quran, the Arabs forcefully opened (conquered) and plundered the countries of the people; whoever became Muslim by pleasantness freed himself and his children from the jizya (tax) and killing, and whoever did not become Muslim by pleasantness they took jizya from him, or they killed them and forcefully brought their children and their women and made them Muslims and made their daughters maids and captives and made them lawful for themselves, and many of the Kurdish tribes fled from the Muslims, they were killing and plundering.

861. Direvîyan diketin çîya û çol û şikefta, xwe vedişartin li bin dar û deviyan.
861. They fled, fell to the mountains and wilderness and caves, hid themselves under trees and bushes.

862. Ji wê çaxê de gelek oldar tev eşîrê xwe revîyan ber bi rojhilat ve qûnax bi qûnax heya gihan rojavayê Hindê û heya niha nevîyên wan li wir in û hin in ji pelên Avista parastine û man ser ola xwe ya zerdeştî.
862. Since that time many religious men along with their tribe fled towards the east stage by stage until they reached the west of India and until now their descendants are there and some have protected leaves of the Avesta and remained on their Zoroastrian religion.

863. Di dema Xelîfe Omer û Osman de ferman dan çi kesê oldarê êzîdî be an zerdeştî be û kî havizê Avista be kuştina wî helal e û durist e, û bi vî hawî welatê Kurdistanê kete bin destê Dewleta Islamê de.
863. In the time of Caliph Omar and Othman they gave the order that whatever person is a religious Ezidî or Zoroastrian and whoever is a memorizer of the Avesta, his killing is lawful and right, and in this manner the country of Kurdistan fell under the hand of the Islamic State.

864. Dema ku kurd bûn misilman, ji dil û can bûn misilman ji ber ku berê xwedênas û xwedî ol bûn, û bi seda zana û leheng
864. When the Kurds became Muslims, they became Muslims from heart and soul because they were God-knowing and owned a religion before, and hundreds of wise men and heroes

865. û mêrxasên kurdan di ber Dewleta Islamê de kar kirin û zanist bi pêş ve birin, û pêşxistin derbasî felsefeya îslamî, edebîyat û rêzimana erebî kirin; herweha bi karên kîmîya û tenduristîyê rabûn, û bi danhev û berhevkarîya peyv û gotinên erebî daketin û ferhengên mezin bi zimanê erebî çêkirin.
865. and braves of the Kurds worked before (for) the Islamic State and advanced science, and passed development into Islamic philosophy, Arabic literature and grammar; likewise they rose with works of chemistry and health, and they descended with (undertook) the gathering and compilation of Arabic words and sayings and made great dictionaries in the Arabic language.

866. Ji wan: Sîbewê, Ibin Sîna, Razî, Zemexşerî, Al Xeyam, Melayê Xewarizmî, û gelekên din wekî Ebû Mislimê Xorasanî bi Ebû Al Ebas re emewî herifandin û ebasî damezirandin.
866. From them: Sibawayh, Ibn Sina, Razi, Zamakhshari, Al-Khayyam, Mela of Khwarazm, and many others like Abu Muslim Khorasani with Abu al-Abbas collapsed the Umayyads and established the Abbasids.

867. Û dema êrîşên xaçperestan hatin ser welatê misilmanan, kurd bi biçûk û mezinê xwe rabûn û welatê ereban parastin û Selahedînê Eyûbî di dîrokê de minarayeke bilind û mezin e, û dema çû Silmanê Ereb miletê wî bin pê kirin û ji hemî mafên wî qut kirin.
867. And when the attacks of the Crusaders came upon the countries of the Muslims, the Kurds with their small and great rose and protected the country of the Arabs, and Saladin Ayyubi is a high and great minaret in history, and when he passed away, Salman the Arab trampled his nation underfoot and cut them off from all their rights.

868. Piştî mirina Selahedîn welatê misilmantîyê kete destên memalîk û mîr û derebegîyan de û gelek ji van herêman man di destên malbata Eyûbîyan de wek li Misrê, Helebê, Mûsilê û li Farqînê (Silîva).
868. After Saladin's death, the country of Islam fell into the hands of Mamluks and mîrs and principalities, and many of these regions remained in the hands of the Ayyubid family, such as in Egypt, Aleppo, Mosul and in Farqîn (Silîva).

869. ## Farqînê (Siliva)
869. ## Farqîn (Silîva)

870. Şarê Farqînê şarekî kevnare ye, ava ye ji berî zayîna Pêxember Îsa.
870. The city of Farqîn is an ancient city, it is built from before the birth of Prophet Jesus.

871. Farqîn dikeve bakur û rojhilatî Amedê (Diyarbekir) bi 170 km.
871. Farqîn falls in the north and east of Amed (Diyarbakır) by 170 km.

872. Di orta her du çemên mezin de ye, Dicle û Ferat (Mûrade).
872. It is in the middle of both great rivers, the Tigris and the Euphrates (Murat).

873. Piştî mirina Selahedîn, Farqîn ma di bin destê Mîr Mamedî, Xazî Aleyûbî û bi navê “Al-Kamil" dihat nasîn hingî qenc û rind û dilovan bû.
873. After Saladin's death, Farqîn remained under the hand of Mîr Mamed, Ghazi al-Ayyubi and was known by the name "Al-Kamil" because he was so good and fine and merciful.

874. Di dema wî de derdora sala 639 koçeyî, 1231 zayînî de miletê Farqînê di xêr û xweşîyê de bû, ji her alîyî ve dewletî bû, bi çandinî û xwedîkirina pez û dewaran gelekî dewletî bû, herweha bi xwendin û zanist û ezberkirina hedîs û Quranê.
874. In his time around the Hijri year 639, Gregorian 1231, the nation of Farqîn was in goodness and pleasantness, from every side it was wealthy, with agriculture and raising of sheep and cattle it was very wealthy, likewise with reading and science and memorization of hadith and the Quran.

875. Êrîşên tetera bi serokatîya Holako hatin welatê Kurdistanê û misilmanan û şar û gund wêran kirin, milet kuştin, malên wan û jinên wan talan û berebat kirin.
875. The attacks of the Tatars under the leadership of Hulagu came to the country of Kurdistan and the Muslims and ruined cities and villages, killed the nation, plundered and desolated their homes and their women.

876. Mir Mamed (Al-Kamil) gelekî mêr û mêrxas bû û leşkerên wî hebûn, bajarê xwe di hundirê sûrê de diparastin.
876. Mîr Mamed (Al-Kamil) was a very manly and brave man and had his soldiers, they protected their city inside the wall.

877. Holako û artêşa xwe ya giran du meha hawîrdora bajêr dorpêç kirin û tu çiq di mîr de nekirin, rabû artêşa xwe hilanî û berê xwe da Heleb û Şamê, û kurê xwe Eşmût li şûna xwe hişt, û nehiştin ne yek here bajêr û ne yek jê derkeve, ango bajar ma dorpêçkiri.
877. Hulagu and his heavy army besieged the surroundings of the city for two months and made no dent in the mîr, he got up, lifted his army and turned his direction to Aleppo and Damascus, and left his son Ashmut in his place, and they let neither one go to the city nor one come out of it, that is to say the city remained besieged.

878. Ev rewş salû şeş mehan dirêj kir, xwarin û vexwarin, pez û dewar giş qelîyan û çek û alîkarî jî jê re ji mîrek û merivan wek Al-Melik El-Nasir, Şeref û Moxîs û xeynî wan nehat.
878. This situation extended for a year and six months, food and drink, sheep and cattle were all exhausted and weapons and help also did not come to him from any mîr and relatives like Al-Malik Al-Nasir, Sharaf and Mughis and others besides them.

879. Piştî çek û xwarin neman, artêşa Eşmût ket hundirê bajêr û sûr û keleh herifandin û ketin nav milet de zilamekî sax neheştin, û jinên wan berebat kirin û Eşmût berê xwe da Helebê û Mîr Mamed (Al-Kamil) di qeyd û bendan de anî cem Holako.
879. After weapons and food were no more, Ashmut's army entered inside the city and collapsed the wall and castle and fell among the nation, they did not leave a man alive, and they desolated their women and Ashmut turned his direction to Aleppo and brought Mîr Mamed (Al-Kamil) in fetters and bindings to Hulagu.

880. Holako ew birçî û tazî dikir û dihişt bi zorê goştê laşê xwe bixwe, ji laşê wî jê dikir û dixiste devê wî de, û bi vî halî mir û xwe berdest nekir, û xwe nekir koleyê Holako wek gelekan ji Şêx, meşayix, derebeg û pêşkêşên ola misilmanan.
880. Hulagu was making him hungry and naked and letting him by force eat the meat of his own body, cutting from his body and putting it into his mouth, and in this state he died and did not surrender himself, and did not make himself Hulagu's slave like many of the Şêxes, elders, lords and leaders of the Islamic religion.

881. Piştî dema Holako çû, milet bi ser xwe ve hat.
881. After Hulagu's time passed, the nation came back to itself.

882. Sal û sal derbas bûn û mexolî careke din bi serokatiya Cengizxan hatin û welatê Kurdistanê careke din dagîr, talan û wêran kirin.
882. Years and years passed and the Mongols once again under the leadership of Genghis Khan came and occupied, plundered and ruined the country of Kurdistan once again.

883. Û miletê kurd tim û tim ma bindest ji firsa, ji romanî û selçûqîyan; ma bindestê ereb û misilmanan, ma jar û belengaz û çavên gelê kurd venebûn û kurd nebûn xwedî dewlet.
883. And the Kurdish nation always and always remained oppressed by the Persians, by the Romans and Seljuks; remained oppressed by the Arabs and Muslims, remained miserable and destitute, and the eyes of the Kurdish people did not open and the Kurds did not become owners of a state.

884. Kengî zanayek rabûba û bigota ez kurd im li nav çavên wî dixistin û mal û gundên wî talan û wêran dikirin.
884. Whenever a wise man would rise and say I am a Kurd they would strike between his eyes and plunder and ruin his house and villages.

885. Ji kevin de bi dehê şoreşên kurdan rabûne û derebegî çêkirine û wêran bûne, wekî Îmara Merwanîyan, Tahir Bababan û Bedirxanîyan; û şoreşên ji sed salî û bi vir de jî bi dehan e.
885. From ancient times tens of Kurdish revolutions have risen and made principalities and been ruined, like the Emirate of Marwanids, Tahir Babans and Bedirkhans; and the revolutions from a hundred years to here too are by the tens.

886. Piştî Şerê Çaldîranê di sala 1514an de, li ser erda Kurdistanê di orta osmanî û sefewîyan de Kurdistan careke din hat talankirin û wêrankirin û miletê wê ma jar û bindest.
886. After the Battle of Chaldiran in the year 1514, on the land of Kurdistan between the Ottomans and Safavids, Kurdistan was once again plundered and ruined and its nation remained miserable and oppressed.

887. Bi dehnê salan derbas bûn heya milet careke din bi ser xwe ve hat û dest bi avakirina bajar û gundan kir û aborîya wan bere
887. Tens of years passed until the nation once again came back to itself and started building cities and villages and their economy gradually

888. bere xweş bû, bi çandinîyê ji genim û ceh û daristan û werza, û xwedîkirina dewar û pez û tilûran.
888. became pleasant, with agriculture from wheat and barley and forests and fields, and raising of cattle and sheep and fowls.

889. Di vê demê de gundê (şarê wêranbûye) Farqînê bûye gundê Silîvayê û gundî hêdî hêdî dest bi cot û cobara kirine û pez û dewaran xwedî dikin.
889. In this time the village (the ruined city) of Farqîn has become the village of Silîva and the villagers slowly have started plowing and farming and raise sheep and cattle.

890. Di vî halî û warî de gernasek di vî gundî de derket, ji nevîyên wa mêrxas û gernasên berê ku bi mêranî du salan li ser hev şerê xwe li dijî Holako kirin heya tiştekî wan nema ye, ne av, ne xwarin, ne cil û ne berg, ne çek û şûr, ne pez û dewar, man li azîyê bêbavê Eşmûtê kurê Holako yê ku sûr û kele herifandin û milet kuşt û talan û berebat kir.
890. In this state and domain a hero came out in this village, from the descendants of those former braves and heroes who with manliness for two years on end fought their war against Hulagu until nothing of theirs remained, neither water, nor food, nor clothes and nor garments, neither weapons and swords, nor sheep and cattle, they remained at the agony of the fatherless Ashmut, son of Hulagu, who collapsed walls and castles and killed the nation and plundered and desolated.

891. Kurek nû çêbû li Silîva, nevîyê wan gernasan bi navê Sîyamend.
891. A new boy was born in Silîva, the descendant of those heroes by the name of Sîyamend.

892. Sîyamend sêwî ye bê dê û bav e, li ber destên ap û amojina bi qerwaşî mezin bûye.
892. Sîyamend is an orphan without mother and father, he has grown up under the hands of his uncle and aunt with servitude.

893. ## Siyamendê Silîva
893. ## Sîyamend of Silîva
