1229. Omer Beg: Since it is so, I will give a comfortable and light work before you.

1230. Gurî: Wek çi?
1230. Gurî: Like what?

1231. Omer Begê: Niha du hespên min hene bi nav û deng in, û du sayis li ber wan in, tu dikarî hema bi zimanê xwe ji wan re bibêjî wilo bikin, wilo mihes bikin, wilo cele bidin wan, hema çavê te li wan be û hew.
1231. Omer Beg: Now I have two horses they are with name and fame, and two grooms are before them, you can just with your tongue say to them do so, groom them so, give them fodder so, just let your eye be upon them and that is all.

1232. Gurî: Ez birazîyê te me, ji bavê wan zêde ye, li wan ne miqate bin.
1232. Gurî: I am your nephew, it is more than their father, lest they not be careful with them.

1233. Gurî bû fermandarê her du sayisan.
1233. Gurî became the commander of both grooms.

1234. Demek dirêj neçû Gurî bala xwe da her du sayisa û çavdêrî li wan kir, dît ku yek ji her duyan wê têkeve imbara (çala) ceh, wê du olçaka derxîne, wê
1234. A long time did not go (pass) Gurî gave his attention to both grooms and observed them, saw that one of the two will enter the storehouse (pit) of barley, will take out two measures, will

1235. yekê bide hespa û yekê bidize bibe malê.
1235. give one to the horses and steal one and take it to the house.

1236. Ne rok û dido û ne deh, Gurî nas kir ku mêrik dizekî eşkere ye.
1236. Not one day and two and not ten, Gurî recognized that the man is a clear thief.

1237. Gurî xist dilê xwe de û bi dizî çavdêrî li wan kir.
1237. Gurî put it in his heart and secretly observed them.

1238. Sibehekê yek ji wan kete imbara ceh û du olçak derxistin, yek xist ber hespa û olçaka din li pişta xwe kir û berê xwe da malê.
1238. One morning one of them entered the storehouse of barley and took out two measures, put one before the horses and put the other measure on his back and turned his direction to the house.

1239. Hema Gurî ji pişt dîwêr ve derket û bi qerpika histê wî girt û jê re got: "Mere ev çima hûn dizîyê dikin?
1239. Just Gurî came out from behind the wall and grabbed the nape of his neck and said to him: "Man why do you do theft?

1240. Ma ev ne xinezî ye", û çîplaqa xwe ji ber xwe derxist û di newqê de lê xist zîzikand erdê, ew jî kuşt.
1240. After all is this not treachery", and took out his sharp dagger from his side and struck him in the waist and dropped him whizzing to the ground, he killed him too.

1241. Navmalîyan, rêncberan bazdan bi ber kuşka Omer Beg de û jê re gotin, "wele Gurî yek ji sayisê hespa jî kuşt".
1241. The household, the laborers ran before the mansion of Omer Beg and said to him, "by God Gurî killed one of the grooms of the horses too".

1242. Gurî anîn kuşka Omer Beg ji bo dadkirinê.
1242. They brought Gurî to the mansion of Omer Beg for judging.

1243. Omer Beg: Gurî law, ev çi bela te ye kuro?
1243. Omer Beg: Gurî boy, what calamity of yours is this boy?

1244. Çima te ew kuşt?
1244. Why did you kill him?

1245. Gurî: Xuya ye zilamên pîs û xiniz tu ji wan hez dike, ezbenî wele dizîya te dikir.
1245. Gurî: It is apparent dirty and treacherous men you like them, sir by God he was doing your theft (stealing from you).

1246. Omer Beg: dizîya min çilo kuro?
1246. Omer Beg: my theft how boy?

1247. Gurî: Wê yek ji wan têkeve imbara ceh, du olçak tanîn yek didan hespa û olçaka din dibir malê, ne rok û ne deh û ne bîst, wele namûsa min got, bikuje.
1247. Gurî: One of them will enter the storehouse of barley, they brought two measures they gave one to the horses and he took the other measure to the house, not one day and not ten and not twenty, by God my honor said, kill him.

1248. Omer Beg: Gurî law, wele ez te pîs nakim di odeya xwe de û di nav gundîyê xwe de, xuya ye tu zilamekî bi namûs e, bux û vexwe, tu bi kêfa xwe yî.
1248. Omer Beg: Gurî boy, by God I do not dirty you in my room and among my villagers, it is apparent you are a man with honor, eat and drink, you are by your pleasure.

1249. Gurî ma bi kêfa xwe, ode û dîwan dagîr kir, tu kes ne ji gundîyan û ne ji rêncber û navmalîyan newêre îşê xwe jê bîne, yan bibêje sîya te xwar e.
1249. Gurî remained by his pleasure, he occupied the room and court, no one neither from the villagers nor from the laborers and household dares to bring their business from him (cross him), or say your shadow is crooked.

1250. Gurî ma bi dest xwe ve, birjîne, bavêje, bû fermandarê hemî xulaman.
1250. Gurî remained by his own hand, let him spill, let him throw, he became the commander of all the servants.

1251. Girtin û berdan, kar û îş man di bin çavdêrîya Gurî de.
1251. Catching and releasing, work and business remained under the observation of Gurî.

1252. Gurî têr xwar û vexwar, cilên nû li xwe kirin, li ser dikê rûdinê û şivka xêzeran dihejîne û fermanan di ber re dide, kuro wilo bik, kuro sewalê xwe derxîn çolê, kuro hespê mêvana girê din, kuro ka kulava raxin, kuro...kuroo...
1252. Gurî ate and drank to satisfaction, put new clothes on himself, he sits on the raised platform and shakes the bamboo rod and gives commands alongside, boy do so, boy take your livestock out to the wilderness, boy tie the horses of the guests, boy well lay out the felt rugs, boy...boyyy...

1253. Hino hino bû cîgirê Omer Begê, serokê xulam û rêncberan.
1253. Little by little he became the deputy of Omer Beg, the head of the servants and laborers.

1254. Gruî madê wî xweş bû, qelew bû, qerpka histê wî qalind bû, çavsor û gewî bû, kes nikare jê re bibêje hikê bilê, yan pozê sola te xwar e.
1254. Gurî his mood was pleasant, he became fat, the nape of his neck became thick, he became red-eyed (fierce) and stout, no one can say to him hikê bilê (a word of protest), or the nose of your shoe is crooked.

1255. ## Bu Bihar
1255. ## It Became Spring

1256. Roj derbas bûn û demsal hatin guhertin, piştî sar û serma, berf û barana, şînkayî û xweşî tê.
1256. Days passed and seasons were changed, after cold and chill, snow and rains, greenery and pleasantness comes.

1257. Dunya germ dibe gul û gîya, çîçek û nêrgiz şîn dibin û rengarenga bîna xweş bi avîya serê sibê re belav dikin.
1257. The world becomes warm roses and grass, flowers and narcissus become green (sprout) and spread their colorful pleasant scent with the dew of early morning.

1258. Rojek germ û xweş, çîvaçîva çûk û çivîka ye, awaz û stranên şarûl û bilbila, bîna biharê, bîna bihuştê, bîna gul û gîya û çîçek û nêrgiza, qada Xwedê giş raxistîye, ji şînkayê, weke bereke evemî rengarenga ye kesk û sor û zer dilerizîne li ezmana û li nav taxê gula, tu dibê wey perçak ji perçê bihuştê daketîye ser qada Xwedê.
1258. A warm and pleasant day, it is the chirping of birds and sparrows, the tunes and songs of starlings and nightingales, the scent of spring, the scent of paradise, the scent of roses and grass and flowers and narcissus, it has spread out all over God's field, from greenery, it is like an awesome colorful carpet green and red and yellow vibrates in the sky and among the neighborhood of roses, you say alas a piece from the piece of paradise has come down upon God's field.

1259. Di rojeke wilo geş û xweş de Gurî li ser dikê rûniştî bû çavdêrîya xulama dikir, carekê dît ku Elîfê qîza Omer Begê û cêrîya xwe xemilandî, hêdî hêdî bi nazikî ber bi bexçeyê bavê xwe de diçe.
1259. On such a bright and pleasant day Gurî was seated on the raised platform he was doing the observation of the servants, at once he saw that Elîf the daughter of Omer Beg and her maid adorned, slowly with delicacy go towards her father's garden.

1260. Gurî tamarên dilê wî lê xistin û şewqek xwezayî ji dila derket û rastî tîrêja dilê Elîfê Xanim hat.
1260. Gurî the veins of his heart struck and a natural light came out from the heart and met the ray of the heart of Elîf Xanim.

1261. Gurî çeng bû ji nişkê ve û rabû ser xwe spîya sekinî û temaşeyî Elîfê kir, hiş û aqil avêt, û dilê wî lerizî ji eşq û evînîyê.
1261. Gurî jerked up suddenly and got up on himself (stood up) stood completely still and watched Elîf, he threw mind and reason (lost his mind), and his heart trembled from passion and love.

1262. Di dilê xwe de got: "Ku vegerîya ez ê herim pêşîyê, bê ez ramîsanekê jê nastînim", û hêdî hêdî daket û berê xwe da bexçeyê Omer Begê, çû çû nêzîkî derîyê bexçe li ser tingekî rûnişt û ma li hêvîya Elîfê.
1262. In his heart he said: "When she returned I will go before her, let's see if I do not take a kiss from her", and slowly he came down and turned his direction to the garden of Omer Beg, went went near the door of the garden sat on a ledge and remained waiting for Elîf.

1263. Elîfê û cêrîya xwe vegerîyan ji nav bexçeyî, dîtin ku Gurî li ser tingekî li ser devê rê ye.
1263. Elîf and her maid returned from inside the garden, they saw that Gurî is on a ledge on the mouth of the road.

1264. Elîfê li carîya xwe zîvirî û got: Keçê Henîfê, ev ne Gurîyê me ye li devê rê de?
1264. Elîf turned to her maid and said: Girl Henîf, is this not our Gurî on the mouth of the road?

1265. Henîfa: Xatûna min qey pêdiviyeke wî bi te heye, ya wê tiştekî bixwaze.
1265. Henîfa: My lady perhaps he has a need with you, or he will want something.

1266. Elîfê û carîyê rêya xwe ji ser Gurî hinekî dagerandin.
1266. Elîf and the maid deviated their road a little from upon Gurî.

1267. Gurî rabû û çû kete pêşîya wan de careke din.
1267. Gurî got up and went fell before them once again.

1268. Elîfê û carîyê nêzîkayî lê kirin.
1268. Elîf and the maid approached him.

1269. Elîfe: Gurî te xêr e tu hatî pêşîya min û devê rê sekinîye, çi pêdivîyên te hene?
1269. Elîf: Gurî what is your goodness (what is the matter) you came before me and stood at the mouth of the road, what needs do you have?

1270. Gurî: Wele Elîfê ez hatime ji bo tu ramîsanekê bide min.
1270. Gurî: By God Elîf I have come for you to give me a kiss.

1271. Elîfê: Hêêê, ez Elîfê qîza Omer Begê, xwedîyê sî û sê gundê qontara çîya, û tu îro ji min dixwaze ramîsanê.
1271. Elîf: Heee, I Elîf the daughter of Omer Beg, owner of thirty-three villages of the foothills of the mountain, and you today want a kiss from me.

1272. Gurîyo, çepelo, mirdalo, dûr keve ji devê rê.
1272. Gurî, filthy one, carrion, fall far from the mouth of the road.

1273. Bi navê Xwedê ku tu vexwe ava satilê, tê biherimîne wê satilê.
1273. By the name of God if you drink the water of the bucket, you will defile that bucket.

1274. Gurî: Hêêê, Elîfê qîza Omer Begê xwedîyê sî û sê gundê qontara çîyê, erê Elîfê, bejna min zirav e, takrîhana li takî bera soza Xwedê li min neketibe, ji niha û ne deren, wê ramîsanê te li cem min bên ne bi perakî.
1274. Gurî: Heee, Elîf daughter of Omer Beg owner of thirty-three villages of the foothills of the mountain, yes Elîf, my figure is slender, a sprig of basil on a sprig lest the promise of God have fallen upon me, from now and not late, those kisses of yours will come by me not with a single penny (for free).

1275. Û Gurî berê xwe dagerand, hat ser dika odeyê û Elîfê û carîya xwe berê xwe dan alîyê malê.
1275. And Gurî turned his direction back, came onto the raised platform of the room and Elîf and her maid turned their direction to the side of the house.

1276. ## Bêş û Baca dewletê ji gunda
1276. ## State Tax and Toll from the villages

1277. Dibêjin di wî zemanî de Ehmed Begê serokê başbazirganê bêşa dewletê bi fermana sultanê dewletê Ehmed Begê bazirgan kar kirîye û li gund û bajarokan digere ku bêşa salê bistîne.
1277. They say in that time Ehmed Beg the head of the chief merchants of the state tax with the command of the sultan of the state merchant Ehmed Beg worked and wanders the villages and towns to take the yearly tax.

1278. Omer Begê jî bêşa sî û sê gundê xwe daye hev û kom kirîye, li hêvîya başbazirganê salêy e ku vê bêşê bibe pêşîya Ehmed Begê, serokê bazirganê dewletê.
1278. Omer Beg too has gathered and collected the tax of his thirty-three villages, he is waiting for the chief merchant of the year to take this tax before Ehmed Beg, the head of the state merchants.

1279. Dema ku Omer Begê bihîst ku Ehmed Begê nêzîk bûye, bi bazirganê salê ye, fermanî ser çend zilamên navdar û berbiçav kit, li hespa siwar bûn û bêşên xwe li qantiran kirin û çûne bi pêşîya bazirgan, qene bêşa xwe bidin dest Ehmed Begê.
1279. When Omer Beg heard that Ehmed Beg has approached, he is with the merchant of the year, he commanded upon several famous and prominent men, they mounted the horses and loaded their taxes on the mules and went before the merchant, so that they give their tax to the hand of Ehmed Beg.

1280. Gurî jî berê xwe da tewi xanê bergîlek derxist û qûşa kurtan xiste qirikê û rişme xiste bin terîyê û beroçeqî (vajî) lê siwar bû û da nav siwara.
1280. Gurî too turned his direction to the stable brought out a packhorse and put the crupper of the packsaddle on its throat and put the halter under its tail and mounted it backwards (in reverse) and went among the riders.

1281. Bi rê de, gundîyan, siwaran wa nerîn ku Qirdikê Qudoş bi çi halî daye nav wa, ji Omer Begê re gotin, "axe tu li vi Qirdikê Qudoş biner, wê me
1281. On the road, the villagers, the riders looked there that in what state Qirdikê Qudoş has come among them, they said to Omer Beg, "agha you look at this Qirdikê Qudoş, he will

1282. bihetikîne li nav xelkê û li pêşîya Ehmed Begê, başbazirganê salê", Omer Begê lê vegerîya û got:
1282. shame us among the people and before Ehmed Beg, the chief merchant of the year", Omer Beg turned to him and said:

1283. Omer Begê: Kuro Gurî, ev çi bela tey e?
1283. Omer Beg: Boy Gurî, what calamity of yours is this?

1284. Vegere mal wê xelk henekê xwe bi me bikin.
1284. Return home the people will make their joke of us (mock us).

1285. Gurî: Wele ez venagerim, ez ê jî bêm başbazirgan bibînim.
1285. Gurî: By God I am not returning, I too will come see the chief merchant.

1286. Omer Begê: Kuro ez ji te re dibêjim veger law, qey xwîna te ketîye çavê te de?
1286. Omer Beg: Boy I say to you return boy, has your blood fallen into your eye?

1287. Gurî: Wele tu min bikujî, ez venagerim.
1287. Gurî: By God even if you kill me, I am not returning.

1288. Omer Begê: "Kuro veger", û hat li hember Gurî sekinî, ji qehra sîlak lê xist, û da pêşîya siwara û meşîya, Gurî jî da nav wan û kudand.
1288. Omer Beg: "Boy return", and came stood opposite Gurî, from anger struck a slap on him, and went before the riders and walked, Gurî too went among them and spurred on.

1289. Omer Begê li siwara zîvirî û got: "Meriv, ka em çilo bikin ji Gurî?"
1289. Omer Beg turned to the riders and said: "Men, well how shall we do about Gurî?"

1290. Gundî û siwar: A baş ew e ku em bêşê bidin dest Gurî û bila ew bibe ji Ehmed Begê re, belkî daqlîçî hev bibin, Ehmed Begê wî bikuje, me jê xelas bike.
1290. Villagers and riders: The good thing is that we give the tax to Gurî's hand and let him take it for Ehmed Beg, perhaps they will clash with each other, Ehmed Beg kills him, saves us from him.

1291. Omer Begê: "Guri, Gurî, hela wer", Gurî bergîlê xwe vegerand û hat.
1291. Omer Beg: "Gurî, Gurî, come here", Gurî returned his packhorse and came.

1292. Gurî: Ferman bike begê min.
1292. Gurî: Command my beg.

1293. Omer Begê: Gurî tu nayê ku em vê bêşê bidin te û tu bibe ji başbazirgan re.
1293. Omer Beg: Gurî will you not come that we give this tax to you and you take it for the chief merchant.

1294. Gurî: Belê wele ez ê bibim, lê mercekî min bi te re heye.
1294. Gurî: Yes by God I will take it, but I have a condition with you.

1295. Omer Begê: Şert û mercê te çi ne Gurî?
1295. Omer Beg: What are your terms and conditions Gurî?

1296. Gurî: Şert û mercê min evi n: tê hespê xwe bide min û şûr û mertal û rima te.
1296. Gurî: My terms and conditions are these: you will give your horse to me and your sword and shield and spear.

1297. Omer Begê: Ku min ev giş dan te, tê çilo bike?
1297. Omer Beg: If I gave all these to you, how will you do?

1298. Gurî: Ez ê bêşê bibim jê re bi navê te, heger girt ez ê vegerim û heger negirt jî ez ê vegerim.
1298. Gurî: I will take the tax to him with your name, if he took it I will return and if he did not take it too I will return.

1299. Omer Begê: Bela te li te keve Gurî, ah ji te hespê min û şûr û mertal û rima xêzeran jî.
1299. Omer Beg: May your calamity fall upon you Gurî, ah for you my horse and sword and shield and bamboo spear too.

1300. Gurî li hespê Omer Begê siwar bû û şûr xiste histê xwe û mertalê xwe bi maregê ve daliqand û rima xêzeranî ya dozdehmovik bi dest xwe ve vegirt û hejand û berê xwe da pêşîya başbazirgan.
1300. Gurî mounted Omer Beg's horse and put the sword on his neck and hung his shield on the saddle-bow and gripped the twelve-jointed bamboo spear in his hand and shook it and turned his direction before the chief merchant.

1301. Omer Begê û gundî û siwarê pê re vegerîyan malê ji hev re dibêjin, "belkî Xwedê ye, Ehmed Begê wî bikuje me jê xelas bike bi carekê re".
1301. Omer Beg and the villagers and the riders with him returned home they say to each other, "perhaps it is God, Ehmed Beg kills him saves us from him at once".

1302. Gurî siwar e li xwe dinere û li cil û çekê li xwe dinere, di dilê xwe de got: "Mane min berê soz û peyman daye, soz û biryara Xwedê li can û cesedê min ketibe: Heya a xerab hebe, ez tu carî nakim a çê".
1302. Gurî is mounted he looks at himself and looks at the clothes and weapons on himself, in his heart he said: "For I have previously given a promise and pact, let the promise and decision of God have fallen upon my soul and body: As long as the bad exists, I never do the good".

1303. Û çû çû li pêşîya bazirgan sekinî û rima xwe di erdê de çikiland û kila û rawestîya di tenga rê de.
1303. And went went stood before the merchant and planted his spear in the ground and brandished it and stopped in the narrowness of the road.

1304. Ehmed Begê: Law Egîto wa siwarek di tenga rê de rawestîya ye, here bê çi daxwaza wî heye, heger mêr kuştibin, jin revandibin, çi kiribe, jê re bibêje, qantire pêşî tev li barê wê ji te re ye, ev adet e.
1304. Ehmed Beg: Boy Egîto there a rider has stopped in the narrowness of the road, go see what request he has, if he has killed men, has abducted women, whatever he has done, say to him, the first mule together with its load is for you, this is custom.

1305. Egîto li hespê siwar bû û da çargavê, çû cem Gurî û jê re got: "Çi pêdiviya te hebe, te çi kiribe, axê min gotîye, qantira pêşî tev barê xwe ji te re ye.
1305. Egîto mounted the horse and set it to gallop, went to Gurî and said to him: "Whatever need you have, whatever you have done, my agha has said, the first mule together with its load is for you.

1306. Gurî: Siwaro, here bêje axê xwe ku ne nîvê bazirgan be ez qayil nabim.
1306. Gurî: Rider, go say to your agha that if it is not half the caravan I will not be satisfied.

1307. Egît: Vegerîya hat ji Ehmed Begê re wilo got: "Nîvê bazirgan dixwaze".
1307. Egît: He returned came said so to Ehmed Beg: "He wants half the caravan".

1308. Ehmed Beg: Ev çi kese?
1308. Ehmed Beg: What person is this?

1309. Çi bela wî ye?
1309. What is his calamity?

1310. Yekî çilo ye?
1310. What kind of one is he?

1311. Egît: Yekî serçav bi xurî ye, gurî ye, mirûskirêt e hema zebenî hebin ev ew e.
1311. Egît: He is one with face with sores, he is scabby, he is ugly-featured just if demons exist this is him.

1312. Ehmed Begê: De xem nake, belkî tu wî qayil bike, jê re bike du qantir, sê qantir.
1312. Ehmed Beg: Then it makes no worry, perhaps you satisfy him, make it two mules, three mules for him.

1313. Egît lê vegerîya û gotina axê jê re got.
1313. Egît returned to him and said the agha's word to him.

1314. Guri: Pismam gotina min yek e, nabe dido, nîvê bazirganê ji min re û nîvî ji wî re, em ê wek du bira li hev par bikin, bera ne qantirek min zêdeyî wî be, û ne qantirek wî zêdeyî min be, de her wilo bêje.
1314. Gurî: Cousin my word is one, it does not become two, half of the caravan for me and half for him, we will share with each other like two brothers, let not one mule of mine be more than his, and let not one mule of his be more than mine, then go say so.

1315. Egît vegerîya û gotinnê Gurî jê re şirove kirin.
1315. Egît returned and explained Gurî's words to him.

1316. Ehmed Beg: Îro çi roj e?
1316. Ehmed Beg: Today what day is it?

1317. Çi bela hatîye pêşîya me?
1317. What calamity has come before us?

1318. Ya Rebî, ya Xwedêyo!
1318. O Lord, o God!

1319. Law Egîto here jê re bike pênc û deh jî belkî qayil bibe.
1319. Boy Egîto go make it five and ten too for him perhaps he will be satisfied.

1320. Egîtê reben careke din vegerîya û gotinên axayê xwe jê re pêşkêş kirin bi hesanî.
1320. Wretched Egît once again returned and presented the words of his agha to him easily (softly).

1321. Gurî: Pismam, veger çi heqê te li nefsa te heye, here bila axê te bê.
1321. Gurî: Cousin, return what right do you have upon your soul (why risk yourself), go let your agha come.

1322. Bi vî hawî bi çûn û hatin bazirgan bi rê de ye, nêzîkayî lê kirin.
1322. In this manner with going and coming the caravan is on the road, they approached him.

1323. Ehmed Beg: Hêêê, lolo siwarê li tenga rêê, law ma tu natirse ji Xwedê, law siwaro, tu îro herimîye, tu ketîye tenga rê.
1323. Ehmed Beg: Heee, lolo rider on the narrowness of the road, boy do you not fear God, boy rider, today you have become defiled, you have fallen to the narrowness of the road.

1324. Û tu îro ji min dixwaze nîvê bazirgana dewletê, mane fermana serê min e.
1324. And today you want from me half the caravans of the state, for it is the command of my head (my life is at stake).

1325. Ma tu nizane ev başbazirganê dewletê ye?
1325. After all do you not know this is the chief merchant of the state?

1326. Lo lo siwaro, çi xwîna te ketîye çavê te, tu rima xêzeranê vê sibê dikilê, lolo siwaro, heger zengilê paşî li zengilê pêşî bizengile û qantira paşî li qantira pêşî bisekine, lolo siwaro malê dewletê ye, fermanadarê min e lolo...oyoyox.
1326. Lo lo rider, how has your blood fallen into your eye, you brandish the bamboo spear this morning, lolo rider, if the rear bell rings against the front bell and the rear mule stops against the front mule, lolo rider it is the wealth of the state, he is my commander lolo...oyoyox.

1327. Gurî: Lo lo siwaro Ehmed Begê, tu min nas nakî, ez Gurî me, Gurîyê Qedê, min sûnd xwarîye bi soz û peymanê Xwedê heya ya xerab hebe, ez nakim ya çê.
1327. Gurî: Lo lo rider Ehmed Beg, you do not recognize me, I am Gurî, Gurî of the Calamity, I have sworn an oath by the promise and pact of God as long as the bad exists, I do not do the good.

1328. Ehmed Begê: Law siwaro, vê sibê tê bela xwe ji me veke ji bo Xwedê.
1328. Ehmed Beg: Boy rider, this morning you will untie your calamity from us for God's sake.

1329. Xulam û karmendê bazirgan feqîr in, zarokên wan birçî ne li malê.
1329. The servants and officials of the caravan are poor, their children are hungry at home.

1330. Gurî: Tu îşê min tune ye, ne ji xulaman, ne ji xizmetkaran, xulam lawê xelkê ne, ez ji te dixwazim malê dewletê nîvê bazirganê salê.
1330. Gurî: I have no business, neither with the servants, nor with the attendants, the servants are the sons of the people, I want from you the wealth of the state half the caravan of the year.

1331. Yek ji Gurî yek ji Ehmed Begê, gotinên wan bi ber hev de hatin.
1331. One from Gurî one from Ehmed Beg, their words came before each other.

1332. Ji hev re daketin meydanê (tiradê).
1332. They came down to the square (arena) for each other.

1333. Gurî li hespê Omer Begê ye û Ehmed Begê li Demirqeranê siwar e û lahorê kuştinê di husta de ye û rima xêziran di dest de ye, hespê wî xurt e, mêrik li xwe û hespê xwe ewle ye, ji Gurî natirse.
1333. Gurî is on Omer Beg's horse and Ehmed Beg is mounted on Demirqeran and the scimitar of killing is on his neck and the bamboo spear is in his hand, his horse is strong, the man is secure in himself and his horse, he does not fear Gurî.

1334. Daketin tiradê, di meydanê de çûn û hatin, hespê xwe gerim kirin, şûha yekê ya didwan ajotin bi alîyê hev de, di şûha sisîya de Demirqeran derfet ji hespê Gurî stand û da ser piştê.
1334. They came down to the arena, they went and came in the square, they warmed their horses, the first charge the second they drove to each other's side, in the third charge Demirqeran took the opportunity from Gurî's horse and put him on his back (overtook him).

1335. Gurî bala xwe dayê ku Demirqeran beza ye, qîrek li hespê xwe kir û got: "Ya Xwedanê şev û rojê û xewna nîvê şevê", û bi zengwa li nav tenga hespê xwe da.
1335. Gurî gave his attention to it that Demirqeran is fast, he made a shout at his horse and said: "O Master of night and day and the dream of midnight", and struck with the stirrups into the flanks of his horse.

1336. Hespê Omer Begê jî hespekî bi nav û deng e, tu hesp bi siwarê xwe ve, nagihêjin toza wî.
1336. Omer Beg's horse too is a horse with name and fame, no horse with its rider, reaches his dust.

1337. Dema Gurî lê qûrîya, hesp rabû ser her du nigên paşî û di cih de li Demirqeran zîvirî, Demirqeran ji ber telaq bû û bezî û Gurî pişt ji Ehmed Begê stand û wî da ser piştê.
1337. When Gurî spurred him on, the horse rose on both hind legs and in place turned on Demirqeran, Demirqeran became startled before him and ran and Gurî took the back from Ehmed Beg (gained the advantage) and put him on his back (got behind him).

1338. Demirqeran bi bezê xurt e, di bazdanê de lê hespê Gurî zêde dikir, Gurî nas kir bi bezê nagihêjê, rabû spîya ser zengwê û rima dozdehmovik kila kila û ji kel û bi hêrs ji par ve avêt Ehmed Begê, di orta her du qilocan de lê xist, buhust û çar tilîya di defa sînga wî re derxist.
1338. Demirqeran is strong in running, in running away he was increasing upon Gurî's horse, Gurî recognized he does not reach him by running, he rose completely straight on the stirrups and brandished the twelve-jointed spear and from boiling and with anger threw it from behind at Ehmed Beg, struck him in the middle of both shoulder blades, brought it out a span and four fingers through the drum of his chest.

1339. Ehmed Begê ji ser Demirqeran hat xwarê, mirîtî li erdê dirêj bû, Gurî di ser re sekinî, rahişt lahorê wî xiste histê xwe û Demirqeran destkêşî xwe kir û da dû bazirgan û berî da gundê Omer Begê.
1339. Ehmed Beg came down from upon Demirqeran, he stretched out dead on the ground, Gurî stood above him, picked up his scimitar put it on his neck and made Demirqeran hand-led for himself and went behind the caravan and turned the direction to Omer Beg's village.

1340. Şivana, gavana, xulama bazdan ber bi kuşka Omer Begê de û jê re gotin, "Gurî Ehmed Begê, başbazirganê dewletê kuşt û wa bazirgan daye pêşîya xwe û berî daye gund".
1340. The shepherds, the herdsmen, the servants ran towards Omer Beg's mansion and said to him, "Gurî killed Ehmed Beg, the chief merchant of the state and there he has put the caravan before himself and turned the direction to the village".

1341. Omer Begê ji tirsa dewletê û talanîya bazirganê bêşa salê, bê hiş û sewdan ji kuşkê derket û bi alîyê gundîyan de bazda, pêxwas sertazî, tena kiras û çû pêşîya Gurî.
1341. Omer Beg from the fear of the state and the pillaging of the merchant of the yearly tax, without mind and senses came out of the mansion and ran to the side of the villagers, barefoot bareheaded, only a shirt and went before Gurî.

1342. Omer Begê got: "Law wele ku vegere bêna rih bi min ve jî nahêle, gava din min şeqamek lê xistibû, de hema bi destê min bigirin, pêxwas û ser serqot bibin pêşîyê, belkî min bibexşîne ji bo wê şeqamê”.
1342. Omer Beg said: "Boy by God if he returns he will not leave a breath of soul attached to me either, the other time I had struck a slap on him, then just take me by the hand, take me barefoot and bareheaded before him, perhaps he will forgive me for that slap”.

1343. Gurî û bazirgan tên bi alîyê gund de û gundî û Omer Begê diçûn
1343. Gurî and the caravan come to the side of the village and the villagers and Omer Beg were going

1344. ber bi wa de, nêzîkayî li hev kirin, Gurî ji hespê xwe peya bû û hat pêşîya Omer Begê û rahişt destê wî û maç kir û xeyidî û got: "Ev çima te wilo li serê xwe kirîye?
1344. towards them, they approached each other, Gurî dismounted from his horse and came before Omer Beg and picked up his hand and kissed it and became angry and said: "Why have you done so to your head (to yourself)?

1345. Hema tu apê min bû li şûna bavê min bû û te sewtak li min xist, ma çi çêbû?"
1345. You were just my uncle in place of my father and you struck a blow to me, after all what happened?"

1346. Giş bi hev re vegerîyan malê û Omer Begê li hespê siwar kirin û wî û Gurî dan pêşîya gundîya û kerwanê bazirganê dewletê; û gundî hemî derketine ser xanîyan, ber dîwaran, ser sergoyan.
1346. All together returned home and they mounted Omer Beg on the horse and put him and Gurî before the villagers and the caravan of the state merchant; and the villagers all have gone out onto the houses, before the walls, on the dung heaps.

1347. Pîr, kal, jin, mêr, zilam, zarok, qîz û keçik giş derketine û li Gurî û kerwanê talankirî temaşe dikin û her yek tiştekî dibêje.
1347. Old women, old men, women, men, males, children, girls and young girls all have gone out and watch Gurî and the plundered caravan and each says something.

1348. xibe xibe, qerebalix e, lîrelîr e, hema qîr û qiyamet e.
1348. it is bustling, it is crowded, it is trilling, it is just shouting and resurrection (chaos).

1349. Siwar û peya, gundî û kerwanê bazirganîyê dan dû hev bi dû Omer Begê û Gurî de berê xwe dane gund, tên malê.
1349. Riders and pedestrians, villagers and the merchant caravan went behind each other behind Omer Beg and Gurî they turned their direction to the village, they come home.

1350. Jin û zilam, pîrek û zarok derketin pêşîya wan bi kêf, şahî, stran û lîrelîr heya gihaştin gund.
1350. Women and males, females and children went out before them with joy, celebration, songs and trilling until they reached the village.

1351. Bû êvar, şev ket erdê, Omer Begê û şêwirdarên xwe man li odeyê û çend siwar û mêrxasên Omer Begê li hev rûniştin û ji nû ve li Gurî pirsîn.
1351. It became evening, night fell to the ground, Omer Beg and his counselors remained in the room and several riders and braves of Omer Beg sat together and anew asked Gurî.

1352. Omer Begê jê re got: Law Gurî, yabo niha tu kî yî?
1352. Omer Beg said to him: Boy Gurî, father now who are you?

1353. Û tu ji ku derê yî?
1353. And where are you from?

1354. Û tu çi kes î?
1354. And what person are you?

1355. Gurî: Wele ez Siyamend im, ez ji xelkê Silîva me.
1355. Gurî: By God I am Sîyamend, I am of the people of Silîva.

1356. Omer Begê: Ê yabo Sîyamend, te mala min xera kir anî mîratê law.
1356. Omer Beg: Eh father Sîyamend, you ruined my house brought it to desolation boy.

1357. Gurî: Çima apo, ezxulam çima?
1357. Gurî: Why uncle, I your servant why?

1358. Mi çi kirîye?
1358. What have I done?

1359. Omer Begê: Te çi kirîye?!
1359. Omer Beg: What have you done?!

1360. Malmîrato, te Ehmed Begê başbazirganê salê kuştîye, hîn tu dibê min çi kirîye.
1360. Ruined-house, you have killed Ehmed Beg the chief merchant of the year, still you say what have I done.

1361. Mane wê sibe Dewleta Osmanî fermana serê min rake û mal û milkê min gişî talan bike law.
1361. For tomorrow the Ottoman State will raise the command of my head (order my execution) and plunder all my wealth and property boy.

1362. Gurî: Metirse apo, heya ez saxim li dinyayê bila tu tirs ji te re çênebe.
1362. Gurî: Do not fear uncle, as long as I am alive in the world let no fear arise for you.

1363. Omer Begê: Law ev dewlet e, artêşa wê bêbav û bêewle ye.
1363. Omer Beg: Boy this is a state, its army is fatherless and unsecure (ruthless and untrustworthy).

1364. Gurî (Siyamend): Ez birazîyê te me, Xwedê bê erê, ez nahêlim kes bi topraxa gundê te keve, yê bê, ew sax venagere malê, ez ê te biparêzim.
1364. Gurî (Sîyamend): I am your nephew, God saying yes, I will not let anyone fall upon the soil of your village, whoever comes, he does not return home alive, I will protect you.

1365. Wê şevê rabûn ji hev belav bûn, her yek çû mala xwe, Sîyamend jî xwe li odeyê ramidand û pix kir xewê.
1365. That night they got up scattered from each other, each went to his home, Sîyamend too stretched himself out in the room and snored to sleep.

1366. Wê şevê pê de şevbihêrka gundîya li ser Gurî û talanîya wî ji kerwan û bazirgan, û kuştina Ehmed Begê, siwarê Demirqeran bû.
1366. That night onward the evening gathering of the villagers was upon Gurî and his plundering of the caravan and merchant, and the killing of Ehmed Beg, the rider of Demirqeran.

1367. Û pisnê mêranîya wî û pêlewanîya wî didan, hin dibêjin, ev çi mêrxasê zilama ye law, û hin dibêjin, ev çi pêlewan û leheng e, û hin dibêjin, ev çi hefrîte law, ji qûlê reş jî mêrtir û xurttir e; û jinên hinekan dibêjin, ku mêr ne wilo bin, ji çi re ne, ah mêrê wilo keleha vedikin û diherifînin.
1367. And they were giving praise of his manliness and his championship, some say, what brave of men is this boy, and some say, what champion and hero is this, and some say, what demon is this boy, he is more manly and stronger than the black slave too; and the wives of some say, if men are not so, what are they for, ah such men open castles and demolish them.

1368. Û bi van gotinan û pesnê Gurî bi mêranî û mêrxasî şev derbas bû.
1368. And with these words and the praise of Gurî with manliness and bravery the night passed.

1369. Sibehê gundîyê Omer Begê ji xew rabûn, hin bi kêf in û hin jî bi tirs in ji fermana dewletê.
1369. In the morning the villagers of Omer Beg woke from sleep, some are with joy and some are with fear from the command of the state.

1370. Omer Begê şand pey zanîyar û şêwirdarên xwe û ji wan re got: "Meriv ka em çi bikin ji Sîyamendî re?"
1370. Omer Beg sent after his wise men and counselors and said to them: "Men well what shall we do for Sîyamend?"

1371. Şêwirdar: Ezbenî wele kesê wek Sîyamend, weke mar e, ne cih û ne war e, û malê dinê jê re ne gerek e, û dûrî mirov û êl û eşîra xwe ketîye, tu pêdiviyên wî nîn in, hema tu ji ya min dikî (ji Omer Begê re dibêjin) tê keça xwe Elîfê lê mehir bikî, wê ji te re bibe stûn û bingehek.
1371. Counselors: Sir by God a person like Sîyamend, is like a snake, no place and no domain, and the wealth of the world is not necessary for him, and he has fallen far from his relatives and clan and tribe, he has no needs, if only you do from mine (they say to Omer Beg) you will marry your daughter Elîf to him, it will become a pillar and foundation for you.

1372. Wele tu kes nikare dest li ber hilîne, zora artêşa dewletekê dibe, a baş ew e tu nêzîkî xwe bike bi keçikê.
1372. By God no one can raise a hand before him, he defeats the army of a state, the good thing is you make him close to yourself with the girl.

1373. Omer Begê rabû şand pey Siyamend, ji xulamekî xwe re got: "Here jê re bêje bila bê odê".
1373. Omer Beg got up sent after Sîyamend, said to a servant of his: "Go say to him let him come to the room".

1374. Sîyamend hat li pêşîya Omer Begê jipîya sekinî û got: "Ha begê min, tu çi ji min divê?"
1374. Sîyamend came stood on his feet before Omer Beg and said: "Ah my beg, what do you want from me?"

1375. Omer Begê: Rûnê kurê min.
1375. Omer Beg: Sit my son.

1376. Sîyamend min û şêwirdarên xwe bi hev re biryar û peymanek daye ji bo xatirê te û vê mêranîya te.
1376. Sîyamend I and my counselors have given a decision and pact together for your sake and this manliness of yours.

1377. Sîyamend: Xêr e, Xwedê xêr bike, hema hûn çi bêjin ez qayil im.
1377. Sîyamend: It is goodness, may God make goodness, just whatever you say I am satisfied.

1378. Omer Begê: Kurê min, Siyamend law ez dixwazim keça xwe Elîfê li te mehir bikim, ka tu dibê çi?
1378. Omer Beg: My son, Sîyamend boy I want to marry my daughter Elîf to you, well what do you say?

1379. Bi dilê te ye, ne bi dilê te ye?
1379. Is it by your heart (pleasing to you), is it not by your heart?

1380. Siyamend: Min qebûl e û bi dilê min e, ma wê çima ne bi dilê min be!
1380. Sîyamend: It is accepted by me and it is by my heart, after all why will it not be by my heart!

1381. Omer Begê: De ser xêrê be law.
1381. Omer Beg: Then may it be upon goodness boy.

1382. Berê xwe da melayê xwe û jê re got: "Seyda de ka mehra wan bibire".
1382. He turned his direction to his mullah and said to him: "Master then well cut their marriage (perform their marriage)".

1383. Seyda rabû: Sîyamend law, were destê amê xwe ramîse.
1383. The master got up: Sîyamend boy, come kiss the hand of your uncle.

1384. Siyamend rabû destê apê xwe Omer Begê maç kir û li hember rûnişt, seyda destê Sîyamend û destê Omer Begê xistin hev û got: "Soz û peyman di orta her duya de", û mehra Sîyamend li Elîfê birî.
1384. Sîyamend got up kissed the hand of his uncle Omer Beg and sat opposite, the master put Sîyamend's hand and Omer Beg's hand into each other and said: "Promise and pact in the middle of both", and cut the marriage of Sîyamend to Elîf.

1385. Deng li nav gundîyan belav bû, qereçî bi lez û bez hatin, geşt û şêranîyê, û mitriba dahol û zirnên xwe saz kirin û berê xwe dan dîwana beg, û qîz û xortan govend gerandin û dîlan kirin.
1385. The voice (news) spread among the villagers, the gypsies came with haste and speed, the touring and sweets, and the musicians set up their drums and clarinets and turned their direction to the court of the beg, and girls and youths turned the govend (line dance) and danced.

1386. Gundî giş bi kêf û şahî ne, daweta Sîyamend û Elîfê ye.
1386. The villagers all are with joy and celebration, it is the wedding of Sîyamend and Elîf.

1387. Hewşa Omer Begê û gasîn û zikakên li dorê tijî ne.
1387. The courtyard of Omer Beg and the plazas and alleys around are full.

1388. Jin, bî, zarok, pîr û kal hemû ji xwe re li dîlanê dinerin.
1388. Women, widows, children, old women and old men all watch the dance for themselves.

1389. Govend gerîyaye ji sibê heya êvarî kesekî betal nekirîye.
1389. The govend has turned from morning until evening no one has quit.

1390. Piza bûkê çer jê kirin û nan çêkirin.
1390. They slaughtered the bride's sheep and made bread.

1391. Zilam û xorta xwarin, qîz û bûkê gund çûn Elîfê girê dan û cilê bûkanîyê lê kirin, xemilandin bi dest û nigê hinekirî, çavên reş û belek bi kilê sibhanî kil kirin, tu li bejn û bala Elîfê dinerî weke perîyek ji perîyên bihuştê ye: Bejna zirav, dêmê gulî, çavên kilkirî, zilf û biskê badayî û hinekirî, dest û rûyê gewr û boz, lêvên sorî şekirî.
1391. The males and youths ate, the girls and brides of the village went tied Elîf and put the bridal clothes on her, adorned her with hennaed hands and feet, blackened the black and spotted (beautiful) eyes with divine kohl, you look at the figure and stature of Elîf she is like a fairy from the fairies of paradise: Slender figure, rosy countenance, blackened eyes, twisted and hennaed locks and braids, fair and white hands and face, red sugary lips.

1392. Hema tu dibê qey Xwedê ji dilê xwe re neqişandîye û nazik û bedew kirîye, hema yek dibê ya Rebî ez ji xwe re têr lê binerim.
1392. Just you say as if God has embroidered her for his own heart and made her delicate and beautiful, just one says o Lord let me look at her to satisfaction for myself.

1393. Carîya û dêya Elîfê odeyak ji bûk û zavê re raxistine û bi merş û beran xemilandine, bi doşek û balîfan, bi nazbalîf û palgehan dagirtine.
1393. The maid and mother of Elîf have laid out a room for the bride and groom and adorned it with rugs and carpets, filled it with mattresses and pillows, with delicate pillows and cushions.

1394. Piştî şeva reş ket erdê, dîlan û gund ferikî, her yek çû mala xwe, xorta bi destê zavê (Siyamend) girtin û birin odeya wî bi henek û laqirdî.
1394. After the black night fell to the ground, the dance and village tired (finished), each went to his home, the youths took the groom (Sîyamend) by the hand and took him to his room with jokes and banter.

1395. Ew xistin hundir û vegerîyan.
1395. They put him inside and returned.

1396. Siyamend jî derbas bû, li ser textê xwe rûnişt û balîf û nazbalîf dan ber kêleka xwe û wilo ma li hêvîya Elîfê.
1396. Sîyamend too passed in, sat on his bed and put the pillows and delicate pillows before his side and remained so waiting for Elîf.

1397. Keçika jî Elîfê xemilandine, kiras û xeftanê tenik bi ser binkiras û hevalkirasê hevirmêşî de lê kirine.
1397. The girls too have adorned Elîf, have put the thin shirt and caftan over the silk under-shirt and slip on her.

1398. Eba neqişandî bi zirikê zîv û zêr lê kirin, kum û serdor û pêşanîk li serî kirin û perdak tenik bi ser çavan dakirin, û şimka req eqanî xistin nigê kilîbozê hinekirî û bi çepk û stran û lîrelîr bi sema û çopî qîzik li dora bûkê dizîvirin û bi destê wê girtin.
1398. They put the embroidered cloak with thread of silver and gold on her, put the cap and headband and frontlet on her head and brought down a thin veil over the eyes, and put the clattering shoes on the white-ankled hennaed feet and with clapping and songs and trilling with sema and line-dance the young girls turn around the bride and took her by the hand.

1399. Ew ji malbavê derxistin; bi kêf û şahî, dîlok û sirêlî Elîfê bi nazikî dimeşînin heya xistin odeya zavê (odeya nûşkê).
1399. They took her out from the father's house; with joy and celebration, wedding songs and trills they walk Elîf with delicacy until they put her into the groom's room (the nuptial room).

1400. Elîfê derbas bû hundir û keçik û govend ji du vegerîyan û derî lê girtin.
1400. Elîf passed inside and the girls and govend returned from behind and closed the door on her.

1401. Elîfê tev li xeml û xêza xwe, xuşîn û gunîn jê tê bi şingsinga xirxala û çingeçinga bazin û bazbenda; xusîn û nalîn jê tê wek xumxuma başbazirganê salê û xuşxuşa kimber û qolana zîvî û gerdenîya zêr li ser sîngê derbasî odeyê bû, li hember Sîyamend jipîya bi şerm û fehêt di cihê xwe de rawestîya.
1401. Elîf together with her adornment and drawing (makeup), rustling and swishing comes from her with the jingling of anklets and clinking of bracelets and armbands; rustling and moaning comes from her like the hubbub of the chief merchant of the year and the swishing of the silver belt and girth and golden necklace on the chest she passed into the room, she stood on her feet with shame and bashfulness in her place opposite Sîyamend.

1402. Sîyamend xwe tev jî nexurciland, li ser doşeka ser text rûniştî ye pala xwe daye balîf û nazbalîfan hayê wî ji bayê felekê tune ye; xwe pê nehisand ku Elîfê derbas bûye û li hember wî sekinîye.
1402. Sîyamend did not move himself at all, he is seated on the mattress on the bed he has leaned back on the pillows and delicate pillows he has no awareness of the wind of fate; he did not make himself feel (notice) that Elîf has passed in and stood opposite him.

1403. Seatek dido, sisê derbas bûn mêrik nelebitî û jinik ser darê lingan qerimî.
1403. One hour two, three passed the man did not stir and the woman cramped up on the wood of her legs (standing).

1404. Şev li wan zîz bû, kes şîyar nema ji gundê Omer Begê, kes bi kesî re napeyive û dengê xwe nadê.
1404. The night became silent upon them, no one remained awake from Omer Beg's village, no one speaks with anyone and does not give their voice.

1405. Dem derbas dibe, ket piştî nîvê şevê.
1405. Time passes, it fell after midnight.

1406. Elîfê nema xwe girt û di dilê xwe de got: "Av bi çogên min ve hatin bavo, wele vîna ez ji dêla xwînîya ve nanîme, ez nema xwe li ser lingên xwe digirim, ez ê du gotinan jê re bêjim, ka bê ew çi dibêje".
1406. Elîf no longer held herself and said in her heart: "Water has come attached to my knees (my knees are swelling) father, by God I have not brought this from the substitute of blood-money (I am not a slave), I no longer hold myself on my legs, I will say two words to him, well let's see what he says".

1407. Elîfê berê xwe dayê û got: "Lo lo, lo lo Sîyamendo, ax lo lo Sîyamendo dilê min dibê ox,
1407. Elîf turned her direction to him and said: "Lo lo, lo lo Sîyamendo, ah lo lo Sîyamendo my heart says oh,

1408. şev e li min û te hatîye nîvê şevê, û tu nabêje tu pirsê tu galegalê.
1408. it is night upon me and you it has come to midnight, and you do not say any question any chatter.

1409. Lo lo, ox lo lo Siyamendo,
1409. Lo lo, oh lo lo Sîyamendo,

1410. ez Elîfê me qîza Omer Begê, xwedîyê sî û sê gundê qontara çîyê,
1410. I am Elîf the daughter of Omer Beg, owner of thirty-three villages of the foothills of the mountain,

1411. û tu li min hove nade, tu ji min nake tu gotin û tu pirs. De lo lo Siyamendo, tu bala xwe bide bejna min ya bilind û zirav weke dara hewrê,
1411. and you do not give a wild glance at me, you do not make any word and any question from me. Then lo lo Sîyamendo, you give your attention to my high and slender figure like the poplar tree,

1412. û tu li zend û bendê min ên kil û boz binêre mîna xîyrê hewagê Edenê,
1412. and you look at my white and fair forearms and wrists like the cucumber of the climate of Eden,

1413. û tu li sînga min binêr mîna perçê berf û qeşê ox ox. Û tu li diranê min dinêre spî ye nola birinca Qerejdaxê ku mirov bîst û çar dem xuleka bavêje ber mîrata dengê ox ox.
1413. and you look at my chest like a piece of snow and ice oh oh. And you look at my teeth it is white like the rice of Karacadağ that a person throws twenty-four time-minutes before the legacy of the voice oh oh.

1414. Û şevê reş dirêj in li min û te bûye nîvê şevê ox, û tu ji min nake çi pirsê û çi gotinê, ox ox li min ê lo lo lo Sîyamendo".
1414. And the black nights are long upon me and you it has become midnight oh, and you do not make any question and any word from me, oh oh upon me lo lo lo Sîyamendo".

1415. Siyamend da ber û got,
1415. Sîyamend replied and said,

1416. "lê lê lê Elîfê, ez ne Sîyamend im, ez Gurî me, Gurîyê wê dema hanê,
1416. "le le le Elîf, I am not Sîyamend, I am Gurî, Gurî of that time back then,

1417. û tê bîra te, gava te digo, gurîo, çepelo, mirdalo, heramo ku tu vexwe ji vê satilê, tê biherimîne ava satilê.
1417. and does it come to your mind, when you said, scabby one, filthy one, carrion, forbidden one if you drink from this bucket, you will defile the water of the bucket.

1418. De lê lê Elîfê, min ji te re digot, bejna min zirav e tak rîhana li takî, û şîn dibe li hawakî,
1418. Then le le Elîf, I was saying to you, my figure is slender a sprig of basil on a sprig, and it grows green in an environment,

1419. mane min ji te re gotibû, soz û biryarê Xwedê li can û cesedê min ketibe, ji niha û ne dereng wê ramîsanê te li cem min bin, ne bi perakî.
1419. for I had said to you, let the promise and decision of God have fallen upon my soul and body, from now and not late those kisses of yours will be by me, not with a single penny.

1420. Lê lê Elîfê, de here tu dê û xwişka min be, min tu navê, li min li min hoy".
1420. Le le Elîf, then go you be my mother and sister, I do not want you, woe is me woe is me hoy".

1421. Elîfê polîpoşman vegerîya malê, kete nav cîyê xwe li holîya xwe.
1421. Elîf full of regret returned to the house, fell into her bed in her hall.

1422. Serê sibê dêya Elîfê ji xew rabû nerî ku Elîfê li holîyê ye, jê pirsî, "law keça min Elîfê, çi bela te ye, çima tu li holîya xwe ye law?"
1422. Early in the morning Elîf's mother woke from sleep looked that Elîf is in the hall, asked her, "boy my daughter Elîf, what is your calamity, why are you in your hall boy?"

1423. Elîfê: Hûû...dayê, ji xwe mêrik li mijî nenerî, û li min hove neda û talîya matalî ji min re got, here mala bavê xwe, min tu navê.
1423. Elîf: Huu...mother, from himself the man did not even look at me, and did not give a wild glance at me and lastly completely said to me, go to your father's house, I do not want you.

1424. Dêya Elîfê: Wele law, qirdê bavê te ye, gurîkî bêtore ye, Xwedê belak ji me re şandîye, gundî û malî pê bizanin ku Sîyamend bi Elîfê qayil nebûye.
1424. Elîf's mother: By God boy, he is the clown of your father, he is a mannerless scabby one, God has sent a calamity for us, the villagers and the household will know of it that Sîyamend was not satisfied with Elîf.

1425. Xelkê bihîst.
1425. The people heard.

1426. Qîz û xort man matmayî, çawa keçeke wek Elîfê bejna zirav û dirêj, rû û dêmê gewr, şox û şeng e û Gurî pê qayil nebû, Gurî loo, tu li Gurî loo!
1426. Girls and youths remained astonished, how a girl like Elîf slender and tall figure, fair face and countenance, she is coquettish and lively and Gurî was not satisfied with her, Gurî loo, you look at Gurî loo!

1427. Çend rojan gundî bi vê çîrokê jî daketin û şevbihêrkên xwe pê derbas kirin.
1427. For a few days the villagers too came down with (discussed) this story and passed their evening gatherings with it.

1428. Demeke ne dirêj derbas bû, Gurî xewnek dît ku nanê wî li vir nema ye û divê ji vir here, birakî wek wî ye Sêwî bê dê û bav e, bi navê Qeregêtran.
1428. A not long time passed, Gurî saw a dream that his bread has not remained here and he must go from here, a brother is like him an Orphan without mother and father, by the name of Qeregêtran.

1429. Serê sibê Gurî hat odeyê silav kir û li pêşîya Omer Begê rawestîya.
1429. Early in the morning Gurî came to the room greeted and stood before Omer Beg.

1430. Omer Begê: Te xêr e law Sîyamend, tu çi ji min dixwazî?"
1430. Omer Beg: What is your goodness (what is the matter) boy Sîyamend, what do you want from me?"

1431. Sîyamend: Ezbenî wele tu apê min î, û li şûna bavê min î, ez ji te dixwazim nan û ava xwe tê li min helal bike, nesîbê min ji cem te hilat, ez ê ji vir herim.
1431. Sîyamend: Sir by God you are my uncle, and you are in place of my father, I want from you that you will make your bread and water lawful for me, my portion rose (finished) from by you, I will go from here.

1432. Omer Begê: Law Sîyamend, ma kes dev ji mala xwe û dê û bavê xwe berdide?
1432. Omer Beg: Boy Sîyamend, after all does anyone release their mouth from (abandon) their house and their mother and father?

1433. Sîyamend: Apo gotina min yeke, min got: Na na ye, hew nesîbê min ji vir hilatîye.
1433. Sîyamend: Uncle my word is one, I said: No is no, enough my portion has risen from here.

1434. Omer Begê bi dev dibêje law mere û di dilê xwe de dibêje wey tu here û venegere.
1434. Omer Beg says with the mouth boy do not go and in his heart says woe you go and do not return.

1435. Rabûn karê Sîyamend kirin, cil û bergên wî danê û xurcezîna demirqerên lê kir û hespekî din jî destkêşî xwe kir û av û xwarina xwe dagirt û xatir xwest.
1435. They got up did Sîyamend's preparation, gave him his clothes and garments and put the saddlebags of Demirqeran on him and made another horse hand-led for himself and filled his water and food and asked for leave (said goodbye).

1436. Berê xwe da Sîpanê Xelatê û kudand, qûnaxek dido hilanîn û danîn.
1436. He turned his direction to Sîpan of Xelat and spurred on, lifted and put down one two stages.

1437. Nêzîkayî li gundekî kir, dinya çile ye sar û serme ye, Sîpan ji berfê xemilî ye, spî ye wek hêkê.
1437. He approached a village, the world is midwinter it is cold and chill, Sîpan is adorned from snow, it is white like an egg.

1438. Sîyamend siwar e li hespê û dikudîne, bala xwe dayê ku reşkek ji dûr ve xuya dike û relekî weke qûçekê dûrî reşayê rûniştîye.
1438. Sîyamend is mounted on the horse and spurs on, gave his attention to it that a black speck appears from afar and a track like a cone has sat far from the blackness.

1439. Di dilê xwe de got: Bi navê Xwedê, ev jî sewterêkî wek min e, mi jî berê wilo dikir, davik û xefk li ber çûkan vedidan.
1439. In his heart he said: By the name of God, this too is a vagabond like me, I too was doing so previously, they were setting snares and traps before the birds.

1440. Nêzîkayî lê kir, ewê wek qûçekê Qeregêtrane rabû ser xwe û dengê xwe hilda, kuro siwaro wirde, çûk hatî ye
1440. He approached him, that one like a cone is Qeregêtran got up on himself and raised his voice, boy rider keep away, the bird has come

1441. ser xefkê, hindik maye ku bi teqîne û têkeve xefkê, Sîyamend nedaye û têbi alîyê davkade, Qeregêtran bang lê kir: Law fire her min qi hê min çûka xwe ji topraxa heft gunda anîye ser xefkê dûr kev law dûr her, bi navê Xwedê ku çûkê min bifire û here Yemenê, têherê bînî ji Yemenê, law siwaro dûr kev qey xwînate ketîye çavên te?
1441. upon the trap, little remains that he will trigger it and fall into the trap, Sîyamend did not give (heed) and comes to the side of the snare, Qeregêtran called out to him: Boy go away I... I have brought my bird from the soil of seven villages upon the trap fall far boy go far, by the name of God if my bird flies and goes to Yemen, you will go bring it from Yemen, boy rider fall far has your blood fallen into your eyes?

1442. law ev çi bela te ye?
1442. boy what calamity of yours is this?

1443. Siyamend ji qazîve ajot ser xefka, çûk firîya, Qeregêtran çiplaq ji ber xwe kişand û êrîş kir Sîyamend, çîplaqek daweşandê, Sîyamend xwe ji ber da alîkî, nehişt lê keve, rape rikîn hev bi gotinan bi destan.
1443. Sîyamend on purpose drove upon the trap, the bird flew, Qeregêtran pulled the sharp dagger from his side and attacked Sîyamend, brought down a sharp dagger on him, Sîyamend put himself aside from before it, did not let it strike him, they clashed with each other with words with hands.

1444. Siyamend: Law kuro, gotinên zêde ji kêm aqilîne, em ê rahjin hev binavê, kê kî avêt erdê bila wî bikuje û hew, de wer bê Xwedê dide ca kê ji me?
1444. Sîyamend: Boy boy, excess words are from lack of reason, we will pick each other up by the waist, whoever threw whom to the ground let him kill him and that is all, then come let us see God gives the place to whom of us?

1445. Bi newqa hevûdu girtin li ser wê berfê, û hevûdu birin û anîn, kesî tu çiq di kesî nekir, Sîyamend got: Ya Xwedanê şev û roj,ê û xewna nîvê şevê, û ji kes û bi hiner ew zîzikand û xiste erdê, lahorê xwe ji ber xwe kişand, ku bide hustêwî ser jêke, Qeregêtran di bin de got: Bira tu ne Sîyamend î?
1445. They grabbed by the waist of each other on that snow, and took and brought each other (wrestled), no one made any crack in anyone, Sîyamend said: O Master of night and day, and the dream of midnight, and from anger and with skill he dropped him whizzing and put him to the ground, pulled his scimitar from his side, to put it to his neck to cut his head off, Qeregêtran underneath said: Brother are you not Sîyamend?

1446. Siyamend: Belê wele, te ji ku zanîbû?
1446. Sîyamend: Yes by God, from where did you know?

1447. kuro ma tu jî ne Qeregêtran î?
1447. boy after all are you too not Qeregêtran?

1448. birayê min î?
1448. are you my brother?

1449. Qeregêtran: Belê wele ez im, min tu ji teqla te nas kir.
1449. Qeregêtran: Yes by God it is me, I recognized you from your form.

1450. Sîyamend: Erê wele, min ji teql û hunera te tu nas kir.
1450. Sîyamend: Yes by God, I recognized you from your form and skill.

1451. Herduyan li tenîş hev rûniştin, û gilî û gazinê xwe bi hev kirin.
1451. Both sat beside each other, and made their complaints and grievances with each other.

1452. Sîyamend: Birê min Qeregêtran: Ev çi kare, ev çi rebenîye, li ber vê sermê, qer û qeşayê?
1452. Sîyamend: My brother Qeregêtran: What work is this, what wretchedness is this, before this cold, frost and ice?

1453. Qeregêtran: Çend zarokên jinapa min hene, biçûk in Xwedê wan nehêle, bi şev û bi roj bi dû min de ne, ji bo ez ji wan re çûkan bigirim, ku ez çûkan didim dest wan, ew jî her yek ji wan parîk nên didin min, ez diavêjim zelûma xwe.
1453. Qeregêtran: My aunt has a few children, they are small may God not leave them (may they perish), by night and by day they are behind me, so that I catch birds for them, when I give birds to their hand, they too each of them give a piece of bread to me, I throw it into my gullet.

1454. Hema ew e ez pê qût dibim, ez namirim.
1454. Just that is what I am sustained by, I do not die.

1455. 2. Zelûm: Bi erebî ye. Kurdîya wê: Qirik.
1455. 2. Zelûm: It is in Arabic. Its Kurdish: Throat.

1456. Sîyamend rabû xurcika xwe vala kir ber xwe û her duyan bi hev re nanê xwe xwarin, jê re got, "rab em ê herin, va min mihîna te anîye, û ez ê cil û çeka ji te re bikirim, û dev ji jinapa xwe û zarokên wê berde, ev cih nema ji te re dibe".
1456. Sîyamend got up emptied his saddlebag before himself and both together ate their bread, he said to him, "get up we will go, here I have brought your mare, and I will buy clothes and weapons for you, and release your mouth from (abandon) your aunt and her children, this place no longer becomes (is suitable) for you".

1457. Û jê pirsî, "ka bajarê we li ku derê ye?"
1457. And asked him, "well where is your city?"

1458. Qeregêtran: Navê bajarê me Elcewazê ye, hema tu vî qelaçî bi qulpîne têbigihê bajêr, her du siwar bûn û dan kêleka hev û çûn bajêr, bi rê de nêzîkî qeleç.
1458. Qeregêtran: The name of our city is Elcewaz, just you turn this hill you will reach the city, both mounted and put to each other's side (rode side by side) and went to the city, on the road near the hill.

1459. Qeregêtran bang Sîyamend kir û got,
1459. Qeregêtran called out to Sîyamend and said,

1460. Qeregêtran: Sîyamend birayê min, ha tu wê şeqala reş ya dirêj dibînî, ji vî serî heya wî serî giş cihê xefk û davên min in, ku ez ne li mal bim jî kesek ji zarokan newêre nêzîkî wan bibe, birayê min û heft kundirê min yên kaba jî hene û heft deq di nav de ne, sibê ez û tu em ê têkevin nav lîskê de, em kabekî bi wan re nahêlin.
1460. Qeregêtran: Sîyamend my brother, ah you see that black long ravine, from this end to that end all are the place of my traps and snares, if I am not at home too no one from the children dares to approach them, my brother and I have seven gourds of knuckle-bones too and seven spots are inside, tomorrow I and you we will enter into the game, we do not leave one knuckle-bone with them.

1461. Sîyamend: Bi Xwedê hîn birayê min sewterîyê nav zaroka.
1461. Sîyamend: By God still my brother is a vagabond among children.

1462. Birayê min ev cih nema ji me re dibe, û ev kar û îş jê biqer, niha em ê herin Elcewazê ez ê cila û çeka ji te re bikirim, û divê em ji xwe re karekî, îşekî bikin, bese em mezin bûne, mal ji me re divê, jin ji me re divin, bese ev rezîltî.
1462. My brother this place no longer is suitable for us, and this work and business turn away from it, now we will go to Elcewaz I will buy clothes and weapons for you, and we must do a work, a business for ourselves, enough we have grown big, wealth is necessary for us, wives are necessary for us, enough this wretchedness.

1463. Gihan bajarê Elcewazê, birayê xwe nih kirîye cil û çek û şûr û mertal û rim û xwarin û ava xwe dagirtin, xistin xurcikê zînê ser pişta hespa û ji bajêr derketin.
1463. They reached the city of Elcewaz, he made his brother new clothes and weapons and sword and shield and spear and filled their food and water, put them in the saddlebag of the saddle on the back of the horses and went out of the city.

1464. Tibabekî çûn bi dûr ketin, li bin sîya derekê rûniştin, hespên xwe ji cihoka kanîyê avdan û di nav çîmen û gîyê de girê dan ji bo biçêrin.
1464. They went a while fell far, sat under the shade of a tree, watered their horses from the stream of the spring and tied them among the meadow and grass so they would graze.

1465. Ew jî rûniştin bo firavînê bixwin, xwarin, vexwarin, xwe rihet kirin.
1465. They too sat down to eat lunch, ate, drank, rested themselves.

1466. Sîyamend axivî,
1466. Sîyamend spoke,

1467. Siyamend: Birayê min, bi salê Xwedê ez ji te mezintir im, ez ji te re bê çi tu ji gotina min dernakeve.
1467. Sîyamend: My brother, by the years of God I am older than you, whatever I say to you you do not go out from my word.

1468. Qeregêtran: Ez tu car ji gotina te dernakevim, û tê jî biryarê bide, tu ti carî lahor li min nakişîne.
1468. Qeregêtran: I never go out from your word, and you too give a decision, you never draw the scimitar on me.

1469. Siyamend: Na na ez ti carî lahor li te nakişînim birayê min, de rabe em ê ji xwe re bigerin, li nav êl û eşîra belkî ji karekî, ji aborekî em ji xwe re bibînin, em xwe pê xwedî bikin.
1469. Sîyamend: No no I never draw the scimitar on you my brother, then get up we will wander for ourselves, among the clans and tribes perhaps we see a work, a livelihood for ourselves, we sustain ourselves by it.

1470. Rabûn her du siwar bûn û li çol û pola digerin.
1470. They got up both mounted and wander in the wilderness and plains.

1471. Nêçîrek girtin wê bixwin û negirtin wê berê xwe bidin kunekî, gundekî, şivanekî, bo parîk nan bixwin.
1471. They catch a prey they will eat it and they do not catch they will turn their direction to a tent, a village, a shepherd, to eat a piece of bread.

1472. Sibehekê ji xew rabûn,
1472. One morning they woke from sleep,

1473. Siyamend got: Wa Qeregêtran!
1473. Sîyamend said: Wa Qeregêtran!

1474. Qeregêtran: Belê ezbenî.
1474. Qeregêtran: Yes sir.

1475. Siyamend: Şevê çûnî min xewnek dît.
1475. Sîyamend: The night of going (last night) I saw a dream.

1476. Qeregêtran: Xewna te xêr be birayê min, îşeleh xewneke baş e?
1476. Qeregêtran: May your dream be goodness my brother, God willing it is a good dream?

1477. Siyamend: Min keçikek di xew de dîtîye, heger li ku be û heya çend salê dibe ez ê wê bibînim, ez ê wê nas bikim û navê wê Xecê ye.
1477. Sîyamend: I have seen a girl in sleep, if wherever she is and up to how many years it becomes I will see her, I will recognize her and her name is Xecê.

1478. Qeregêtran: Çilo te dît?
1478. Qeregêtran: How did you see?

1479. Li ku derê bû?
1479. Where was she?

1480. Te çilo navê wê nas kir?
1480. How did you recognize her name?

1481. Siyamend: Min dît li bin kunekî bû, bi navê Xecê bang kirinê.
1481. Sîyamend: I saw she was under a tent, they called her by the name of Xecê.

1482. De rabe xwe girê de, em ê lê bigerin û heya rok ji temenê min hebe, ez ê lê bigerim.
1482. Then get up tie yourself (prepare yourself), we will search for her and as long as a day from my life exists, I will search for her.

1483. Qeregêtran: Kuro!
1483. Qeregêtran: Boy!

1484. Qey tu dîn bûye?
1484. After all have you become crazy?

1485. em ê çilo wê bibînin, em ne wê û malbata wê nas dikin, û ne êl û eşîra wê, û ne cih û warê wê.
1485. how will we find her, we do not recognize her and her family, and not her clan and tribe, and not her place and domain.

1486. Sîyamend: Ma min negot, tu tu carî ji gotina min dernakevî.
1486. Sîyamend: After all did I not say, you never go out from my word.

1487. Qeregêtran: Belê, min birîyar daye, rabe ez bi te re heya talîya dinya yê.
1487. Qeregêtran: Yes, I have given a decision, get up I am with you until the end of the world.

1488. Siyamend: Em ê bigerin, êl û eşîrin: Hesenane, Heyderane, Şikaka û Reş Kutane, Cibirane û Gêsane, û Zozane li ku derê be, em ê gepek nanê xwe bixwin, bi xweşî bû bû, bi xweşî nebû em ê bi zorê nanê xwe bistînin, û siwar bûn û dan ser oxirê.
1488. Sîyamend: We will wander, they are clans and tribes: Hesenans, Heyderans, Şikaks and Reş Kutans, Cibirans and Gêsans, and wherever the Highlands are, we will eat our bite of bread, if it was with pleasantness it was, if it was not with pleasantness we will take our bread by force, and they mounted and set upon the journey.

1489. Dinya bihar e gul û gîya ye, xweş û hênik e, kuçir û xwedî pez li berîyê belav bûne, her du siwar in dilê wan ku bixwaze berê xwe didin wir, berî fireye zozan û gelî û newal in, weke cîhangera, seyranvana, weke nêçîrvana ji xwe re digerin.
1489. The world is spring it is flowers and grass, it is pleasant and cool, nomads and sheep owners have scattered on the plain, both are mounted if their heart wants they turn their direction there, the plain is wide they are highlands and valleys and ravines, like globe-trotters, sightseers, like hunters they wander for themselves.

1490. Gihan nav êl û eşîrê Şikaka, ji zozên heya destê konê wan bela welan e, rojekê bi esrê ve rastî kunekî hatin, ne serî xuya ye ne binî, ji hev re gotin: Xwedê bê erê îşev em ê bibin mêvanê vî kunî, û bi ber kun de dirin hêdî hêdî nêzîkayî li kun kirin, nerîn zerîyek ji bin kun ve derket bejin zirav û bilind, dêmê gul şox û şeng e, bi nazikî diçe û tê, cilê tenik neqişandî li ber sira bayê hênik dipirpire.
1490. They reached among the clan and tribe of Şikak, from the highlands up to the handle of their tents it is spread out wide, one day towards afternoon they came across a tent, neither the top is visible nor the bottom, they said to each other: God saying yes tonight we will be the guests of this tent, and they go towards the tent slowly they approached the tent, they looked a fair one came out from under the tent slender and tall figure, rosy countenance she is coquettish and lively, with delicacy she goes and comes, the thin embroidered clothes flutter before the breeze of the cool wind.

1491. Sîyamend serê xwe rakir û lê temeşe kir, bi nêrîneke tûj û dijwar û got: ah birayê min, nêçîra ez lê digerîyam va ye, ha ev kehra xezala ku ez lê digerim (Xeca min).
1491. Sîyamend raised his head and watched her, with a sharp and fierce look and said: ah my brother, the prey I was searching for is this, ah this fawn of the gazelle that I search for (my Xecê).

1492. Qeregêtran: Xezala çi kuro?
1492. Qeregêtran: What gazelle boy?

1493. û Xeca çi law?
1493. and what Xecê boy?

1494. qey tu dîn bûye Sîyamend?
1494. after all have you become crazy Sîyamend?

1495. Sîyamend: Ez ne gêj im û ez ne dîn im, ha ev e ya min di xewna xwe de dîtibû, navê wê Xecê ye, de bajo bin kun, aniha têbi çavên xwe bibînî.
1495. Sîyamend: I am not dizzy and I am not crazy, ah this is the one I had seen in my dream, her name is Xecê, then drive under the tent, right now you will see with your eyes.

1496. li pêşîya kun peya bûn, hespên xwe bi şirîtê ve girê dan, keçik alîyê odeyê şanî wan da, bi rûniştin dan, xwarin û vexwarin ji wan re anî, danî ber wan û derket, berî ro here ava nerîn, şeş heft siwar li pey hev hatin bin kun xwişka wan çû pêşîya wan, û ji wa re got: Du siwar li odeyê rûniştîne, ne wek insana ne.
1496. They dismounted before the tent, tied their horses with the rope, the girl showed the side of the room to them, seated them, brought food and drink for them, put it before them and went out, before the sun went down they looked, six seven riders came behind each other under the tent their sister went before them, and said to them: Two riders are sitting in the room, they are not like humans.

1497. Siwar bi hev re peya bûn û cil û bergê xwe danîn, xwe şûştin, û hatin alîyê odeyê xêrhatin di mêvanê xwe dan, û rûniştin, û ketin şitexalîyê de û ser nêçîrê ji xwe re gengeşî kirin, Xecê jî karê şîva wan dike.
1497. The riders together dismounted and put down their clothes and garments, washed themselves, and came to the side of the room gave welcome to their guests, and sat, and fell into conversation and discussed about the hunt for themselves, Xecê too does the work of their dinner.

1498. Şîv ji wan re hat, bi hev re şîva xwe xwarin, şevbihêrka xwe derbas kirin bi hev re razan, serê sibê taştîya xwe xwarin, çar pênc heb ji wan siwar bûn çûn û du zilam li ber malê hiştin ji bo pêşwazîya mêvanan.
1498. Dinner came for them, together they ate their dinner, passed their evening gathering together they slept, early in the morning they ate their breakfast, four five of them mounted went and they left two men before the house for the receiving of the guests.

1499. Şevek, dido, sisê derbas bûn, karê wan ev e, wê ji nêçîrê bên û şîva xwe bixwin, û şevbihêrka xwe bikin, û tu pirsê ji mêvanan nakin, her yek karê xwe dike, ji nêçîrê, serdanan, kerîyê pez û mîyan, şivana.
1499. One night, two, three passed, their work is this, they will come from the hunt and eat their dinner, and do their evening gathering, and they make no question from the guests, each does his work, of the hunt, visits, flock of sheep and ewes, shepherds.

1500. Çend roj qedîyan, Siyamend ji Qeregêtran re got: Birayê min wilo nabe, heger mêvantî be bese, ne zikê me diçire, û ne nanê wan xelas dibe, divê em ji xwe re çarakê bikin, em li vir genî bûn, bese.
1500. A few days finished, Sîyamend said to Qeregêtran: My brother it does not become so, if it is guestship enough, neither our stomach tears, nor their bread finishes, we must do a remedy for ourselves, we became rotten here, enough.

1501. Qeregêtran: Ka em çi bikin?
1501. Qeregêtran: Well what shall we do?

1502. çi çare heye?
1502. what remedy is there?

1503. ka bibêje?
1503. well say?

1504. Siyamend: Çare çare îşev têbibîne, ez birayê te me, ez dizanim.
1504. Sîyamend: Remedy remedy tonight you will see, I am your brother, I know.

1505. Bû êvar, siwarê malê hatin wek her roj xwe şûştin, şîva xwe xwarin, şevbihêrka xwe kirin û ketin nav peyv û gotin û gengeşeyê de.
1505. It became evening, the riders of the house came like every day washed themselves, ate their dinner, did their evening gathering and fell into words and talk and discussion.

1506. Siyamend dengê xwe hilda û got: Gelî birano, ev neh, deh şevên me li vir qedîyan, ne nanê we xelas dibe, û ne zikê me têrdibe, ma hûn ji me nakin tu pirse, tu gotine.
1506. Sîyamend raised his voice and said: O brothers, these nine, ten nights of ours finished here, neither your bread finishes, nor our stomach becomes full, after all do you not make any question, any word from us.

1507. Yekî ji biraya lê vegerand û got: Gelî bira, hûn mêvanin, mêvan mêvanê Xwedê ne, bixwin û vexwin ser sera û ser çavan, heger pêdiviyek we hebe, hûn ê bibêjin?
1507. One from the brothers returned (replied) to him and said: O brother, you are guests, guests are the guests of God, eat and drink upon the heads and upon the eyes, if you have a need, will you say?

1508. Siyamend: Gelî bira, Xwedê mezin e, kî ji we mezinê birayan e?
1508. Sîyamend: O brothers, God is great, who from you is the eldest of the brothers?

1509. Xorşîd (birayê mezin e): Ez im yê mezin mêvanê delal çi pêdiviya te heye?
1509. Xorşîd (is the eldest brother): I am the eldest dear guest what need do you have?

1510. Siyamend: Pismam pirsa bê şerm û fedî, wele em hatine mirovîya we dixwazin, bi helalîya Xwedê, em hatine Xecê ji min re, ez Sîyamend im û ev jî birayê min Qeregêtran e bixwazin.
1510. Sîyamend: Cousin question without shame and bashfulness, by God we have come we want your kinship, with the lawfulness of God, we have come to want Xecê for me, I am Sîyamend and this too is my brother Qeregêtran.

1511. Xorşîd: Pismam tu dibînî bi çavê xwe, em heft biran e û xwişka me Xecê yeka tenê ye, heft pismamên me hene Xecê dixwazin û di devê rê de ne, em ji wan re dibêjin, heft jina berdêlî ji me re bînin, em ê Xecê bidin yekî ji we.
1511. Xorşîd: Cousin you see with your eye, we are seven brothers and our sister Xecê is an only one, we have seven cousins they want Xecê and they are in the mouth of the road (waiting), we say to them, bring seven substitute wives for us, we will give Xecê to one of you.

1512. Ezbenî wele qelenê Xecê giran e, bi heft jina ye.
1512. Sir by God the bride-price of Xecê is heavy, it is with seven wives.

1513. Sîyamend ji birayê xwe Qeregêtran re got: Rabe her destên pismamê xwe, min qebûl kir, ez ê heft jina ji wan re bînim.
1513. Sîyamend said to his brother Qeregêtran: Get up go (kiss) the hands of your cousin, I accepted, I will bring seven wives for them.

1514. Pepûkê Qeregêtran newêre ji ya wî derkeve û tiştekî bibêje, ji neçarî hema rabû û çû destên Xorşîdî birayê Xecê yê mezin maç kir û soz û birîyar dan hev û pêşgotina xwe xwendin bi kêf û şahî.
1514. Wretched Qeregêtran does not dare to go out from his (word) and say a thing, from necessity just got up and went kissed the hands of Xorşîd the eldest brother of Xecê and they gave promise and decision to each other and read their preamble (Fatiha) with joy and celebration.

1515. Piştî şevbihêrka xwe kirin bi mervantî, birayên Xecê çûn ser cihên xwe razan û Sîyamend û Qeregêtran man bi tenê li alîyê odeyê.
1515. After they did their evening gathering with kinship, the brothers of Xecê went onto their places slept and Sîyamend and Qeregêtran remained alone at the side of the room.

1516. Qeregêtran: Malmîrato!
1516. Qeregêtran: Ruined-house!

1517. Tu dibînî metelîk jî bi me re tune ye, em ê heft jina ji van camêra re ji ku derê bînin, qey te hişê xwe xwarîyî?
1517. You see a coin too is not with us, from where will we bring seven wives for these gentlemen, after all have you eaten your mind (lost your mind)?

1518. Sîyamend: Êh, bê çi ehmeq e, kuro sibê zû em ê rabin û dûr herin ji arvanî, karvanî, qirşvanî, em ê heft qîza ji wan re bînin, bidin wan û em ê ya xwe siwar kin û bibin; ku me ya xwe berdestî xwe kir û em çûn, me çi ji wan e?
1518. Sîyamend: Eh, what a fool he is, boy tomorrow early we will get up and go far from flour-millers, caravaneers, brushwood-gatherers, we will bring seven girls for them, give them and we will mount ours and take her; when we have made ours available to ourselves and we went, what is it of us from them (what do we care about them)?

1519. Serê sibê zû rabûn û dûr çûn ji bo zû bi zû pirsîyan li wan çênebe û bi derengî bikeve bê li ku ne, heft jin girtin ji avjanîya, qirşvanîya û anîn danîn bin konê birayê Xecê û gotin, "yabo va me heft jin ji we re anîn de ka ya me bidin me, hîn sibe ye li me dereng e, divê em herin".
1519. Early in the morning they got up and went far so that quickly inquiries would not arise upon them and it would fall late where they are, they took seven wives from swimmers, brushwood-gatherers and brought put them under the tent of Xecê's brother and said, "father here we brought seven wives for you then well give ours to us, still it is morning it is late upon us, we must go".

1520. Xorşîd (birayê Xecê): Wele divê em herin cil û xişran ji wan re bikirin.
1520. Xorşîd (the brother of Xecê): By God we must go buy clothes and jewelry for them.

1521. Sîyamend: Meriv dûr e, her yek ji me bila dergîsîya xwe bixemilîne.
1521. Sîyamend: Man it is far, each one of us let him adorn his fiancée.

1522. Xorşîd: Nabe, wilo nabe, va bajarê Elcewazê di bin çengê me de ye, û em ê herin cil û bergan, xişr û zêran bikirin û em ê bên.
1522. Xorşîd: It does not become, so it does not become, here the city of Elcewaz is under our arm (nearby), and we will go buy clothes and garments, jewelry and gold and we will come.

1523. Siyamend (li ber digere): Mervo em dest teng in, rêya me dûr e, ka yabo Xecê em herin.
1523. Sîyamend (pleads with him): Man we are narrow-handed (poor), our road is far, well father Xecê let us go.

1524. Xorşîd: Çênabe pismam, xwişka me ya tenê ye delalî ye, bê xeml û rihel em nadin.
1524. Xorşîd: It does not arise (it is not possible) cousin, our sister is an only one she is a dear one, without adornment and trousseau we do not give.

1525. Rabun zilaman karên xwe kirin û li hespan siwar bûn û berê xwe dan Elcewazê.
1525. They got up the men did their works and mounted the horses and turned their direction to Elcewaz.

1526. Bi rê ketin tilbabekî meşîyan, Sîyamend di dilê xwe de got: "Aniha wê xwedîyên van jina bên û wê qîzê xwe bibin, hîn em venegerîyane", û bang kir Xorşîd,
1526. They set on the road walked a while, Sîyamend said in his heart: "Right now the owners of these wives will come and they will take their girls, still we have not returned", and called out to Xorşîd,

1527. Siyamend: Pismam em ê zilam herin, ne durist e em van jina, qîza bi tenê bihêlin.
1527. Sîyamend: Cousin we men will go, it is not proper we leave these wives, girls alone.

1528. Xorşîd: Çima?
1528. Xorşîd: Why?

1529. Çi heye?
1529. What is there?

1530. Ma xwene wê gur wan bixwin, an diz wan birevînin?
1530. After all will wolves eat them, or thieves abduct them?

1531. Siyamend: Nabe pismam, hema ji karekî, îşekî, mêvanekî, pêdiviyekê.
1531. Sîyamend: It does not become (it is not good) cousin, just from a work, a business, a guest, a need.

1532. De hema bila birayê min Qeregêtran li mal bimîne û em ê herin.
1532. Then just let my brother Qeregêtran remain at home and we will go.

1533. Tibabeki meşîyan, Siyamend got: "Gelî pismaman bimeşin îşekî min bi birayê min hey, û ez ê zû li we vegerim".
1533. They walked a while, Sîyamend said: "O cousins walk I have a business with my brother, and I will quickly return to you".

1534. Hespa xwe dagerand û da telebê hate cem Qeregêtrên.
1534. He turned his horse and put to a gallop came to Qeregêtran.

1535. Siyamend: birayê min weleh ez ê te girê dim ya ez ê te biçînim.
1535. Sîyamend: my brother by God I will tie you or I will plant you (bury you).

1536. Qeregêtran: Kuro law, çilo tê min girê dî!
1536. Qeregêtran: Boy boy, how will you tie me!

1537. Û hema xwedîyê wan hatin?
1537. And just if their owners came?

1538. Bihêl ez karekî, tiştekî bikim, wa vegerînim.
1538. Leave me let me do a work, a thing, return them.

1539. Siyamend: Wele birayê min ez li te ewle nabim, belkî di dû min re tu Xecê birevîne û ji xwe re bibe?
1539. Sîyamend: By God my brother I do not become secure in you (trust you), perhaps behind me you will abduct Xecê and take her for yourself?

1540. Qeregêtran: Batil batil, pek û sed carî pek, kuro ev çi çêra xerab ketîye dilê te de?!
1540. Qeregêtran: False false, pop and a hundred times pop (nonsense), boy what bad grazing (thought) has fallen into your heart?!

1541. Kuro kesekî ev bêbextî bi birayê xwe re kirîye?
1541. Boy has anyone done this treachery with his brother?

1542. lawo kuro wê xelk bên qîzê xwe, jinê xwe bibin, wê min jî bikujin û Xecê jî bibin law.
1542. boy boy the people will come take their girls, their wives, they will kill me too and take Xecê too boy.

1543. Siyamend lahor kişandîye û dûrî kun erd kolaye û Qeregêtran xistîye, çandîye serî tenê ji derve hiştîye û jê re got: "Çavê te li wan be".
1543. Sîyamend has drawn the scimitar and far from the tent has dug the ground and has put Qeregêtran, has planted him only the head has left from the outside and said to him: "Let your eye be on them".

1544. Siyamend vegerîya giha birayên Xecê û çûn Elcewazê xemil û rihela bûkan kirîn heya bazar kirin û heya li hev kirin û kirîn
1544. Sîyamend returned reached the brothers of Xecê and went to Elcewaz bought adornment and trousseau of the brides until they bargained and until they agreed and bought

1545. cilê heşt bûkan e giran e li wan bû êvar.
1545. it is the clothes of eight brides it is heavy it became evening upon them.

1546. Pirsîyan li van qîzan, jinan çêbû.
1546. Inquiries arose upon these girls, wives.

1547. Xelkê ji wan re gotin, "wele qîz û jinên we di mala Xorşîdê Şikakî de ne".
1547. The people said to them, "by God your girls and wives are in the house of Xorşîd of Şikak".

1548. Xwedîyên van jinan li hespan siwar bûn û cil û çekên xwe li xwe kirin û hatin şerê birayê Xecê, çilo qîz û jinên wan revandine.
1548. The owners of these wives mounted the horses and put their clothes and weapons on themselves and came to the fight of Xecê's brother, how they have abducted their girls and wives.

1549. Siwar û gundî hatin bin konê bavê Xecê, yê hat qîza xwe bir, yê hat xwişka xwe bir û yê hat jina xwe bir, û her yekî ji wan vegerîya mala xwe.
1549. The riders and villagers came under the tent of Xecê's father, whoever came took his girl, whoever came took his sister and whoever came took his wife, and each one of them returned to his home.

1550. Dema ji bin kun derketin, dîtin serîkî insana wa li wê dera ha ye, yekî şûrek di zîlana hustê de lê xist rehek dido qut kirin, serê Qeregêtran xiîlya, bû pingîna mêşa li ser serê wî.
