1874. Then with sticks the people were sending their buckets and he too was filling water from the spring of the well and lifting and the head of the merchant was taking money from them until it fell to the evening time, all drank full water together with the beasts.

1875. Zîrek werîs hejand û deng da: "Min bikşînin, min bikşînin".
1875. Zîrek shook the rope and gave a sound: "Pull me, pull me".

1876. Du kesa bi milê wî girtin û ew kişandin ber qefê û jê pirsîn, "xorto, ka bibêje bê çi li dinyayê şêrîn û xweş e?"
1876. Two persons caught his arm and pulled him before the edge and asked him, "youth, well tell let's see what is sweet and pleasant in the world?"

1877. Zîrek pojinî, û mitale kir, "çi şêrîn e, çi xweş e?"
1877. Zîrek pondered, and considered, "what is sweet, what is pleasant?"

1878. Hat ramanê wî ku zêrek di vê bazarê de daye û got: "Dilketina qîz û xortan tiştê herî xweş û şêrîn e li dinyayê".
1878. It came to his thought that he has given a gold coin in this bargain and said: "The heart-falling (falling in love) of girls and youths is the most pleasant and sweet thing in the world".

1879. Her du kesan qîz û xortek bûn, hevûdu revandibûn.
1879. Both persons were a girl and a youth, they had abducted each other.

1880. Du lib hinar bexşîş û dîyarî danê û jê re gotin, "oxir be ji te re here derkeve ji bîrê".
1880. They gave him two grains of pomegranate as a tip and gift and said to him, "let it be a good journey for you go come out of the well".

1881. Zîrek bi dengekî bilind ji binê bîrê dîsa bang kir û got: "Min bikşînin, min derxînin".
1881. Zîrek with a loud voice from the bottom of the well again called out and said: "Pull me, take me out".

1882. Xelkê kerwên û bazirgan man gosretmayî ew ji binê bîrê kişandin.
1882. The people of the caravan and the merchants remained bewildered they pulled him from the bottom of the well.

1883. Sax derket.
1883. He came out alive.

1884. Kêfa serokê wî gelekî hat û şahî jê re çêkir, berî kerwanê xwe bar bikin.
1884. The pleasure of his head greatly came and he made a celebration for him, before they load their caravan.

1885. Zîrek her du hinar (tijî libê cewheran e) dan mamosteyê xwe û pereyê jê re kom kirbûn, û pîra dêya xwe û Zelîxayê re şandin.
1885. Zîrek gave both pomegranates (it is full of grains of jewels) to his master and the money they had gathered for him, and sent them for his old mother and Zelîxa.

1886. Kerwanên bazirganîyan bar kirin û berên xwe dan oxira xwe bajarên Heleb û Şamê.
1886. The caravans of the merchants loaded and turned their direction to their journey the cities of Heleb and Şam.

1887. Kirîn û firotinê dikin û bi vî halî, bazirgan li her derê disekine û kirîn û firotinê dike û wilo heya digihêjin Şamê û vedigerin Amedê, zêdî salekê çêdibe.
1887. They do buying and selling and with this condition, the merchant stops at every place and does buying and selling and so until they reach Şam and return to Amed, more than a year happens.

1888. Kerwan bar kir û bi jêr de dimeşe, qûnax bi qûnax û xan bi xan, pêrgî bazirganê ji Şam û Helebê tên û berê wan li Amedê ye.
1888. The caravan loaded and walks downwards, stage by stage and inn by inn, they met the merchants who come from Şam and Heleb and their direction is to Amed.

1889. Li hev sekinîn û pirsa bazaran kirin û nameyên xwe, kesên bazirgan, karker û xwedîyên kerwanan dan wan ji bo xatirê ku bigihînin mirovên wan li welêt.
1889. They stopped at each other and did the question of the markets and gave their letters, the persons of the merchants, workers and owners of the caravans gave to them for the sake that they bring them to their people in the country.

1890. Başbazirganê Zîrek jê re got: "Zîrek va mal û perê te gelek çêbûne û tu bi ya min dikî, tê bi vî bazirganî re vegerî malê û perê xwe bi xwe re bibî".
1890. The chief merchant of Zîrek said to him: "Zîrek here your wealth and money have become much and you do by mine (if you listen to me), you will return home with this merchant and take your money with yourself".

1891. Zîrek: Na begê min, ez ji oxira xwe venagerim, ji min re zêr û pere û hinarekê bişîne ji Zelîxayê re, va navnîşan ev e, û bera hinarek bimîne, nêvî min û te be û em ê pê bazirganîyê bikin.
1891. Zîrek: No my beg, I do not return from my journey, send gold and money and a pomegranate for me to Zelîxa, here the address is this, and let a pomegranate remain, let it be half for me and you and we will do commerce with it.

1892. Pere û zêr û hinarek ji cewahir ji Zelîxayê re bi başbazirgan re şandin.
1892. Money and gold and a pomegranate of jewels for Zelîxa were sent with the chief merchant.

1893. Û Zîrek bû hevkar û hevbeşê bazirganîya mamosteyê xwe û berê xwe dan Helebê û Şamê, ji bo kirîn û firotina bazirganîya xwe bikin.
1893. And Zîrek became coworker and partner of the commerce of his master and turned their direction to Heleb and Şam, to do the buying and selling of their commerce.

1894. Başbazirganê Heleb û Şamê giha Amedê, li ser navnîşanê, nameya Zîrek û mal û pere dan Zelîxayê, piştî Zelîxe nameya Zîrek xwend, nas kir ku pere û zêr çilo dan hev û çilo du heb hinarê cewher danê di bîrê de.
1894. The chief merchant of Heleb and Şam reached Amed, upon the address, gave the letter of Zîrek and wealth and money to Zelîxa, after Zelîxa read the letter of Zîrek, she recognized how he gathered money and gold and how they gave two pieces of pomegranates of jewels to him in the well.

1895. Zelîxe rabû cil û bergê xort û zilaman li xwe kirin, û dest bi avanîya qesr û qûnaxa kir, di gêla bajêr de, û carê hinek ji kevirê cewher xurde dike,û xerc dike, kuşkek mezin û bilind û fireh ava kir wek kuşka bavê xwe, û cil û ber lê raxistin wek yê mala bavê, û hemû firax û tepsî û şûşe û kevçî û kursî û mase, her tişt wek yê mala bavê wê ye, ne mûk kêm, ne yek zêde.
1895. Zelîxa got up put the clothes and garments of youths and men on herself, and started the building of castles and mansions, in the center of the city, and sometimes breaks some of the stones of jewels into change, and spends them, built a big and high and wide palace like the palace of her father, and spread carpets and rugs in it like those of the father's house, and all dishes and trays and glasses and spoons and chairs and tables, everything is like those of her father's house, not a hair less, not one more.

1896. Kesekî ji bajêr Zelîxa nas nekir, û kes nizane ku jin e.
1896. No one from the city recognized Zelîxa, and no one knows that she is a woman.

1897. Ji pêvî yekî cad û kar, dida dû Zelîxe bi şev bi roj, bi dizî kir û nekir, tu çiq nekir, û kula dilê wî xwe bigihîne Zelîxe.
1897. Except for a witch and worker (a sorcerer), he was giving behind (following) Zelîxa by night by day, secretly he did and did not (tried everything), he made no crack (made no progress), and the wound of his heart is to reach himself to Zelîxa.

1898. Dem derbas bûn, sal zîvirî, kerwanê baziganîyan nêzîkayî kirin, name diçin û tên di orta karker, bazirgan û malên wan de.
1898. Times passed, the year turned, the caravan of merchants approached, letters go and come in the middle of workers, merchants and their homes.

1899. Bazirgan rojava kete nav bajêr û berê xwe dan xan û imbara malên xwe daxistin ser pişta dewaran, heya mal bi cih
1899. The merchants at sunset fell into the city and turned their direction to the inns and warehouses brought their goods down onto the back of the animals, until goods in place

1900. kirin başbazirgan û Zîrek di ser serê karkeran re diçin û tên, û heya şîv ji wan re danîn kete nîvê şevê.
1900. they made (they placed the goods) the chief merchant and Zîrek go and come over the head of the workers, and until they put down dinner for them it fell to midnight.

1901. Zîrek berê xwe da malê û dilezîne, bi kêf e û devliken e, kengî wê pîra dêya xwe û dergîsîya xwe bibîne, yeqîn nake bigihê malê.
1901. Zîrek turned his direction to the house and hurries, he is with joy and is smiling, when will he see his old mother and his fiancée, he does not believe to reach home.

1902. Zelîxe jî li hêvîya dergîsîyê xwe ye bi kêf û şahî, û di dilê xwe de dibêje: Ez ê pêşwazîya wî bikim bi xeml û xêza bûkanîyê, û ez ê wî li kuşkê bigerînim, ode bi ode, û kursî û masê tê de û berên raxistî, û sibehê em ê mehra xwe bibirin, û em ê şû bikin bi kêf û şahî.
1902. Zelîxa too is in hope of her fiancé with joy and celebration, and says in her heart: I will do his welcoming with the adornment and drawing of bridal state, and I will tour him in the palace, room by room, and chairs and tables in it and the spread rugs, and in the morning we will cut our marriage, and we will wed with joy and celebration.

1903. Û kete ser şoka avgermê xwe biso û veşo û cilê zilama bavêje û xeml û xêza bûkanîyê li xwe bike û pêşwazîya dergîsîyê xwe bike.
1903. And she fell upon the shock of the hot water to wash and cleanse herself and throw the clothes of men and put the adornment and drawing of bridal state on herself and do the welcoming of her fiancé.

1904. Çawa Zîrek derbasî hewşê bû, pîra dêya wî li devê derî li hêvîyê bû, pîra dêya wî ew girt û berneda heya serê wî dagirt bi derew û bêbextîya, û gelacîya jinkê kir û got: Law kurê min, ev çi jin bû te xiste hundir, xwe kirbû zilam û cilê zilama li xwe kirin û bi şev û bi roj di nav xorta û meyvexura de, û bi ser serîya re digerîya, bi qehpetî, qûnekî, pîsitî.
1904. As soon as Zîrek passed into the courtyard, his old mother was at the mouth of the door in hope, his old mother caught him and did not let go until she filled his head with lies and treacheries, and did the backbiting of the woman and said: Boy my son, what woman was this you put inside, had made herself a man and put the clothes of men on herself and by night and by day among youths and wine-drinkers, and was touring over the heads, with whoredom, faggotry, dirtiness.

1905. Pepûkê Zîrek şaş û hêbetmayî ma, gêjomêjo bû, dunya li dora serê wî dizîvirî, hiş û aqil di serî de nema ji qehra û gotina.
1905. Wretched Zîrek remained confused and awe-struck, he became dizzy, the world was turning around his head, mind and reason remained not in the head from the wraths and the words.

1906. Çawa pepûka Zelîxe hat pêşwazîya wî, xwelîsero dinya li ber çavên wî reş bûye, hema ji hêrs û kerba xencer kişand û Zelîxe da ber xencera, ew bê hiş xiste erdê.
1906. As soon as wretched Zelîxa came to his welcoming, ash-on-head (wretch) the world has become black before his eyes, just from anger and grief he drew a dagger and gave Zelîxa before daggers, put her without mind to the ground.

1907. Piştî derbas bû kuşkê û li odeyê û dîwana nerî, li kursî û masa, li tej û bera, poşman bû.
1907. After he passed to the palace and looked at the room and the court, at chairs and tables, at scraps and rugs, he became regretful.

1908. Vegerîya û got: "Ev giş bêbextî bûn, û dûv re ev qîza paşê ye ku bibihîze wê serê min jê bike".
1908. Returned and said: "These all were treachery, and afterwards this is the girl of the paşa if he hears he will cut my head off".

1909. ma heyirî wê çilo bike, rabû wê şevê çû mala yekî xerat û tabûtek kirî anî û Zelîxe xiste tê de, û pembo û derman bi ser wer kir û nas kir hîn saxe, rahiştêli pişta xwe kir wê şevê û anî avêt çemê mezin û vegerîya malê.
1909. remained bewildered how he will do, got up that night went to the house of a carpenter and bought a coffin brought and put Zelîxa in it, and threw cotton and medicine upon it and recognized she is still alive, picked it up put it on his back that night and brought threw it into the big river and returned home.

1910. Ro derket, li qesr û qûnaxa nerî, bê heydê jinkê çi kuşk û sera ava kirine, û ji xelk û cîrana pirsî nas kir ku dêya wî bêbextî kirîye.
1910. The sun came out, he looked at the castles and mansions, let's see oh my what palaces and manors the woman has built, and asked from the people and neighbors recognized that his mother has done treachery.

1911. Derî giş girtin û kilît kirin û kuşka xwe û malê di xanê de giş emanetî başbazirgan kir û hespek ji xanê derxist, xurcezîna
1911. Closed all doors and locked and made his palace and the wealth in the inn all a trust to the chief merchant and took a horse out of the inn, saddlebags

1912. wê lê kir û tijî zêr û xwarin û vexwarin kir, siwar bû û ber jêr bû di kêleka çem re û hêdî hêdî da dû Zelîxe.
1912. he put on it and filled it with gold and food and drink, mounted and went downwards by the side of the river and slowly slowly gave behind (followed) Zelîxa.

1913. Mêrekî cadûkar jî rojek dido derbas bûn, pêjna jinkê nekir, hat dora mala wê pirsî, pirsî nas kir ku birîndar e û di çem de ye.
1913. A sorcerer man too one day two passed, did not sense the woman, came around her house asked, asked recognized that she is wounded and is in the river.

1914. Wî jî kar û barê xwe kir û li hespê xwe siwar bû û çem û çem ber jêr bû û da dû tabûta Zelîxe.
1914. He too did his work and affairs and mounted on his horse and river by river went downwards and gave behind (followed) the coffin of Zelîxa.

1915. Rok dido derbas bûn, yekî nêçîrvanê masîya li ber çem tora xwe bi şev di çem de girê dabû, serê sibê dema ji malê hat, tora xwe kişand, kişand, nerî bê çi girane, hêdî hêdî dikşîne nerî jora tabûtekê (sebetekê) xuya kir got: Belkî Xwedê rizqek ji me re şandîye, kêfa wî hat û tora xwe kişand ber kevîya çem û jora wê vekir, sibhan ji navê xwedê re bê çi jinek sipehî û xweşik, bi xeml û xêza xwe di nav xwînê de maye.
1915. One day two passed, a hunter of fishes (fisherman) by the river had tied his net by night in the river, early in the morning when he came from home, he pulled his net, pulled, looked let's see how heavy it is, slowly slowly pulls looked the top of a coffin (a basket) appeared he said: Perhaps God has sent a provision for us, his pleasure came and he pulled his net to the edge of the river and opened the top of it, glory to the name of God let's see what a pretty and beautiful woman, with her adornment and drawing has remained in the middle of blood.

1916. Nêçîrvan lê temaşe kir û dît ku tamarê xwîna wê dilebitin, û dilê wê lê dixe hêdî deng dide.
1916. The hunter watched her and saw that her blood veins flutter (pulsate), and her heart beats slowly gives a sound.

1917. Hema rahiştê bire ser pişta kerê xwe kir û bir malê, û birînê wê şûştin û paqij kirin û derman kirin, û bi kevçîya hinek rûnê Zelîxe hilandî û şorbe xiste devê wê, û ma lê miqate bi şev û roj, bi derman û xwarin jinik bi ser hişê xwe ve hat, rok dido deh, jinkê çavên xwe vekirin, hê, ka ez li ku derê me, çi bi serê min hatîye?
1917. Just he picked her up took put her upon the back of his donkey and took home, and washed her wounds and cleaned and treated them, and with spoons put some melted fat of Zelîxa (melted butter) and soup into her mouth, and remained careful of her by night and day, with medicine and food the woman came upon her mind (regained consciousness), one day two ten, the woman opened her eyes, hey, well at where am I, what has come upon my head?

1918. ez çilo hatime vir?
1918. how have I come here?

1919. Nêçîrvan: Tu birîndar bû, di tabûtekê de bû, di çem de bû, kete tora min.
1919. Hunter: You were wounded, you were in a coffin, you were in the river, fell into my net.

1920. Û min tu anî malê û bi şûştin û derman Xwedê tu sax kir.
1920. And I brought you home and with washing and medicine God made you alive (healed you).

1921. Mehek, dido, sisê Zelîxe hat ser derba xwe, û qîzanîye xwe, rind û sipehî tema nêçîrvan lê xerabû, û xwest li xwe şobike.
1921. One month, two, three Zelîxa came upon her strike (recovered), and her maidenhood, beautiful and pretty the greed of the hunter ruined upon her (he coveted her), and wanted to wed her to himself.

1922. Jinkê nas kir ku nêta mêrik xerabe, rabû di nîvê şeveke reş û tarî de cilê nêçîrvan li xwe kirin, û li hespê wî siwar bû û derket revîya, û tim û tim ber jêr bû bi çem re dimeşe, û dikudîne.
1922. The woman recognized that the intention of the man is bad, got up in the middle of a black and dark night put the clothes of the hunter on herself, and mounted on his horse and went out fled, and always and always went downwards walks by the river, and gallops.

1923. Nêçîrvan sibê rabû ji xew ku her nêçîrê, nerî ne cil û ne hesp, hema wî jî li kerekê siwar bû û da dû, çem û çem çû.
1923. The hunter in the morning got up from sleep when he goes to hunting, looked neither clothes and nor horse, just he too mounted on a donkey and gave behind, river and river went.

1924. Zelîxe li hespê xwe siwar e, nizane wê bi ku derê de here, carekê rêke bazirganîya kete ber, wê jî da ser rê got: Belkî li şarekî, bajarekî rast bêm, ez karîbim eborekê ji xwe re bikim, gepek nanê xwe pê bixum, daye dû kerwana û dimeşe, gihan bajarekî mezin, hawîrdor sûr û bend kirî ye.
1924. Zelîxa is mounted on her horse, does not know to where she will go, once a road of commerce fell before her, she too gave upon the road said: Perhaps I will come across a city, a town, I will be able to make a livelihood for myself, eat a bite of my bread with it, gave behind the caravans and walks, they reached a big city, surroundings made a wall and barrier.

1925. Li xan û dana kirwan peya bûn, Zelîxe jî hespê xwe xiste xanê û çû cihê razanê, xwe rihet kir, bi cilê zilama ye, ji bo karekî, îşekî ji xwe re peyda bike.
1925. At the inns and stations the caravans dismounted, Zelîxa too put her horse in the inn and went to the place of sleeping, rested herself, she is with the clothes of men, for to provide a work, a business for herself.

1926. Bi banga serê sibê re, bangêr di menara, û ser pişta xanîya, û li zikaka, bang didin û dibêjin: Şevê çû paşê me çû ber dilovanîya Xwedê.
1926. With the call of early morning, criers in minarets, and on the back of houses, and in alleys, give a call and say: The night that went our paşa went before the mercy of God.

1927. Gundî, malî, jin, zilam, zarok, xelkê bajêr giş derketin cada û zikaka û guhdarî dikirin, û bangêr dibêjin: Hêê gelê gundîya û mirov û dosta, em ê paşe di nîvro de veşêrin, û piştî em ji ser goristanê vegerin, em ê bazê dewletêberdin, ku bazê şahîn li ser serê kê deyne wê ew bibe paşe û şahê dewletê, hêê kes di malê de nemîne ha.
1927. Villagers, household members, women, men, children, the people of the city all went out to the streets and alleys and were listening, and the criers say: Hey the people of villagers and relatives and friends, we will bury the paşa at noon, and after we return from upon the graveyard, we will release the falcon of the state, that the falcon of kings on whose head it puts (lands) he will become paşa and king of the state, hey let no one remain in the house ha.

1928. ## Li Goristanê
1928. ## At the Graveyard

1929. Xort û karmendên goristanê tirbeke mezin û xweşik ji Şahê xwe re dikolin û dibêjin: Belkî mirovê wî, kizîrê wî bên hinek pere bidin me, û xêreke mezin lê bidin qene em têr bixwin.
1929. The youths and workers of the graveyard dig a big and beautiful tomb for their King and say: Perhaps his relatives, his viziers will come give some money to us, and will give a big alms (charity) on it so that we eat full.

1930. Mela û feqe û suxte li pala gir di ser tirbê re rûniştine û Quranê dixwînin, ew jî ji bo hinek pere bistînin, û sofî û mela dibêjin: Em ê ji wezîrê wî re bibêjin: Divê em pêncî olçek genim lê bihêjînin, di ber gunehê wî de, ji bo wî genimî ji xwe re bibin malê.
1930. Mullahs and students and softas (theology students) have sat at the slope of the hill over the tomb and read the Quran, they too to take some money, and sufis and mullahs say: We will say to his vizier: We must sift fifty measures of wheat on it, for his sins, to take that wheat for ourselves home.

1931. Gundî û xelk li hawîrdor rûniştî ne, û her yek ji xwe re û bi hevalê xwe re dipeyive, hin dibêjin: We paşê ne dilovan bû, baş bû nan û xwarin dida feqîran, û hin dibêjin: Wele paşakî zordar bû xelk eşkence dikirin, û dixistin zindanan de, û hin dibêjin: Erê zalim û zordar bû, lê rehma wî jî hebû, di êvarên înan û di cejnan de xêr didan.
1931. Villagers and people have sat in the surroundings, and each one speaks for himself and with his friend, some say: Oh wasn't the paşa merciful, he was good he was giving bread and food to the poor, and some say: By God he was an oppressive paşa he was torturing the people, and throwing them in prisons, and some say: Yes he was cruel and oppressive, but his mercy too existed, on Friday evenings and on holidays they were giving alms.

1932. Bi vî halî hin pesnê wî didan û qencîyê wî dibêjin, û hin dev davênê û xerabîyê wî dibêjin, û wilo heya term hat xelk giş rabûn ser xwe mela û feqa û sofîya li ser nimêj kirin, û suxta Yasîn dixwendin, dahiştin tirbê, ax lê vegerandin, telqîn xwendin, bi pêş gotina Quranê, û berê xwe dan malê, bangêr bang kir: Hêê, em ê bazê Şahîn berdin ha.
1932. With this condition some were giving his praise and say his goodness, and some throw mouth at him (criticize) and say his badness, and so until the corpse came the people all got up on themselves mullahs and students and sufis prayed upon him, and theology students were reading Yasin, they lowered him to the tomb, returned earth on it, read the telqîn (last rites), with the reciting of the Quran, and turned their direction home, the crier called out: Hey, we will release the falcon of kings ha.

1933. Kesek nekevin hundira û xanîya, û herkes derkevin gasîna, cada, ser pişta xanîya, hêê, kes di hundira de nemîne haa.
1933. Let no one fall into insides and houses, and everyone go out to squares, streets, on the back of houses, hey, let no one remain in insides haa.

1934. Wezîr û kizîr û şêwirdar, û dadmendê dewletêgiş li sasîna bajêr sekinîn, û bazê Şahîn berdan, baz firîya, firîya, û gerîya û rist rist di ser serê xelkê re û li bajêr gişî gerîya, li dora sûr û bendê, çû û hat û li ser serê Zelîxe danî, kesekî xerîbe nû hatîye bajêr, kes wî nas nake, rabû bazê xwe girtin û birin xistin dîwana şah de, û Zelîxe ji wir birin cihekî din nav kumek zilam, û çûn careke din bazê xwe berdan, bazê şah rist rist û hat li ser serê Zelîxe danî, bû elah elahê xelkê û gotin: Ku ev zilam ne ji cihekî mezin ba, û ne kurê şahekî ba, yan mîrekî li welatêjê hatîye, lewma baz li ser serî datîne.
1934. The viziers and deputies and counselors, and the judges of the state all stood at the square of the city, and released the falcon of kings, the falcon flew, flew, and toured and circled circled over the heads of the people and toured the whole city, around the walls and barriers, went and came and put (landed) on the head of Zelîxa, a strange person newly has come to the city, no one recognizes him, got up caught their falcon and took put it in the court of the king, and took Zelîxa from there to another place among a group of men, and went once again released their falcon, the falcon of kings circled circled and came put (landed) on the head of Zelîxa, it became the "Allah Allah" of the people (the people's exclamation of awe) and they said: If this man were not from a big place, and were not the son of a king, or a mîr in the country he has come from, therefore the falcon puts (lands) on the head.

1935. Şêwirmenda gotin: Cara sêsya heger li ser serê ev camêrî danî wê ewê bibe paş e û şahê me, û rabûn careke din baz xistin cihekî reş, û Zelîxe birin odeyakê û cil û bergê cû lê kirin û ebak bi ser de, û li civatekê rûniştin û gotin: Bazê Şah berdin.
1935. The counselors said: The third time if it puts (lands) on the head of this gentleman he will become our paşa and king, and got up once again put the falcon in a black place, and took Zelîxa to a room and put different clothes and garments on her and an aba upon them, and sat in an assembly and said: Release the falcon of the King.

1936. Baz berdan, baz firîya firîya li dora bajêr gerîya û rist rist û hat careke din li ser serê Zelîxe danî, bû elah elaha xelkê û gotin: Ew şah e û şah kurê şaha ye û bazê Şêh sê caran li ser serê wî danîye, û xelkê civatê di dîwana mîr de giş rabûn pîrozbahîya şahê nû kirin, û birin odeya şah, cilê şahetîyê li xwe kirin û hat li ser kursîya şah rûnişt û tac dan serî, û wezîr, şêwirdar, û dadmend li pêşbera şah her yek li cihê xwe rûniştin.
1936. They released the falcon, the falcon flew flew toured around the city and circled circled and came once again put (landed) on the head of Zelîxa, it became the "Allah Allah" of the people and they said: He is a king and a king is the son of kings and the falcon of the King has put (landed) on his head three times, and the people of the assembly in the court of the mîr all got up did the congratulation of the new king, and they took him to the room of the king, put the clothes of kingship on himself and he came sat on the chair of the king and they gave a crown to the head, and viziers, counselors, and judges before the king each one sat in his place.

1937. Paşê nûhilbijartî, rabû serê sibê li nav bajêr gerîya, bê ka çi dikin û aborîya milet çawa ye, û vegerîya dîwanê û gelek ferman derxistin ji bo kar û îşê milet, û jîyana wan xweştir bibe, û wê neyê xweyî keçkanî û bi xeml û xêz li jora dergehê
1937. The newly elected paşa, got up early in the morning toured in the city, let's see well what they do and how the economy of the nation is, and returned to the court and took out many orders for the work and business of the nation, and their life becomes more pleasant, and a picture of herself girl-like and with adornment and drawing at the top of the gate

1938. sûrê xest û denek av danî û dergevan wê çav dêrbe li her çar derîyê sûrê û ji wan re got: Kî hat av vexwar ji rêwîya û sekinî û bi kul û xem li wêneyê keçikê nerî, yan pirsa wê kir, hûnê wî bigirin û bînin dîwana şah, û jinkê kar û barê şahitîya xwe kir, bê kesek wê nas bike ku jine.
1938. of the wall she requested (hung) and put a vat of water and a gatekeeper will be watcher at all four doors of the wall and she said to them: Whoever came drank water from the travelers and stood and with wound and sorrow looked at the picture of the girl, or asked her question (asked about her), you will catch him and bring to the court of the king, and the woman did the work and affairs of her kingship, without anyone recognizing her that she is a woman.

1939. Mehek, dido, sisê derbas bûn, hersê rêwî hîn bi dû de digerin (mêrê wê Zîrek, û cadûkar, û nêçîrvan).
1939. One month, two, three passed, all three travelers still go around behind (her) (her husband Zîrek, and the sorcerer, and the hunter).

1940. Nêçîrvan: Ji hal ketîye, li kera xwe siwar bi rêwî û kerwana re hat wî bajarî, li devê derîyê sûrê sekinîn û av vexwarin, û derbas bûn, nêçîrvan jî dema av vexwar li jor nerî çavên wî li wêneyê keçikê ket, şaş ma û ziq li wêne dinere û keserek kûr da û got: Ka ez ê te li ku bibînim û te li ku bigirim?
1940. Hunter: Has fallen from condition, mounted on his donkey with travelers and caravans came to that city, at the mouth of the door of the wall they stopped and drank water, and passed, the hunter too when he drank water looked up his eyes fell upon the picture of the girl, he remained confused and stares intently at the picture and gave a deep sigh and said: Well where will I see you and where will I catch you?

1941. hema dergevan bi qeperê girt, û ew bire dîwana şah.
1941. just the gatekeeper caught him by the collar, and took him to the court of the king.

1942. Zelîxe lê nerî ew nas kir ku nêçîrvan û bijîjkê wê ye, temînîya wî kir û xistin odeyakê de, bi xwarin û vexwarin û miqate bûn.
1942. Zelîxa looked at him recognized him that he is her hunter and doctor, made his assurance and they put him in a room, with food and drink and they became careful of him (attended to him).

1943. Cadûkar: Çendak derbas bû, ê cadûkar jî bi kerwanê bazirgana re hat wî bajarî, li ber dergehê sûrê peyabûn, kerwan derbas bû, cadû dar westîyaye, hat ser denê avê tasa xwe têdakir û vexwar, çavên wî li wêneyê keçikê ket got: Ah bi Xwedê min nêzîkayî lê kirîye, li vi bajarî ye, û hema lê dinere û dibêje: Ma vê derbê tu nema ji destê min xelas dibe, min zanîbû tu qîzî û keçikî, lê min nikarîbû ez tiştekî bikim, û ziq li wêne dinere, dergevan bi qepera wî jî girt û anî dîwana şah.
1943. Sorcerer: A while passed, the sorcerer too with the caravan of the merchants came to that city, before the gate of the wall they dismounted, the caravan passed, the sorcerer has gotten tired, came upon the vat of water put his bowl in it and drank, his eyes fell upon the picture of the girl he said: Ah by God I have done closeness to her (gotten close to her), she is in this city, and just looks at it and says: After all this time you no longer get saved from my hand, I had known you are a maiden and a girl, but I was not able to do a thing, and stares intently at the picture, the gatekeeper caught him too by his collar and brought him to the court of the king.

1944. Zelîxe lê nerî ew nas kir ku cadûkare, ferman da û got wî bibin zindanê û çavên we lê be, ne reve ji zindanê.
1944. Zelîxa looked at him recognized him that he is the sorcerer, gave an order and said take him to the prison and let your eyes be on him, he does not flee from the prison.

1945. Zîrek: Bi kul û xeme zikê wî tijeye ji qehra û kerba, bi lez û bez digere û dipirse, ne bi şev û ne bi roj nasekine, ew û hespê xwe her du çûne helakê, ew jî li kerwanekî biçûk rast û bi ware berê xwe da wî bajarî, qene çend rokî xwe lê rihet bike, û here xanekê têrrazê û hespê wî jî bi ser xwe ve bê.
1945. Zîrek: He is with wound and sorrow his stomach is full of wrath and grief, with haste and running he walks around and asks, neither by night and nor by day he stops, he and his horse both have gone to ruin, he too came across a small caravan and with them gave his direction to that city, so that he rests himself in it for a few days, and goes to an inn sleeps full and his horse too comes upon itself (recovers).

1946. Zîrek û kerwan hatin li ber dergehê sûrê rawestîyan xwe vegesînin, Zîrek jî hat ser devê avê û tas têdakir û hilda av vexwar, çavên wî li wêneyê Zelîxe ket, di cih de axîn û oxîn jê hat û got: Hewar hewar Zelîxe, ka tu li ku ma?
1946. Zîrek and the caravan came stood before the gate of the wall to rest themselves, Zîrek too came upon the mouth of the water and put the bowl in it and lifted drank water, his eyes fell upon the picture of Zelîxa, in place groaning and moaning came from him and said: Cry for help cry for help Zelîxa, well where did you remain?

1947. tu çûyî bi ku derê de?
1947. to wherever did you go?

1948. ezê çilo te bibînim?
1948. how will I see you?

1949. min bi destê xwe mala xwe xerakir, lê ez çibikim, çûye derbas bûye.
1949. I with my hand ruined my home, but what shall I do, it has gone it has passed.

1950. Ya Xwedanê şev û roj têcarekê destê min û wê têxe hev.
1950. O Master of night and day you will one time put my hand and hers together.

1951. Hema dergevan bi çeplê wî girt û ew bir dîwana şah.
1951. Just the gatekeeper caught his arm and took him to the court of the king.

1952. Zelîxe nerî nas kir û dilê wê gelekî pê şewitî, bê Zîrek ketîye çi halî, mest û jar û rezîl bûye, bê xwarin, bê razan, ne sekin û ne hedan.
1952. Zelîxa looked recognized and her heart greatly burned with it, let's see into what condition Zîrek has fallen, he has become intoxicated (dazed) and miserable and wretched, without food, without sleeping, neither stopping and nor resting.

1953. Şah (Zelîxe) ferman kir got: Wî bibin serşoka mezin û qenc bişon û veşon, û bedlek cilê nû lê bikin, û çi xwarin û vexwarinên xweş hebin deynin ber, û dûre wî bibin odeya razanê bera razê, û hespê wî bibin xanê û lê miqate bin, têr av û êm bikin, têr ceh bikin.
1953. The king (Zelîxa) gave an order said: Take him to the big bathroom and wash and cleanse him well, and put a suit of new clothes on him, and whatever pleasant foods and drinks there are put before him, and then take him to the room of sleeping let him sleep, and take his horse to the inn and be careful of it, do full water and feed, do full barley.

1954. Çend roj derbas bûn, her yek ji her sê rêwîyan ji xwe re dibêje: Ev çi ye û çi şah û ferman e, ma qey ev şah min nas dike wey?
1954. A few days passed, each one of all three travelers says to himself: What is this and what king and order is it, after all does this king really recognize me alas?

1955. Cadûkar bi xwe re dipeyive: Hema bi Xwedê ev şaha han min nas dike û an tiştin ser min bihîstine, ma çima ez xistime zindanê?
1955. The sorcerer speaks with himself: Just by God this very king recognizes me and or has heard things upon me, after all why has he put me in prison?

1956. ma min çi kirîye?
1956. after all what have I done?

1957. ez zilamekî rêwî me, û kesekî ji vî bajarî nas nakim, bi Xwedê ez ditirsim ku belak min hebe, wê ji wî wêneyê devê dergehê sûrê be?
1957. I am a traveler man, and I do not recognize anyone from this city, by God I fear that I have a trouble, will it be from that picture of the mouth of the gate of the wall?

1958. Nêçîrvan: Law, kuro ma kî li vir min nas dike?
1958. Hunter: Boy, boy after all who recognizes me here?

1959. kî zane ez li çi digerim?
1959. who knows what I walk around for (what I am looking for)?

1960. ma qey min çikirbû?
1960. after all really what had I done?

1961. min jî wek xelkê li wêneyê keçikê dinerî, na yabo na, yê min bi xwe min bi kul û keder lê dinerî, heger hicranek min hebe, ji wê ye.
1961. I too like the people was looking at the picture of the girl, no father no, I myself I was looking at it with wound and sorrow, if I have an affliction, it is from that.

1962. Zîrek: Kuro, tu dibê qey ev paşe, ev şah min nas dike law, wiqas qedir dane min, bi Xwedê ev mi nas dike, belkî hinek ji bazirgana, ew ê bi me re kar dikirin li dora şah in, xwe bi min nas kirin nedan.
1962. Zîrek: Boy, you say really this paşa, this king recognizes me boy, they gave this much value to me, by God he recognizes me, perhaps some of the merchants, those who were doing work with us are around the king, they did not give themselves to be recognized by me (did not reveal themselves to me).

1963. Ma ev miqate bûn ji ku tê?
1963. After all this being careful comes from where?

1964. helbet tiştek heye, hinek min nas dikin, de ka bê Xwedê çawa dike, ez ê namakê ji şah re bişînim belkî dilê wî bi min bişewite, min berde, ku ez herim bi oxira xwe de, û ez li dergîsîya xwe Zelîxa bigerim.
1964. of course there is a thing, some recognize me, then let's see well how God does, I will send a letter to the king perhaps his heart burns with me, releases me, so that I go in my journey, and I look for my fiancée Zelîxa.

1965. Dadgeh (1): Serê sibê şah û civata xwe rûniştin, û dadmendê dewletêferman kir û got: herin filanê gunehkar ji odeya wî bînin (nêçîrvan), dergevana çûn û mêrik anîn dadgehê, di rekela gunehkara de.
1965. Court (1): Early in the morning the king and his assembly sat, and the judge of the state ordered and said: go bring so-and-so sinner from his room (the hunter), the gatekeepers went and brought the man to the court, in the cage of the sinners.

1966. Şah: Tu kî ye?
1966. King: Who are you?

1967. û navê te çi ye?
1967. and what is your name?

1968. û karê te çi ye?
1968. and what is your work?

1969. û tu ji kîjan welatî ye?
1969. and you are from which country?

1970. Nêçîrvan: Ez Şerîfo me, û ez nêçîrvanê masîya me, û ez ji filan gundî li hêla jêr.
1970. Hunter: I am Şerîfo, and I am a hunter of fishes (fisherman), and I am from so-and-so village at the lower side.

1971. Şah: Çima te li wêneyê ber dergehê sûrê nerî û te keser veda, qey tu nas dikî?
1971. King: Why did you look at the picture before the gate of the wall and you gave a sigh, really do you recognize it?

1972. Nêçîrvan: Şahê min ev qîzik di tabûtek text de bû, û birîndar bû bi xenceran, kete tora min û min ew derxist û bire malê, û min ew şûşt ji xwînê, û birînên wê derman kirin, û bi şev û bi ro ez lê miqate bûm, piştî rihet bû û spî sax bû, şevekê hespê min û cilê min birin û revîye, kes nizane bê çû bi ku derê de, û hingî dilê min bi ser ve bû, min da dû, heya min wêneyê wê li devê dergehê sûrê dît, min nas kir ku ew keçik e, min got xwezî min bi saxî bidîta.
1972. Hunter: My king this little girl was in a wooden coffin, and was wounded with daggers, fell into my net and I took her out and took her home, and I washed her from blood, and treated her wounds, and by night and by day I was careful of her, after she rested and became completely healthy, one night she took my horse and my clothes and has fled, no one knows well to wherever she went, and then my heart was upon it, I gave behind, until I saw her picture at the mouth of the gate of the wall, I recognized that it is that girl, I said I wish I had seen her alive.

1973. Şah: Tu çi jê dixwaze?
1973. King: What do you want from her?

1974. û çi pêdivîyên te pê hene?
1974. and what needs do you have with her?

1975. Nêçîrvan: Ezbenî, wele dilê min bi ser ve ye, lê ne layîqî min e, ez jê mezintir im lê hema xweşika, heqê textorîya min, û hespê min bigiha min û jar û rezîltîya ev du-sê mehan ez ketimê û bi dû de digerim, û min mal û zarokên xwe birçî hiştine.
1975. Hunter: Sir, by God my heart is upon her, but she is not worthy of me, I am bigger (older) than her but just beauty, the wage of my doctoring, and my horse reach me and the misery and wretchedness of these two-three months I fell into and go around behind, and I have left my wealth and children hungry.

1976. Şah: Ferman da, hespekî ji yê wî çêtir, û cil û bergên nû lê kirin, û têra wî pere û zêr danê û got: de veger malê nav zarokên xwe, Xwedê bi te re be.
1976. King: He gave an order, a horse better than his, and they put new clothes and garments on him, and they gave enough money and gold for him and said: then return home among your children, God be with you.

1977. Dad geh (2): Piştî çend rojên din, civîna dadgehê rûnişt û paşe (sah) hat ser kursîyê xwe rûnişt, ferman kir: Herin ew ê
1977. Court (2): After a few other days, the meeting of the court sat and the paşa (king) came sat on his chair, ordered: Go those who

1978. di zindanê de bînin, çend dergevan û çavdêr rabûn çûn zindanê cadûkar anîn pêşbera dadgehê, û xistin rekela gunehkaran de.
1978. are in the prison bring, a few gatekeepers and watchers got up went to the prison brought the sorcerer before the court, and put him in the cage of the sinners.

1979. Şah: Tu kî yî kuro?
1979. King: Who are you boy?

1980. tu ji ku derê yî?
1980. you are from where?

1981. û tu li çi digerî?
1981. and what do you walk around for (what are you looking for)?

1982. Cadûkar: Ez Silko me, ji bajarê Amedê me, ez li xwedîya wêneyê digerim.
1982. Sorcerer: I am Silko, I am from the city of Amed, I walk around for (I am looking for) the owner of the picture.

1983. Şah: Xwedîya wêneyê çîyê te ye?
1983. King: The owner of the picture is what of yours?

1984. û tu çima bi dû de ye?
1984. and why are you behind her?

1985. Cadûkar: Xwedîya wêneyê, ne tiştekî mine, cilê zilama li xwe kiribû û qesr û qûnax ava dikirin, ji lepta wê, û dengê wê, û çavên wê, min nas kir ku jine, ne mêre.
1985. Sorcerer: The owner of the picture, is not a thing of mine, she had put the clothes of men on herself and was building castles and mansions, from her movement, and her voice, and her eyes, I recognized that she is a woman, she is not a man.

1986. Şah: Ê ma îşê te pê hebû, û te çi jê bû?
1986. King: Well after all did you have a business with her, and what were you from her?

1987. Cadûkar: Ez dilketim kar û îşê wê, û zanebûna wê.
1987. Sorcerer: I fell in love with her work and business, and her knowledge.

1988. Şah: Û karê te çi bû?
1988. King: And what was your work?

1989. te çi kar dikir?
1989. what work were you doing?

1990. Cadûkar: Ez cadûkarim, bi fen û fûta min kir û nekir, min tu çiq tênekir.
1990. Sorcerer: I am a sorcerer, with trickery and deceit I did and did not (tried everything), I did not make any crack in her.

1991. Şah: Tu çi jê dixwazî?
1991. King: What do you want from her?

1992. û çima tu bi dû de yî?
1992. and why are you behind her?

1993. Cadûkar: Piştî min bihîst ku mêrê wê ew tijî xencer kirîye, û xistîye tabûtekê avêtîye çem, min da dû, qene ez bibînim, û derman bikim û ji xwe re bînim.
1993. Sorcerer: After I heard that her husband has filled her with daggers, and has put her in a coffin thrown her into the river, I gave behind, so that I see her, and I treat her and bring her for myself.

1994. Şah: Tê tobe bike, tu dev ji vî karî berdî, û karekî paqij ji xwe re bibînî, û heger tu tobe nekî ji dil û can, ez ê niha te bi eşkence têxim zindanê de, heya tu sax bî li darê dinya yê.
1994. King: You will do repentance, you will let go of this work, and you will see a clean work for yourself, and if you do not do repentance from heart and soul, I will now put you in prison with torture, until you are alive in the tree of the world (in this world).

1995. Cadûkar: Ezbenî, ez di bextê te û Xwedê de me, zarokên min hû rin, tê min bibexşînî, û ez soz û peymanê didim û tobe dikim, li ber destê te û vê civatê, û Xwedê di ser me re ye, me dibîne, min tobe ye, tobe ye, tobe ye.
1995. Sorcerer: Sir, I am in your luck and God's (I implore you and God), my children are small, you will forgive me, and I give promise and covenant and do repentance, before your hand and this assembly, and God is over us, sees us, my repentance is, repentance is, repentance is.

1996. Şah: Dest û lingê wî vekin û çend zêra bidinê, bera here nav zarokên xwe.
1996. King: Open his hands and legs and give a few gold coins to him, let him go among his children.

1997. Dada sêyem: Çend roj qedîyan, dadgeh li dar xistin di dîwana şah de, wezîr û cîger û şêwirmend û dadmend, û kesên zane û xwedî nas.
1997. The third court: A few days finished, they set up the court in the court of the king, viziers and deputies and counselors and judges, and knowing and recognizable persons.

1998. Şah hat li ser kursîyê xwe rûnişt û ferman kir: Herin Zîrek bînin dadgehê, dergevan û çavdêr rabûn çûn bi destê Zîrek girtin û anîn di rekela gunehkara de be rûniştin dan.
1998. King came sat on his chair and ordered: Go bring Zîrek to the court, gatekeepers and watchers got up went caught Zîrek's hand and brought him in the cage of the sinners gave him sitting.

1999. Şah jê pirsî: Tu kî ye?
1999. King asked him: Who are you?

2000. û tu ji ku derê yî?
2000. and you are from where?

2001. û tu li çi digerî?
2001. and what are you walking around for (what are you looking for)?

2002. Zîrek: Ez ji bajarê Amedê me, navê min Zîreke, ez li xwedîya wêneyê ber dergehê sûrê digerim.
2002. Zîrek: I am from the city of Amed, my name is Zîrek, I walk around for (I am looking for) the owner of the picture before the gate of the wall.

2003. Şah: Çima tu lê digerî?
2003. King: Why do you walk around for her?

2004. ma qey çi yê te ye?
2004. after all really she is what of yours?

2005. Zîrek: Xwedîya vî wêneyî dergîsîya min e, û Xwedê ji min re xerakir, ez kur kirim û min bi gotina pîra dêya xwe kir, hingî di serê min de xwend û bêbextî lê kirin, û ez jî ne li mal bûm, salek min qedya bû, min nizanîbû bê çi heye çi tune ye, hema ji kuranî min jinik da ber xencera, û ji tirsa bavê wê min xist tabûtekê (sebetekê) û avêt çem, piştî ez vegerîyam malê, min li qesr û qûnaxa nerî, û li kar û îşê wê nerî û min pirs kir bê çilo bû?
2005. Zîrek: The owner of this picture is my fiancée, and God ruined for me, made me blind and I did by the word of my old mother, then she read into my head and they did treachery upon her, and I too was not at home, one year of mine had finished, I did not know well what there is what there is not, just from blindness I gave the woman before daggers, and from the fear of her father I put her in a coffin (a basket) and threw her into the river, after I returned home, I looked at the castles and mansions, and looked at her work and business and I asked a question let's see how was it?

2006. çawa bû?
2006. how was it?

2007. kê ev kuş û sera ava kirine?
2007. who built these palaces and manors?

2008. min nas kir ku dergîsîya min qîza şahê amedê ye, cilê zilama li xwe dikirin qene kes wê nas neke, û ev qas kar û îş kirin, ez gelekî poşman bûm, û min serê xwe li dîwar xist, min xwe bi girî kuşt, min go tu çare tune ye, û ez ê li vir çi bikim piştî çavên Zelîxe, û jîyana min ji çire ye?
2008. I recognized that my fiancée is the girl of the king of Amed, she was putting the clothes of men on herself so that no one recognizes her, and did this much work and business, I became greatly regretful, and I hit my head on the wall, I killed myself with crying, I said there is no remedy, and what will I do here after the eyes of Zelîxa, and my life is for what?

2009. hema ew qas kuşk û sera, û ew qas malê bazirganîyê di xanê de hişt, û ez bi ser pişta hespê xwe ketim, û çem û çem ez dimeşim, bi şev û bi roj birçî, tazî, min gelek rezîltî dît, hema carekê min da pey kerwanekî û ez di vire derketim, li ber dergehê sûrê ez rûniştim qederkê piştî min av ji denê vexwar, çavên min li wêneyê Zelîxe ketin, hiş û sewdan di serê min de nema, axîn û nalîn bi min ket û barînî ji min hat û ez têrgirîyam, û dîna min dî bi çeplê min girtine û ez anîm dîwana mîr, lê Xwedê ji û paşê we razîbe, miho ya Xwedê bêje, gelekî ji min re baş bûn, bi şûştin û veşûştin, û xwarim û vexwarin, û razan, cihê min gelekî xweş bû.
2009. just I left that many palaces and manors, and that much wealth of commerce in the inn, and I fell upon the back of my horse, and river and river I walk, by night and by day hungry, naked, I saw much wretchedness, just once I gave behind a caravan and I went out here, before the gate of the wall I sat a while after I drank water from the vat, my eyes fell upon the picture of Zelîxa, mind and reason did not remain in my head, groaning and moaning fell into me and pouring came from me and I cried full, and my looking saw (I saw) they caught my arm and brought me to the court of the mîr, but may God be pleased with your paşa, say the "miho" of God (tell the truth of God), they were very good to me, with washing and cleansing, and food and drink, and sleeping, my place was very pleasant.

2010. Lê ez ji we dixwazim hûnê destûra min bidin, rêya min dûr e ez ê herim li dergîsîya xwe bigerim.
2010. But I want from you you will give my permission, my road is far I will go walk around for (look for) my fiancée.

2011. Şah: Têhere ku li dergîsîya xwe bigere, ma saxe, mirîye?
2011. King: You will go to where to look for your fiancée, after all is she alive, has she died?

2012. Zîrek: Ez nizanim, ne saxe û ne mirîye, û ne li ku derê ye.
2012. Zîrek: I do not know, neither is she alive and nor has she died, and nor at where she is.

2013. Lê dilê min ji min re dibêje saxe û heya ez saxbim ez ê lê bigerim.
2013. But my heart says to me she is alive and as long as I am alive I will look for her.

2014. Şah: Tu ji ya min dike, têvegere malê xan û danê te, kuşk û serayê jinkê ji te re ava kirine.
2014. King: You do by mine (if you listen to me), you will return home your inns and stations, the palaces and manors the woman has built for you.

2015. Zîrek: hew hew, ma ez ê çi bikim ji mal û zêra, ez çi bikim ji kuşk û seray, ji qesr û qûnaxa ku xwedîya wa ne tê de be, pepûkê bi zor û zehmetîyê giş ava kirin, û hîn min û wê hevûdu nedîtibû, û me hev xweşik nas nekirbû, di wê şeva bavê wê damin, di wê şevê de min dév jê berda, û ez bi çola ketim, bi yekî bazirgan re ji feqîrtî, û ji ne çarî.
2015. Zîrek: enough enough, after all what will I do from wealth and gold, what will I do from palaces and manors, from castles and mansions when their owner is not in them, the wretch with force and hardship built them all, and still I and she had not seen each other, and we had not recognized each other beautifully, on that night her father gave her to me, in that night I let go of her mouth (let go of her), and I fell to the deserts, with a merchant from poverty, and from having no remedy.

2016. Şah: Gelî civatêev zilam rast dipeyive, û zêdî salekê dûrî malê ma, û ev qas mal û pere û zêr wî şandin ji jinkê re, û jinik jî qîza şahê Amedê ye, li xwe dananî va pera xerc bike û birjîne û biavêje, rabû qesr û qnaxê wek ê bavê xwe çêkirin û avanîyê mezin wek kuşk û seraya dewletê.
2016. King: O people of the assembly this man speaks true, and he remained away from home more than a year, and this much wealth and money and gold he sent for the woman, and the woman too is the girl of the king of Amed, she did not put upon herself (allow herself) to spend this money and spill and throw it away, she got up built castles and mansions like those of her father and big buildings like the palaces and manors of the state.

2017. Lê Xwedê ji gelac û bêbexta re nehêle, nehiştin bi hev şabibin gelî civatê, ev zilam (Zîreke) dergîsîyê min e, û ez Zelîxa me keça paşayê Amedê.
2017. But may God not leave it to the backbiters and treacherous ones, they did not let them be happy together O people of the assembly, this man (Zîrek) is my fiancé, and I am Zelîxa the daughter of the paşa of Amed.

2018. Civat: Humîn û gumîn lê ket, û bû elah elah civatêû her yek dibêje: ev çi çîrok bû law, ev çi serpêhatî bû, ev çi jine gidîyano, ev çend salê wê li hêvîya dergîsîyê xwe ye çi qîza camêraye, û mêrik jî zilamekî bi namûse, û zîreke, evaqas mal daye hev, û şandîye ji jinkê re, bê ku hev xweşik nas bikin, ew yekî parsek û jinik qîza paşê bajêr.
2018. Assembly: Roaring and rumbling fell into it, and it became the "Allah Allah" of the assembly and each one says: what a story this was boy, what an adventure this was, what a woman this is O you folks, for these several years she is in hope of her fiancé what a girl of gentlemen she is, and the man too is a man with honor, and is clever (zîrek), has gathered this much wealth, and has sent it for the woman, without them recognizing each other beautifully, he a beggar and the woman the girl of the paşa of the city.

2019. Zelîxe: Gelî civatêbazê we ne şaşbû ku li ser serê min danî, û va dergîsîyê min hatîye bi dû min de, û şîr helale ji dil û can ez ê şahitîya we bidim we û carek din bazê xwe berdin, û ew kesê me anîn dadgehê: Yê pêşî nêçîrvan bû û textorê min bû, Xwedê ez sax kirim, wî ez sax kirim.
2019. Zelîxa: O people of the assembly your falcon was not wrong when it put (landed) on my head, and here my fiancé has come behind me, and he is with lawful milk (legitimate/pure) from heart and soul I will give your kingship to you and release your falcon once again, and those persons we brought to the court: The first was the hunter and was my doctor, God healed me, he healed me.

2020. Û yê didwa ew cadûkar bû, dixwest fenekê li min bike û gelek xefk û devk vedan, lê
2020. And the second was that sorcerer, he was wanting to do a trick upon me and set many traps and snares, but

2021. tiştek bi dest wî neket, we dît min derfetek dayê qene tobe bike, û ji bo jina wî û zarokên wî min ew bexişand, û vaye niha ez ê xatira ji we bixwazim, ez qîzim û ev xort dergîsîyê min e, bavê min bi helalîya Xwedê ez damê de.
2021. nothing fell to his hand, you saw I gave an opportunity to him so that he does repentance, and for his wife and his children I forgave him, and here now I will ask for sake from you (say goodbye to you), I am a maiden and this youth is my fiancé, my father with the lawfulness of God gave me to him.

2022. Em ê vegerin welatêxwe, cem dê û bavê xwe, û ji nûvre em ê daweta xwe li darxin, û civat bela bû û banggêr careke din bang kir: Hêê, şahê me keçik bû, wê here welatêxwe bi dergîsîyê xwe re, hêê, em bazê şah berdin, bê ka li ser serê kê datîne, piştî nîvro giş derkevin gasîn û kulana.
2022. We will return to our country, to our mother and father, and anew we will set up our wedding, and the assembly dispersed and the crier once again called out: Hey, our king was a girl, she will go to her country with her fiancé, hey, we will release the falcon of kings, let's see well on whose head it puts (lands), after noon all go out to squares and streets.

2023. Zîrek û Zelîxe karê xwe kirin û du hesp ji tewlxana paşê derxistin û dan nav kerwanê bazirganê ji Şam û Helebê tên wê herin Amedê, û qûnax bi qûnax bi kerwan re dimeşin.
2023. Zîrek and Zelîxa did their work and took out two horses from the stable of the paşa and put them into the caravan of the merchants coming from Şam and Heleb they will go to Amed, and stage by stage they walk with the caravan.

2024. ## Li Amedê
2024. ## At Amed

2025. Piştî demekê kerwan û Zîrek û Zelîxe gihan şarê Amedê.
2025. After a time the caravan and Zîrek and Zelîxa reached the city of Amed.

2026. Derbas bûn qesr û qûnaxa, her tişt di cihê xwe de ye, çend kar û cêrî anîn, xan û dan, mal û firax, kursî û mase, tej û ber, giş paqij kirin, yê daweşandin, yê şûştin, her tişt kirin wek zîvê qurs.
2026. They passed to the castles and mansions, everything is in its place, they brought a few workers and maids, inns and stations, goods and dishes, chairs and tables, scraps and rugs, they cleaned all, those they shook out, those they washed, they made everything like pure silver.

2027. Rabûn nanekî giran û mezin çêkirin, çi kesê berpirsîyar û xuyayî ji wezîr û şêwirdarê şah û malbata şah, kesê zanîyar û bazirgan tev oldarê bilind wek qazî û miftî.
2027. They got up made a heavy and big bread (feast), whatever responsible and visible persons from the viziers and counselors of the king and the family of the king, knowing persons and merchants together with high religious figures like qadis and muftis.

2028. tevde ser nan û xwarinê hatin xwestin, xelk jî hatin rûniştin.
2028. all upon the bread and food were wanted (invited), the people too came sat.

2029. Rêza pêşî ji şah û malbata wî re di odeke mezin de û rêza din ji ber pirsîyara û wezîr û cîgira û zanîyar û oldara re, û dîwane ji serokê kerwan û bazirganîya re, û li ser serê wa mamostê wî (başbazirgan) hevbeşê wî û hemû karkerê bi wan re bûn bi kirîn û firotinê.
2029. The first row for the king and his family in a big room and the other row for the responsible ones and viziers and deputies and knowing ones and religious figures, and the court for the heads of the caravans and merchants, and on their heads his master (the chief merchant) his partner and all the workers who were with them with buying and selling.

2030. Û nan û xwarin kişandin ber mêvanan, kişandin û kişandin, li gasîna kuşkê danîn û xelk û gundî û feqîr û belengaz û parsekê nav bajêr giş anîbûn.
2030. And they pulled bread and food before the guests, they pulled and pulled, at the square of the palace they put down and they had brought the people and villagers and poor and wretched and beggars of the city all.

2031. Rêzek radibe û yek rûdinê.
2031. One row gets up and one sits.

2032. Her yek wê têr bixwe û rabe here mala xwe, hino hino şev ket erdê, û xelk giş çûn malên xwe, ji bilî kesê di ode û dîwana de.
2032. Each one will eat full and get up go to his home, little by little night fell to the ground, and the people all went to their homes, except the persons in the rooms and courts.

2033. Ew piştî xwarinê fêkî û vexwarin li ber wan hat danîn, û şah û malîya xwe û zarokên xwe di odeyekê de ne, wek a mala
2033. They after food fruit and drinks were put before them, and the king and his household and his children are in a room, like that of his house

2034. wî ye, ji kursî û maseyan, ji tepsîk û kevçî û şûşa û çi xwarina şah û malbata xwe jê hez dikirin hat ber wan.
2034. it is, from chairs and tables, from trays and spoons and glasses and whatever foods the king and his family were loving came before them.

2035. Şah û jina xwe ji hev re dibêjin, "tu dibêje qey yek ji mala me di vir de ye, yan em li mala xwe ne", man gosretmayî.
2035. The king and his wife say to each other, "you say really one from our house is in here, or we are in our house", they remained bewildered.

2036. Piştî şîvê û fêkî û vexwarinê, şah û malîya xwe destûra çûnê ji Zîrek û Zelîxeyê (bi cilê zilama ye) xwestin.
2036. After dinner and fruit and drinks, the king and his household asked for the permission of going from Zîrek and Zelîxa (she is with the clothes of men).

2037. Gotin: Şahê min ezxulam, hema bîskekê xwe ragirin.
2037. They said: My king your servant, just hold yourselves a moment.

2038. Her du derketin û çûn odeya xwe cilê li xwe ji xwe danîn û cil û bergine nû li xwe kirin, cilê zavatî û bûkanîyê, her duyan bi destê hev girtin û hatin pêşîya şah û malîya wî.
2038. Both went out and went to their room put the clothes on themselves down from themselves and put new clothes and garments on themselves, the clothes of groomhood and bridal state, both caught by the hand of each other and came before the king and his household.

2039. Şah û jina xwe û zarokên xwe man hêbetmayî û ziq li wan nerîn.
2039. The king and his wife and his children remained awe-struck and stared intently at them.

2040. Zelîxe: Yabo, yadê qey we ez ji bîra kirime?
2040. Zelîxa: Father, mother really have you forgotten me?

2041. Ez Zelîxa me, qîza we me û ev jî Zîreke dergîsîyê min e, dema te ez damê de û hîn em qîz û xort in, min şo nekirîye.
2041. I am Zelîxa, I am your girl and this too is Zîrek my fiancé, when you gave me to him and still we are maiden and youth, I have not wedded.

2042. Hevûdu ramîsandin û çîroka xwe bi ta û derzî vekirin.
2042. They kissed each other and opened their story with thread and needle (in detail).

2043. Bang mela û miftî û qazî kirin û ji nûv re mehra wan birîn û serê sibê daweta wan li dar xistin, hefteyekê bi dahol û zirne û govend û dîlan, bi kêf û şahî jiyana xwe derbas kirin.
2043. They called the mullah and mufti and qadi and anew they cut their marriage (performed their marriage) and early in the morning they set up their wedding, for a week with drum and zurna and dance and celebration, with joy and celebration they passed their life.

2044. ## Hesenê Alê û Têlî Eyşê
2044. ## Hesen of Alî and Têlî Eyşê

2045. Hesenê Alê birazîyê Omer Begê û pismamê Têlî Eyşê û Mîr Mamedê kurê Omer Begê bû.
2045. Hesen of Alî was the nephew of Omer Beg and the cousin of Têlî Eyşê and Mîr Mamed the son of Omer Beg.

2046. Omer Begê Walîyê Şamê ye, soz û peyman dabû birayê xwe Alî Begê Bavê Hesen Alê ku keça xwe Têlî Eyşê bidê Hesenê Alê û bi hev re her du dane ber xwendinê.
2046. Omer Beg is the Governor of Şam, he had given promise and covenant to his brother Alî Beg the Father of Hesen of Alî that he will give his daughter Têlî Eyşê to Hesen of Alî and together they gave both to reading (school).

2047. Çend sal derbas bûn her du (qîz û xort) bîrwer bûn gelekî hez ji hevudû dikirin, zarok bûn, bi kêf û şahî bûn, bi şev û bi roj dixwendin û dilîstin, ji hev qut nedibûn gelekî hilfa xwe avêtibûn ser hev.
2047. A few years passed both (maiden and youth) became mindful they were loving each other greatly, they were children, they were with joy and celebration, by night and by day they were reading and playing, they were not cutting off from each other they had greatly thrown their vow upon each other.

2048. Bê hev gepek nan nedixwarin, temenê wa bû deh dozdeh salî Alî Begê Bavê Hesenê Alê nexweş ket û çû ber dilovanîya Xwedê.
2048. Without each other they were not eating a bite of bread, their age became ten twelve years old Alî Beg the Father of Hesen of Alî fell sick and went before the mercy of God.

2049. Pepûkê Hesenê Alê ma sêwî ber destê ap û amojinê, hino hino çavreşî avêtinê, dûrî Têlî Eyşê kirin ji xwendinê dûr kirin, xistin ber kehr û berxika de li çolê zikekî têr û dehê birçî, pêxwas cil û postperitî.
2049. Wretched Hesen of Alî remained an orphan before the hand of his uncle and aunt, little by little they threw black-eyedness (envy) at him, they made him away from Têlî Eyşê they made him away from reading, put him before the kids and lambs in the desert one full stomach and ten hungry, barefoot clothes and skins torn.

2050. Sal qedîyan hezkirina Hesenê Alê û Têlî Eyşê ji bîr nebû û zêdetir bû û navê wan bi ser zimana ket.
2050. Years finished the loving of Hesen of Alî and Têlî Eyşê was not forgotten and became more and their names fell upon the tongues.

2051. Hesenê Alê bûye xortekî bedew û mêrxas, şivanê pezê apê xwe ye, apê zordest û dilkevirî bera Hesenê Alê da ji ber pezê xwe û ew dûrî şarê Şamê kir.
2051. Hesen of Alî has become a handsome and brave youth, he is the shepherd of the sheep of his uncle, the oppressive and stone-hearted uncle gave the direction of Hesen of Alî from before his sheep (dismissed him) and made him away from the city of Şam.

2052. Pepûkê Hesenê Alê tî û tazî û birçî bi çolê ket û berê xwe da Çîyayê Derzîdaxê cihê çete û keleşa û qaşxûnê dewletê.
2052. Wretched Hesen of Alî thirsty and naked and hungry fell to the desert and turned his direction to the Mountain of Derzîdax the place of bandits and robbers and the fugitives of the state.

2053. Hesenê Alê kete çîyê û kete nav çete û pêxwasan de.
2053. Hesen of Alî fell to the mountain and fell among bandits and vagabonds.

2054. Rojek, dido, sisê Hesenê xwende û mêrxas, hêdî hêdî xwe dûrî çete û pêxwasan kir û giha Gênc Xelîl Axa siwarê şînbozê û qafxûnê dewletê û
2054. One day, two, three Hesen the read (educated) and brave, slowly slowly made himself away from bandits and vagabonds and reached Gênc Xelîl Axa the rider of the blue-gray and the fugitive of the state and

2055. bû destbirakê Gênc Xelîl Axa.
2055. became the blood brother of Gênc Xelîl Axa.

2056. Bi hev re diçin nêçîrê.
2056. Together they go to hunting.

2057. Hesenê Alê xortekî zana û mêrxas e, bû xwedîyê hespa bayînî û şûr û mertale Misrê û siwarekî bi nav û deng e, piştî cihê xwe girt û bû siwarekî ku rêwî û bazirgan dûrî wî herin, kela evînîyê ew hilanî û axîn û fixan jê hat hingî bêrîya Têlî Eyşê kiribû.
2057. Hesen of Alî is a knowing and brave youth, he became the owner of the wind-like horse and the sword and shield of Egypt and he is a rider with name and fame, after he took his place and became a rider that travelers and merchants go far from him, the boiling of love lifted him and groaning and wailing came from him then he had missed Têlî Eyşê.

2058. Rabû êvarekê destûr ji destbirakê xwe Gênc Xelîl Axa xwest û di şevreşê de berê xwe da Şamê piştî nîvê şevê hespê xwe xiste tewilexaneyê û berê xwe da holîya dotmama xwe Têlî Eyşê.
2058. He got up one evening wanted permission from his blood brother Gênc Xelîl Axa and in the pitch-black night turned his direction to Şam after midnight put his horse in the stable and turned his direction to the hut of his cousin Têlî Eyşê.

2059. Tîlê Eyşê ji kêfa re bask tune bûn ku bifirîya rabû destek cilê bûkanîyê li xwe kirin û bi xeml û xêz li tenist pismamê xwe Hesenê Alê rûnişt û ketin nav henek û laqirdîyan de, û jîyana zarokîtîya xwe anîn bîra xwe heya destê sibê.
2059. Têlî Eyşê for joy wings were not that she fly (she lacked wings to fly from joy) got up put a suit of clothes of bridal state on herself and with adornment and drawing sat next to her cousin Hesen of Alî and they fell into jokes and jests, and brought the life of their childhood to their memory until early morning.

2060. Hesenê Alê rabû xatir ji dotmama xwe xwest û soz dayê ku her êvara înê di serê heyvê de wê bê serdana wê, û ji holîyê derket çû li hespê xwe siwar bû û berê xwe da Çîyayê Derzîdaxê cem destbirakê xwe Gênc Xelîl Axa.
2060. Hesen of Alî got up wanted sake from his cousin (said goodbye) and gave promise to her that every Friday evening at the head of the moon he will come to her visiting, and went out from the hut went mounted on his horse and turned his direction to the Mountain of Derzîdax to his blood brother Gênc Xelîl Axa.

2061. Dem û wext derbas bûn, her ji çendakî di êvarê îna de li hespê bayînî siwar dibe û berê xwe dide Şamê serdana dotmama xwe Têlî Eyşê.
2061. Times and times passed, every once in a while on Friday evening he mounts on the wind-like horse and gives his direction to Şam visiting his cousin Têlî Eyşê.

2062. Dem bihar e, Şamê xemilîye bi gul û çîçeka, çîveçîve çûka li ser dara, hêlînên xwe girê didin û qirişika dicivînin û dihûnin li ser hev datînin hêlînê xweşik û nermik ava dikin û hêka dikin qene çêlîka derxin.
2062. The time is spring, Şam is adorned with roses and flowers, the tweeting of birds on the trees, they tie their nests and gather twigs and weave them put them on each other build beautiful and soft nests and do eggs so that they take out chicks.

2063. Bedirxan Begê serokê başbazirganê dewletê her sal di vî çaxî de kar û barê xwe dike li gund û bajaran digere, distîne bêş û baca dewletê.
2063. Bedirxan Beg the head of the chief merchants of the state every year in this time does his work and affairs walks around the villages and cities, takes the tribute and taxes of the state.

2064. Bedirxan Begê û çend siwar pê re li pêşîya bazirgan dikudînin.
2064. Bedirxan Beg and a few riders with him before the merchants gallop.

2065. Nêzîkayî li Şamê kirin zilamekî bi siwarî şand Şamê cem Omer Begê qene amade bike bêşa dewletê ji beg û axan re, û bazirganê Şamê Omer Begê kurê xwe Mîr Mamed li hespê siwar kir û şand pêşîya Bedirxanî û jê xwest bibe mêvanê Omer Begê Walîyê Şamê û got: "Mamo silavê bavê min Omer Begê li te hene û dixwaze tu bibe mêvanê dîwan û keleha Şamê, mêvanê Omer Begê".
2065. They did closeness to Şam sent a man mounted to Şam to Omer Beg so that he prepares the tribute of the state for the begs and agha, and the merchant of Şam Omer Beg mounted his son Mîr Mamed on a horse and sent him before Bedirxan and wanted from him to become the guest of Omer Beg the Governor of Şam and said: "Uncle the greetings of my father Omer Beg are upon you and he wants you to become the guest of the court and castle of Şam, the guest of Omer Beg".

2066. Bedirxan Begê: Kurê min law, Mamed Begê, ne li ser bextê min be li ser bextê gotîya be, dibêjin, pismamê te Hesenê Alê, qaşxûnê dewletê bûye çete ketîye Çîyayê Derzîdaxê, her êvara
2066. Bedirxan Beg: My son boy, Mamed Beg, let it not be upon my luck let it be upon the luck of the sayers, they say, your cousin Hesen of Alî, the fugitive of the state has become a bandit fallen to the Mountain of Derzîdax, every evening

2067. îna tê Şamê dibe mênavanê dotmama xwe Têlî Eyşê, ji nîvê şevê pê ve heya destê sibê, wê malê dewletê batmîş bike, fermana serê min e.
2067. of Friday comes to Şam becomes the guest of his cousin Têlî Eyşê, from midnight onwards until early morning, he will sink (plunder) the wealth of the state, it is the order of my head (it will cost my head).

2068. De here kurê min bêje bavê xwe ez nikarim bêm navenda Şamê, keleh û dîwana Omer Begê.
2068. Then go my son say to your father I cannot come to the center of Şam, the castle and court of Omer Beg.

2069. Mamed Begê vegerîya cem bavê xwe û jê re ta bi derzîyê ve vekir ji gotinên Bedirxan Begê.
2069. Mamed Beg returned to his father and for him opened with thread and needle from the words of Bedirxan Beg (told him in detail).

2070. Omer Begê: Kurê min, law Mamedo, Bedirxan Begê serokê başbazirganê dewletê ye, ji bavê te re şerm e ku bazirgan û başbazirganê dewletê ji dervî Şamê razên ji tirsa diz û keleşa.
2070. Omer Beg: My son, boy Mamedo, Bedirxan Beg is the head of the chief merchants of the state, for your father it is a shame that the merchants and chief merchants of the state sleep outside of Şam from the fear of thieves and robbers.

2071. De here jê re bêje, silavê bavê min Omer Begê li te hene û dibêje, bera dilê te tesel be ku qantireke te here, ez ê du qantiran têxim şûnê de.
2071. Then go say to him, the greetings of my father Omer Beg are upon you and he says, let your heart be comforted if a mule of yours goes, I will put two mules in its place.

2072. Bedirxan Begê: Kurê min, law Mamedo, ez nikarim malê dewletê ye, ez nikarim biparêzim di hundirê Şamê de, diz û çete wê malê me talan bikin.
2072. Bedirxan Beg: My son, boy Mamedo, I cannot it is the wealth of the state, I cannot protect it inside Şam, thieves and bandits will plunder our wealth.

2073. Kurê min Mamedo dibêjin, pismamê te Hesenê Alê her şevê êvara îna tê Şamê, mêvanê Têlî Eyşê, dibêjin, çetakî mêrxas e, mêrekî di ser xwe re ye, çavên wî ji tiştekî naşkê û natirse ji dewletê.
2073. My son Mamedo they say, your cousin Hesen of Alî every night of Friday evening comes to Şam, guest of Têlî Eyşê, they say, he is a brave bandit, he is a man over himself (outstanding), his eyes do not break from anything (he fears nothing) and he does not fear from the state.

2074. Ez nikarim xwe têxim tor û bela wî de, malê dewletê ye law, ez ê xwe bavêjim qûntara çîyê û singê çadira bera erdê bidim û barê qantira deynim di orta çadir û pêwanandara de, qene ez karibim biparêzim malê dewletê.
2074. I cannot put myself in his net and trouble, it is the wealth of the state boy, I will throw myself to the skirt of the mountain and give the stakes of the tents to the ground and put the loads of the mules down in the middle of the tents and watchmen, so that I am able to protect the wealth of the state.

2075. Kurê min Mamedo, de here bêje bavê xwe Omer Begê bê silavê apê min Bedirxan Begê li te hene û nikare vî barê giran têxe histê te.
2075. My son Mamedo, then go say to your father Omer Beg well the greetings of my uncle Bedirxan Beg are upon you and he cannot put this heavy load on your neck.

2076. Mîr Mamed vegerîya cem bavê xwe û jê re bersiva Bedirxan Begê.
2076. Mîr Mamed returned to his father and for him the answer of Bedirxan Beg (relayed the answer).

2077. Omer Begê hêrs bû, û çav di serî de sor bûn û gelekî li ber xwe diket.
2077. Omer Beg became angry, and the eyes in his head became red and he was greatly falling before himself (was very upset).

2078. Omer Begê bang kir kurê xwe û got: "Mamedo kurê min law, de here xwe berde kuk meydanê Şamê, li hespê qemer siwar be û xwe berde pêşîya Bedirxan Begê, başbazirganê dewletê û jê re bibêje, silavê bavê min Omer Begê gelek li te hene û soz û peyman bide li ber Xwedê, heger tiştek ji malê te çû bi destê diz û çetê dora Çîyayê Derzîdaxê bi destê Hesenê
2078. Omer Beg called his son and said: "Mamedo my son boy, then go throw yourself exactly to the square of Şam, mount on the roan horse and throw yourself before Bedirxan Beg, the chief merchant of the state and say to him, the greetings of my father Omer Beg are greatly upon you and give promise and covenant before God, if a thing from your wealth went by the hand of the thieves and bandits around the Mountain of Derzîdax by the hand of Hesen

2079. Alê, ez ê bi dest Têlî Eyşê bigirim û lê mehir bikim û jê re têxim mihafê û siwar kim ser pişta devê".
2079. of Alî, I will catch Têlî Eyşê by the hand and marry her to him and for him put her in a litter and mount her on the back of the camel".

2080. Bedirxan Begê kenîya û kêfa wî gelekî hat, dema Mîr Mamed soz û peymana bavê xwe Omer Begê jê re got û nexasim navê Têlî Eyşê li ber guha ket.
2080. Bedirxan Beg laughed and his joy greatly came (he was very pleased), when Mîr Mamed said the promise and covenant of his father Omer Beg to him and especially the name of Têlî Eyşê fell before the ears.

2081. Hema ferman da bazirgana û got: "Hemû berê xwe bidin kuk meydana Şamê, îşev em ê mêvanê Omer Begê bin, û her yek barê xwe li meydana xanê deynin û qantirê xwe têxin xanê de û her yek herin ji xwe re razên, şîyarî û çavdêrî ma li ser xaneyê li cem Omer Begê".
2081. Just he gave an order to the merchants and said: "All give your direction to exactly the square of Şam, tonight we will be the guest of Omer Beg, and let each one put his load down at the square of the inn and put his mules into the inn and each one go sleep for himself, waking and watching remained upon the inn at the side of Omer Beg".

2082. Bazirganî û karmend bi kêf û lez xwe berdan cê şûştinê (avgermê) xwe şûştin û veşûştin û şîva xwe xwarim û ketin xewa şêrîn de.
2082. The merchants and workers with joy and haste threw themselves to the place of washing (bathhouse) washed and cleansed themselves and ate their dinner and fell into sweet sleep.

2083. Ji nîvê şevê pê ve, Hesenê Alê kete nava bajarê Şamê li hespê xwe siwar e, bi lez û bez e wekîcacoka payîzî ye.
2083. From midnight onwards, Hesen of Alî fell into the middle of the city of Şam he is mounted on his horse, with haste and running he is like the autumn whirlwind.

2084. Li tewilxaneyê peya bû ku hespê xwe girê de û berê xwe bide dotmamê, di orta hewşa xanê de dît heydê bar û têrê başbazirganê salê ye, hema li barê pêşî daqûl hat vekir devê xaş û têrê qantira jê derxist hevirmêş û qeytanê Hemedanê û şimkê Mêrdînê û rahişte tûrkê sêvê xelatê dîyarî bire ji dotmama xwe re Têlî Eyşê li holîya jorî, û derbasî odeya dotmamê bû li holîyê danî ber hevirmêş û qeytanê Hemedanê û şimkê Mêrdînê, û ketin kêf û henek û laqirdîyan heya berê sibê.
2084. At the stable he dismounted so that he tie his horse and give his direction to his cousin, in the middle of the courtyard of the inn he saw indeed it is the load and sack of the chief merchant of the year, just he came stooped at the first load opened the mouth of the bags and sacks of the mules took out of it the silk and braid of Hemedan and the slippers of Mêrdîn and grabbed the bag of apples the present gift he took for his cousin Têlî Eyşê at the upper hut, and passed to the room of his cousin at the hut put the silk and braid of Hemedan and slippers of Mêrdîn before her, and they fell into joy and jokes and jests until early morning.

2085. Berî roj hilat, Hesenê Alê rabû û xatir ji dotmama xwe xwest û ji holîyê daket çû xaneyê li hespê xwe siwar bû û berê xwe da Çîyayê Derzîdaxê cihê qajxûn û firarê dewletê.
2085. Before the sun rose, Hesen of Alî got up and asked for sake (said goodbye) from his cousin and went down from the hut went to the inn mounted on his horse and gave his direction to the Mountain of Derzîdax the place of fugitives and escapees of the state.

2086. Hesenê Alê li hespê siwar e û paşpanî lê dan, hespê rehwan wek rewrewkê car û newal qulaptin, wek îcacokê bi kaşa ve hildikişe û dema ji serê kêş tê xwarê weke şîpa lehîyê ye.
2086. Hesen of Alî is mounted on the horse and gave back-heels (spurred) it, the pacing horse overturned (traversed) the tracks and valleys like a mirage, like a whirlwind it climbs up by the inclines and when it comes down from the head of the incline it is like the torrent of a flood.

2087. Hesenê Alê gihaşt cih û warê xwe li Çîyayê Derzîdaxê nav dost û hevalên xwe û dest bi karê nêçîr û çeteyê kir hayê wî ji bayê felekê tune ye, bê bi şûn wî de çi çêdibe li Şamê, û çi bi serê dotmama wî tê.
2087. Hesen of Alî reached his place and camp at the Mountain of Derzîdax among his friends and companions and started the work of hunting and banditry he has no awareness of the wind of fate, let's see well what happens behind him in Şam, and what comes upon the head of his cousin.

2088. Serê sibê karmendê bazirganê Bedirxan ji xew rabûn li xaneyê û hatin ku barê xwe saxlî bikin, dîtin bê heydê barê sê
2088. Early in the morning the workers of the merchant Bedirxan got up from sleep at the inn and came so that they make their load secure (check their load), they saw well indeed the load of three

2089. qantira vebûye û jê hatîye dizîn û hin ji hevirmêş û qeytanê Hemedanê û ji şimkên Mêrdînê hatîye derxistin û dizîn.
2089. mules has opened and has been stolen from it and some from the silk and braid of Hemedan and from the slippers of Mêrdîn has been taken out and stolen.

2090. Hema karmendan berê xwe dan dîwana Omer Begê cihê razana Bedirxan Begê.
2090. Just the workers gave their direction to the court of Omer Beg the place of sleeping of Bedirxan Beg.

2091. Bedirxan Begê ji xew rabû, "çi heye?
2091. Bedirxan Beg got up from sleep, "what is there?

2092. Çi çêbûye?
2092. What has happened?

2093. Çima karmendê wî hatine dîwanê?”
2093. Why have his workers come to the court?”

2094. Ji wan pirsî, "ha lawo çi çêbûye?
2094. He asked them, "ha boy what has happened?

2095. Xwedê xêr ke!"
2095. May God make good!"

2096. Karmend: Begê me, wele malê me hatîye dizîn, barê sê qantira vebûye.
2096. Workers: Our beg, by God our wealth has been stolen, the load of three mules has opened.

2097. Bedirxan Begê: Wê kuro law, qey kes şîyar tune bû, mane dergevanê Omer Begê şîyarî û dergevanî li xanê dikirin, çavdêrê barê kerwan bûn.
2097. Bedirxan Beg: Woe boy boy, really was no one awake, after all the gatekeepers of Omer Beg were doing waking and gatekeeping at the inn, they were the watchers of the load of the caravan.

2098. Karmend: Begê min, te ji me re got herin xwe bison û razên heya sibê, îşev nobetdarîya mal û bara di bin çavdêrîya dergevanê xanê de ye.
2098. Workers: My beg, you said to us go wash yourselves and sleep until morning, tonight the guarding of wealth and loads is under the watching of the gatekeepers of the inn.

2099. Bedirxan Begê dibin simbêla re dikene û di dilê xwe de dibêje, "ji min re lê ket û Xwedê li hev anî, ez ê Têlî Eyşê ji Omer Begê bistînim û li hafê siwar kim û ji rih û canê xwe re bibim bi bûkanî û jinîtî".
2099. Bedirxan Beg laughs under his mustache and says in his heart, "it fell for me and God brought it together, I will take Têlî Eyşê from Omer Beg and mount her in the litter and take her for my soul and spirit in bridal state and womanhood".

2100. Bedirxan Begê bi kêf û şahî şande pey Omer Begê, ka were xaneyê û binere bi çavên xwe, bê çawa li barê sê qantiran hatîye vekirin û jê hatîye dizîn.
2100. Bedirxan Beg with joy and celebration sent after Omer Beg, well come to the inn and look with your eyes, let's see how the load of three mules has been opened and has been stolen from it.

2101. Omer Begê bi dilekî kul û bi şerm û fedî û gelekî li ber xwe diket, û bi çavên xwe dît bê çawa xaş û têrê qantiran vekirî ne û mal jê çûye.
2101. Omer Beg with a wounded heart and with shame and embarrassment and was falling greatly before himself (was very upset), and with his eyes saw well how the bags and sacks of the mules are open and the wealth has gone from it.

2102. Vegerîya malê, ser di ber de, dipojine, ka wê çilo û çawa bike û soz û peyman daye ku tiştek here bi destê çetê dora Çîyayê Derzîdaxê bi destê birazîyê wî Hesenê Alê wê Têlî Eyşê giraw û carî bide Bedirxan Beg, û lê mehir bike Têlî Eyşê.
2102. He returned home, head down, ponders, well how and how will he do and he has given promise and covenant that if a thing goes by the hand of the bandits around the Mountain of Derzîdax by the hand of his nephew Hesen of Alî he will give Têlî Eyşê as pawn and maid to Bedirxan Beg, and will marry Têlî Eyşê to him.

2103. Dinya niha li serî bûye tara bêjingê, nema zane wê çawa bike, wê çilo xwe ji vê wertê xelas bike.
2103. The world now has become the mesh of a sieve upon his head, he no longer knows how he will do, how he will save himself from this situation.

2104. Rabû şande pey wezîr û qazîyên wîlayetê û hal û hewalê xwe ji wan re ji pêşî heya dawî got, ta bi derzîyê ve vekir.
2104. He got up sent after the viziers and qadis of the province and said his condition and situation to them from first to last, opened it with thread and needle (in detail).

2105. Her sê li hev rûniştin û bi hev re şêwirîn ku wê çawa çareyekê jê re bibînin, gotin ku çawa em ê nas bikin bê Hesenê Alê hatîye xaneyê û malê wan ji dotmama xwe Têlî Eyşê re birîye.
2105. All three sat together and consulted with each other that how they will see a remedy for it, they said well how will we recognize well if Hesen of Alî has come to the inn and has taken their wealth for his cousin Têlî Eyşê.

2106.
